CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE informix.sp_updatelatestorderstatus(i_mtt_id INT)

    DEFINE row_no INT;
    DEFINE status_found INT;
    DEFINE latest_status NVARCHAR(10);
    DEFINE o_result INT;

    -- Check if mtt exists
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO row_no
    FROM rms_mtt_pg
    WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

    IF row_no > 0 THEN

        -- Check if there is a payment record with pg_txn_status = 0 for the mtt_id
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO status_found
        FROM rms_mtt_pg
        WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id AND pg_txn_status = 0;

        IF status_found > 0 THEN
            -- If a record with pg_txn_status = 0 is found, return 0
            Let o_result = 0;
        ELSE
            -- If no record with pg_txn_status = 0 is found, find the latest pg_txn_status
            foreach c_something for

                SELECT FIRST 1 pg_txn_status 
                INTO o_result
                FROM rms_mtt_pg
                WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id
                ORDER BY dt_created DESC
            end foreach;
            
        END IF;

        -- Lookup proper name for order status
        CASE o_result
            WHEN 0 THEN let latest_status = 'P'; -- "Paid"
            WHEN 1 THEN let latest_status = 'F'; -- "Failed";
            WHEN 2 THEN let latest_status = 'PP'; -- "Pending Payment"
            ELSE let latest_status = 'PP';
        END CASE;

        -- Update mtt's order status
        UPDATE rms_mtt
        SET order_status = latest_status
        WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

    END IF;

END PROCEDURE;
GO

create or replace procedure sp_checkdocexist(i_file_nm VARCHAR(255))
returning int as o_doc_exist;

    -- Declare a variable to store the count of records with the given document name
    DEFINE o_doc_exist INT;

    -- Check if the document name exists in the fms_doc table
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO o_doc_exist
    FROM rms_fms_doc
    WHERE file_nm = i_file_nm;

    -- Set the output parameter based on the count
    return o_doc_exist;
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_checkfeetaxbyid(i_fee_grp_id int, i_tax_cd_id int)
returning int as result;

define o_result int;

select case
        when exists( select 1 
                     from rms_mft
                     where (i_fee_grp_id IS NULL OR fee_grp_id = i_fee_grp_id)
                     and (i_tax_cd_id is null or tax_cd_id = i_tax_cd_id)
                     and status NOT IN ('RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD')
                    )
        then 1
        when exists( select 1
                     from rms_mft_wf
                     where (i_fee_grp_id IS NULL OR fee_grp_id = i_fee_grp_id)
                     and (i_tax_cd_id is null or tax_cd_id = i_tax_cd_id)
                     and status NOT IN ('RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD')
                   )
        then 1
        else 0
end into o_result;

return o_result;
            
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_checkfmsbyid(i_fms_id int)
returning int as result;

define o_result int;
define total_mft_items int;

-- Get the total items in the mft table
let total_mft_items = (select count(*) from rms_mft);
select case
        when exists( select 1
                     from rms_fms
                     where fms_id = i_fms_id
                       and (
                           select count(case when t2.found = 'F' and t2.status = 'A' then 1 else null end)
                             from rms_fms_ledger t2
                            where t2.fms_id = i_fms_id
                       ) >= total_mft_items
                    )
        then 1
        else 0
        end into o_result;

return o_result;
            
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_checkLatestOrderStatus(i_orn_no NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNING NVARCHAR(10) AS status;--,int as withinMin;

DEFINE o_paymentStatus NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_mtt_id int;
DEFINE rowCount int;
DEFINE o_withinMin int;
DEFINE latestDt DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
--DEFINE time_difference INTERVAL MINUTE TO SECOND;

select COUNT(*)
into rowCount
FROM rms_mtt
WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

if rowCount<1 then
	let o_paymentStatus='';
	let o_withinMin=0; --false
else
	select mtt_id
	into o_mtt_id
	from informix.rms_mtt
	WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

	-- update latest order status from payment table
	call sp_updateLatestOrderStatus(o_mtt_id);
	
	SELECT order_status||'_false'
	INTO o_paymentStatus
	FROM rms_mtt
	WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

	select max(dt_created)
	into latestDt
	from rms_mtt_pg
	where mtt_id = o_mtt_id;
	--order by dt_created desc;
	
	-- get param
	-- Calculate the time difference between current time and dt_created
    --LET time_difference = current YEAR TO FRACTION(5) - latestDt;
   
   	-- Check if the time difference is less than 5 minutes
    --IF time_difference <= INTERVAL(5) MINUTE THEN
        --LET o_withinMin = 1; --true
    --ELSE
        LET o_withinMin = 0; --false
    --END IF
	
END if
		
	RETURN o_paymentStatus;--,o_withinMin;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_checkLatestOrderStatus_v2(i_orn_no NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNING NVARCHAR(10) AS status;
DEFINE o_paymentStatus NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_mtt_id INT;
DEFINE rowCount INT;
DEFINE o_withinMin NVARCHAR(5);
DEFINE latest_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE time_diff INT;
DEFINE time_check int;

if (i_orn_no is null or i_orn_no = '') then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_orn_no is null or empty";
end if

LET  i_orn_no = UPPER(i_orn_no);

SELECT COUNT(*)
INTO rowCount
FROM rms_mtt
WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

IF rowCount < 1 THEN
	LET o_paymentStatus = '';
	LET o_withinMin = 0 ; --false
ELSE
	SELECT mtt_id
	INTO o_mtt_id
	FROM informix.rms_mtt
	WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

	-- update latest order status from payment table
	call sp_updateLatestOrderStatus(o_mtt_id);

	SELECT order_status
	INTO o_paymentStatus
	FROM rms_mtt
	WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no;

    SELECT config_value
    into time_check
    FROM rms_config
    where config_cd = 'PIP_BlockPayOnline_In_Minute';

    let time_check = time_check*60;
 
    SELECT 
      CASE 
        WHEN (current - (SELECT MAX(dt_created) FROM rms_mtt_pg WHERE mtt_id = o_mtt_id)) <= time_check UNITS SECOND THEN 'TRUE'
        ELSE 'FALSE'
      END 
    INTO o_withinMin
    FROM sysmaster:sysdual;


END IF
 
LET o_paymentStatus = o_paymentStatus || '_' || o_withinMin;
 
-- o_paymentstatus_true
RETURN o_paymentStatus;
END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_checkpymtrcpt(i_orn_no NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNS INT as row_cnt;

DEFINE o_row_cnt INT;

SELECT COUNT(*) as result
INTO o_row_cnt
FROM rms_mtt_rcpt t1
INNER JOIN rms_mtt t2 ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
WHERE t2.orn_no = i_orn_no;

RETURN o_row_cnt;

END PROCEDURE
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_checkuserperm(
    i_username NVARCHAR(25),
    i_perm_cd_list VARCHAR(255)
) 
RETURNING LVARCHAR(500) AS o_has_access;

    DEFINE o_has_access LVARCHAR(500);
    DEFINE t_user_role_id INT;

    SELECT sp_group_concat(t4.perm_cd) into o_has_access
    FROM rms_user_role t5
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user t1 ON t1.ssm4uuserrefno = t5.ssm4uuserrefno
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_role t2 ON t5.role_id = t2.role_id
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_role_perm t3 ON t3.role_id = t2.role_id
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_perm t4 ON t3.perm_id = t4.perm_id
    WHERE i_username = t5.ssm4uuserrefno
    AND t4.perm_cd IN (SELECT * FROM TABLE (regex_split(i_perm_cd_list, ','))) AND is_allow = 1;

    RETURN o_has_access;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_delfeegroup (i_fee_grp_nm_en NVARCHAR(50), i_fee_grp_nm_bm NVARCHAR(50), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),i_status NVARCHAR(10))
	RETURNING INT as row_count;

	DEFINE o_row_count INT;

	UPDATE rms_fee_group
	SET status = i_status,
	dt_modified = current,
	modified_by = i_modified_by
	WHERE (i_fee_grp_nm_en IS NULL OR fee_grp_nm_en = i_fee_grp_nm_en)
	AND (i_fee_grp_nm_bm IS NULL OR fee_grp_nm_bm = i_fee_grp_nm_bm);

	LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_delfms(i_fms_cd NVARCHAR(50))
RETURNING INT AS row_count;

DEFINE o_row_count INT;

DELETE FROM rms_fms
WHERE fms_id = (SELECT MAX(fms_id) FROM rms_fms WHERE fms_cd = i_fms_cd);

LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_delmtt(i_mtt_id int8)
returns int8 as row_cnt;

define o_row_cnt INT8;

/* Delete from rms_mtt*/
delete from rms_mtt
where mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

/* Delete from rms_mtt_item*/
delete from rms_mtt_item
where mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

/* Delete from rms_mtt_pg*/
delete from rms_mtt_pg
where mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_delpgtxn(i_rc_pgtxn_id int8)
returning int8 as result;
 
define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
 
on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
 
-- Set a default value
LET o_result = '0';
 
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;
 
-- check exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pgtxn
where rc_pgtxn_id = i_rc_pgtxn_id;
 
if o_exist > 0 then
 
    -- delete record
    delete from rms_rc_pgtxn
    where rc_pgtxn_id = i_rc_pgtxn_id;
 
    -- get deleted id
    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');
 
end if;
 
commit work;
 
if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;
 
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_delroleperm (i_role_id integer)

returning int as row_count;

define o_row_count int;

delete from rms_role_perm where role_id = i_role_id;

let o_row_count = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

return o_row_count;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_deltaxcode (i_tax_cd NVARCHAR(10), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10))
	RETURNING INT as row_count;

	DEFINE o_row_count INT;

	UPDATE rms_tax_code
	SET status = i_status,
	dt_modified = current,
	modified_by = i_modified_by
	WHERE tax_cd = i_tax_cd;

	LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace function sp_gc_comb(partial1 LVARCHAR, partial2 LVARCHAR)
    RETURNING LVARCHAR;
    IF partial1 IS NULL OR partial1 = '' THEN
        RETURN partial2;
    ELIF partial2 IS NULL OR partial2 = '' THEN
        RETURN partial1;
    ELSE
        RETURN partial1 || ',' || partial2;
    END IF;
END FUNCTION;
GO
create or replace function sp_gc_fini(final LVARCHAR) RETURNING LVARCHAR;
    RETURN final;
END FUNCTION;
GO
create or replace function sp_gc_init(dummy VARCHAR(255)) RETURNING LVARCHAR;
    RETURN '';
END FUNCTION;
GO
create or replace function sp_gc_iter(result LVARCHAR, value VARCHAR(255))
    RETURNING LVARCHAR;
    IF result = '' THEN
        RETURN TRIM(value);
    ELSE
        RETURN result || ', ' || TRIM(value);
    END IF;
END FUNCTION;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_generateAgingReport(asOfDate nvarchar(10), rcptNo nvarchar(20), pgTxnId nvarchar(30), stmtNo nvarchar(25),
		matchRec nvarchar(10), pgDtStmtFr date, pgDtStmtTo date, showDupTrans boolean)
	returning datetime year to fraction(5), nvarchar(255), nvarchar(255), nvarchar(255), decimal(16,2),
			datetime year to fraction(5), nvarchar(255), nvarchar(255), nvarchar(255), decimal(16,2),
			integer;
		 
			DEFINE o_dn_dt datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_dn_txn_id nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_dn_rms_bn nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_dn_fms_ref nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_dn_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_cn_dt datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_cn_txn_id nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_cn_rms_bn nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_cn_fms_ref nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_cn_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_status integer;
			
			define o_statement lvarchar(2000);
			let o_statement = "select drb.dt_created as dn_dt, pg.pg_txn_id as dn_txn_id, drh.rms_batch_no as dn_rms_bn, drh.fms_ref_no as dn_fms_ref, drh.amt as dn_amt, crb.dt_created as cn_dt, case when (crb.mtt_pg_id is null or crb.mtt_pg_id = '') then null else pg.pg_txn_id end as cn_txn_id, case when (crb.mtt_pg_id is null or crb.mtt_pg_id = '') then null else crh.rms_batch_no end as cn_rms_bn, case when (crb.mtt_pg_id is null or crb.mtt_pg_id = '') then null else crh.fms_ref_no end as cn_fms_ref, case when (crb.mtt_pg_id is null or crb.mtt_pg_id = '') then null else crh.amt end as cn_amt, case when (crb.mtt_pg_id is null or crb.mtt_pg_id = '') then date('" || asOfDate || "') - cast(drb.dt_created as date) else cast(crb.dt_created as date) - cast(drb.dt_created as date) end as status from rms_fms_drmemo_b drb left join rms_fms_crmemo_b crb on crb.mtt_pg_id = drb.mtt_pg_id left join rms_mtt_pg pg on drb.mtt_pg_id = pg.mtt_pg_id left join rms_fms_drmemo_h drh on drb.drmemo_hid = drh.drmemo_hid left join rms_fms_crmemo_h crh on crb.crmemo_hid = crh.crmemo_hid left join rms_mtt_rcpt rcpt on drb.mtt_pg_id = rcpt.mtt_pg_id left join rms_rc_pgmtt rcpgmtt on drb.mtt_pg_id = rcpgmtt.mtt_pg_id left join rms_rc_pg rcpg on rcpgmtt.rc_pg_id = rcpg.rc_pg_id  where drb.dt_created <= date('" || asOfDate || "') and rcpg.dt_settlement <= date('" || asOfDate || "')";
			if (rcptNo is not null and rcptNo != '') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and rcpt.rcpt_no like '%" || rcptNo || "'";
			end if
			if (pgTxnId is not null and pgTxnId != '') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and pg.pg_txn_id like '%" || pgTxnId || "'";
			end if
			if (stmtNo is not null and stmtNo != '') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and rcpg.stmt_no like '%" || stmtNo || "'";
			end if
			if (pgDtStmtFr is not null and pgDtStmtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and cast(rcpg.dt_settlement as date) >= " || pgDtStmtFr || " and cast(rcpg.dt_settlement as date) <= " || pgDtStmtTo;
			end if
			if lower(matchRec) = 'matched' then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and crb.dt_created is not null";
			elif lower(matchRec) = 'unmatched' then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and crb.dt_created is null";
			end if
			if (showDupTrans = 't') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and (rcpt.rcpt_no is null or rcpt.rcpt_no = '')";
			end if
			let o_statement = o_statement || ";";
			
			prepare s from o_statement;
			declare c cursor for s;
			open c;
			while(1 = 1)
				fetch c into o_dn_dt, o_dn_txn_id, o_dn_rms_bn, o_dn_fms_ref, o_dn_amt, o_cn_dt, o_cn_txn_id, o_cn_rms_bn, o_cn_fms_ref, o_cn_amt, o_status;
				IF (SQLCODE != 100) THEN
			    	RETURN o_dn_dt, o_dn_txn_id, o_dn_rms_bn, o_dn_fms_ref, o_dn_amt, o_cn_dt, o_cn_txn_id, o_cn_rms_bn, o_cn_fms_ref, o_cn_amt, o_status WITH RESUME;
			  	ELSE
			    	EXIT;
			  	END IF
			END while
			
			close c;
			free c;
			free s;
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_generatericpagingreport(asOfDate nvarchar(10), issDtFr date, issDtTo date, showExp boolean, showCanVoid boolean, 
								entityType nvarchar(50), entityNm nvarchar(100), pymtDtFr date, pymtDtTo date,
								expDtFr date, expDtTo date, woDtFr date, woDtTo date, canDtFr date, canDtTo date,
								voidDtFr date, voidDtTo date)
	returning nvarchar(30), nvarchar(25), nvarchar(50), nvarchar(100), nvarchar(50), decimal(16,2),
			decimal(16,2), date, datetime year to fraction(5), date, date, date, date, integer;
		 
			DEFINE o_bat_no nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
			DEFINE o_entity_type nvarchar(50);
			DEFINE o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_ricp_status nvarchar(50);
			DEFINE o_cp_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_net_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_dt_issuance date;
			DEFINE o_pymt_dt datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_dt_expiry date;
			DEFINE o_dt_wo date;
			DEFINE o_dt_can date;
			DEFINE o_dt_void date;
			DEFINE o_status integer;
					
			define o_statement lvarchar(2000);
			let o_statement = "select fjh.batch_no, fjh.fms_ref_no, fullEntT.nm_en, itm.entity_nm, fullStatusName.nm_en, ricp.cp_amt, itm.net_amt, ricp.dt_issuance, rcp.rcpt_dt, ricp.dt_expiry, ricp.dt_writeoff, ricp.dt_cancel, ricp.dt_void, date('" || asOfDate || "') - ricp.dt_issuance as status from rms_ricp ricp left join (select SUBSTR(SUBSTR(attr_ext_ref_no, CHARINDEX('-', attr_ext_ref_no)+1), 1, CHARINDEX('-', SUBSTR(attr_ext_ref_no, CHARINDEX('-', attr_ext_ref_no)))) as ricp_id, batch_no, fms_ref_no from rms_fms_jn_h) fjh on ricp.ricp_id = fjh.ricp_id left join rms_mtt_item itm on ricp.cp_no = itm.cp_no left join rms_mtt_rcpt rcp on itm.mtt_id = rcp.mtt_id left join (select param_cd, nm_en from rms_param where param_grp_nm = 'RICP-Status') as fullStatusName on ricp.status = fullStatusName.param_cd left join (select param_cd, nm_en from rms_param where param_grp_nm = 'EntityType') as fullEntT on ricp.entity_type = fullEntT.param_cd where ricp.dt_issuance <= date('" || asOfDate || "') and ricp.dt_issuance >= date('" || issDtFr || "') and ricp.dt_issuance <= date('" || issDtTo || "')";

			if (showExp = 'f') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.status != 'WO'";
			end if
			
			if (showCanVoid = 'f') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.status != 'C' and ricp.status != 'V'";
			end if
			
			if (entityType is not null and entityType != '') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.entityType = '" || entityType || "'";
			end if
			
			if (entityNm is not null and entityNm != '') then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and itm.entity_nm like '%" || entityNm || "'";
			end if
			
			if (pymtDtFr is not null and pymtDtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and cast(rcp.rcpt_dt as date) >= " || pymtDtFr || " and cast(rcp.rcpt_dt as date) <= " || pymtDtTo;
			end if
			
			if (expDtFr is not null and expDtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.dt_expiry >= " || expDtFr || " and ricp.dt_expiry <= " || expDtTo;
			end if
			
			if (woDtFr is not null and woDtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.dt_writeoff >= " || woDtFr || " and ricp.dt_writeoff <= " || woDtTo;
			end if
			
			if (canDtFr is not null and canDtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.dt_cancel >= " || canDtFr || " and ricp.dt_cancel <= " || canDtTo;
			end if
			
			if (voidDtFr is not null and voidDtTo is not null) then
				let o_statement = o_statement || " and ricp.dt_void >= " || voidDtFr || " and ricp.dt_void <= " || voidDtTo;
			end if
			
			let o_statement = o_statement || ";";
			
			prepare s from o_statement;
			declare c cursor for s;
			open c;
			while(1 = 1)
				fetch c into o_bat_no,o_fms_ref_no,o_entity_type,o_entity_nm,o_ricp_status,o_cp_amt,o_net_amt,o_dt_issuance,o_pymt_dt,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_wo,o_dt_can,o_dt_void,o_status;
				IF (SQLCODE != 100) THEN
			    	RETURN o_bat_no,o_fms_ref_no,o_entity_type,o_entity_nm,o_ricp_status,o_cp_amt,o_net_amt,o_dt_issuance,o_pymt_dt,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_wo,o_dt_can,o_dt_void,o_status WITH RESUME;
			  	ELSE
			    	EXIT;
			  	END IF
			END while
			
			close c;
			free c;
			free s;
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getbanknostmt(i_page integer,i_size integer, i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_file_nm nvarchar(255), i_uploaded_by nvarchar(255), i_dt_uploaded date)
returning nvarchar(255) as file_nm, integer as file_size_kb, nvarchar(255) as uploaded_by, date as dt_uploaded, integer as total;

define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_file_size integer;
define o_uploaded_by nvarchar(255);
define o_dt_uploaded date;
define calculatedpage integer;
define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

    let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
    let total = (select count(1) 
                from rms_rc_bankdoc t1
                left join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
                left join rms_user t3 on t1.created_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
                where (i_task_no is null or t2.task_no = i_task_no)
                and (i_file_nm is null or t1.file_nm like '%' || i_file_nm || '%')
                and (i_uploaded_by is null or t3.nm = i_uploaded_by)
                and (i_dt_uploaded is null or t1.dt_created = i_dt_uploaded));

    foreach c_sp_getbanknostmt for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.file_nm, t1.file_size_kb , t3.nm, t1.dt_created
		into o_file_nm, o_file_size, o_uploaded_by, o_dt_uploaded
	    from rms_rc_bankdoc t1
        left join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
        left join rms_user t3 on t1.created_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
	    where (i_task_no is null or t2.task_no = i_task_no)
                and (i_file_nm is null or t1.file_nm like '%' || i_file_nm || '%')
                and (i_uploaded_by is null or t3.nm = i_uploaded_by)
                and (i_dt_uploaded is null or t1.dt_created = i_dt_uploaded)

		return o_file_nm, o_file_size, o_uploaded_by, o_dt_uploaded, total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getbankpgfiletxn(i_page integer,i_size integer, i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_txn_ref nvarchar(50), i_dt_posting date)
returning nvarchar(50) as txn_ref, decimal(15,5) as credit, date as dt_posting, integer as total;

define o_txn_ref nvarchar(50);
define o_credit decimal(15,5);
define o_dt_posting date;
define calculatedpage integer;
define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

    let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
    let total = (select count(1)
                 from(
                    select t1.txn_ref, t1.dt_posting, t1.credit
                    from rms_rc_banktxn t1
                    inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
                    where t2.task_no = i_task_no
                    and substring(t1.txn_ref from 0 for 14) in (select stmt_no 
                                                                from rms_rc_pg t1
                                                                inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id)
                    )t3
                 where (i_txn_ref is null or t3.txn_ref = i_txn_ref)
                 and  (i_dt_posting is null or t3.dt_posting = i_dt_posting)
                 );

    foreach c_getbankpgfiletxn for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t3.txn_ref, t3.credit, t3.dt_posting
        into o_txn_ref, o_credit, o_dt_posting
        from(
             select t1.txn_ref, t1.dt_posting, t1.credit
             from rms_rc_banktxn t1
             inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
             where t2.task_no = i_task_no
             and substring(t1.txn_ref from 0 for 14) in (select stmt_no 
                                                         from rms_rc_pg t1
                                                         inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id)
             )t3
         where (i_txn_ref is null or t3.txn_ref = i_txn_ref)
         and  (i_dt_posting is null or t3.dt_posting = i_dt_posting)

		return o_txn_ref, o_credit, o_dt_posting, total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getbankpgtxnlisting(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_txn_date date,
                                    i_txn_type nvarchar(25), i_fnd_pg nvarchar(3), i_txn_id nvarchar(30), i_txn_cd nvarchar(50))
returning DateTime year to second as dt_txn,
          nvarchar(30) as txn_id,
          nvarchar(25) as txn_type,
          nvarchar(25) as txn_cd,
          nvarchar(3) as found_in_pg,
          --nvarchar(25) as sub_criteria,
          decimal(15,2) as txn_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as mdr_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as sst_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as net_amt,
          int as total;

define o_txn_date           DateTime year to second;
define o_txn_id             nvarchar(30);
define o_txn_type           nvarchar(25);
define o_txn_cd             nvarchar(25);
define c_fnd_in_pg          int;
define o_fnd_in_pg          nvarchar(3);
--define o_sub_cri            nvarchar(25);
define o_txn_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_mdr_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_sst_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_net_amt            decimal(15,2);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if;

--temp set to null
let i_txn_date = null;

if(i_fnd_pg is not null and i_fnd_pg = 'Yes') then
    let c_fnd_in_pg = 1;
elif (i_fnd_pg is not null and i_fnd_pg = 'No') then
    let c_fnd_in_pg = 0;
else
    let c_fnd_in_pg = null;
end if;

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(1)
             from rms_rc_bank t1
             inner join rms_rc_pgtxn t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
             where (i_task_no is null or t1.task_no = i_task_no)
             and (i_txn_date is null or t2.dt_txn = i_txn_date)
             and (i_txn_type is null or t2.txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
             and (c_fnd_in_pg is null or t2.found_in_rms = c_fnd_in_pg)
             and (i_txn_id is null or t2.txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
             and (i_txn_cd is null or t2.txn_cd like '%' || i_txn_cd || '%')
             --and (i_sub_cri is null or t2.sub_criteria like '%' || i_sub_cri || '%')
             );

foreach c_getbankpgtxnlisting for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t2.dt_txn, t2.txn_id, t2.txn_type, t2.txn_cd, 
            case when t2.found_in_rms = 1 then 'Yes'
                else 'No'
            end found_in_rms, 
           --t2.sub_criteria,
           t2.txn_amt, t2.mdr_amt, t2.sst_amt, t2.net_amt
    into o_txn_date, o_txn_id, o_txn_type, o_txn_cd, o_fnd_in_pg, 
         --o_sub_cri, 
         o_txn_amt, o_mdr_amt, o_sst_amt, o_net_amt 
    from rms_rc_bank t1
    inner join rms_rc_pgtxn t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
    where (i_task_no is null or t1.task_no = i_task_no)
    and (i_txn_date is null or t2.dt_txn = i_txn_date)
	and (i_txn_type is null or t2.txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
    and (c_fnd_in_pg is null or t2.found_in_rms = c_fnd_in_pg)
    and (i_txn_id is null or t2.txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
    and (i_txn_cd is null or t2.txn_cd like '%' || i_txn_cd || '%')
    --and (i_sub_cri is null or t2.sub_criteria like '%' || i_sub_cri || '%')

    return o_txn_date, o_txn_id, o_txn_type, o_txn_cd, o_fnd_in_pg, 
           --o_sub_cri,
           o_txn_amt, o_mdr_amt, o_sst_amt, o_net_amt, total with resume;

end foreach;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getBankRecon(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_rc_bank_id int8, i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_dt_settlement nvarchar(100), 
								i_merchant_id nvarchar(25), i_task_status nvarchar(25), i_dt_upload nvarchar(100), 
								i_recon_status nvarchar(25))
								
returning 
		int8 as o_rc_bank_id,
		nvarchar(40) as o_task_no,
		nvarchar(100) as o_dt_settlement,
		nvarchar(50) as o_merchant_id,
		nvarchar(50) as o_task_status,
		nvarchar(100) as o_dt_upload,
		nvarchar(50) as o_recon_status,
		integer as total;
	
	define total integer;
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define o_rc_bank_id int8;
	define o_task_no nvarchar(40);
	define o_dt_settlement nvarchar(100);
	define o_merchant_id nvarchar(50);
	define o_task_status nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_upload nvarchar(100);
	define o_recon_status nvarchar(50);
	
if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
        raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
    end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
		from rms_rc_bank T1
        left join rms_param T2 on T1.task_status = T2.param_cd and T2.param_grp_nm='Status-Task'
        left join rms_param T3 on T1.recon_status= T3.param_cd and T3.param_grp_nm='Status-BRC'
        left join rms_rc_pg T4 on T1.rc_pg_id=T4.rc_pg_id 
--        left join rms_param T4 on T1.txn_type= T4.param_cd and T4.param_grp_nm='RIPL-TxnType'
        where (i_rc_bank_id is null or rc_bank_id = i_rc_bank_id)
        				  and (i_task_no is null or T1.task_no like '%' || i_task_no || '%')
                          and (i_dt_settlement is null or date(T4.dt_settlement) == to_date(i_dt_settlement,'%Y-%m-%d')::Date)
                          and (i_merchant_id is null or T4.merchant_id like '%' || i_merchant_id || '%')
                          and (i_task_status is null or T1.task_status == i_task_status)
                          and (i_dt_upload is null or date(T1.dt_upload) == to_date(i_dt_upload,'%Y-%m-%d')::Date)
                          and (i_recon_status is null or T1.recon_status == i_recon_status)
        			);

	foreach c_getBankReconTask for
        select  skip calculatedpage limit i_size T1.rc_bank_id, T1.task_no, TO_CHAR(T4.dt_settlement, '%d %b %Y'),
        T4.merchant_id, T2.nm_en, TO_CHAR(T1.dt_upload, '%d %b %Y %H:%M:%S'), T3.nm_en
        into o_rc_bank_id,o_task_no, o_dt_settlement, o_merchant_id, o_task_status, o_dt_upload, o_recon_status
        from rms_rc_bank T1
        left join rms_param T2 on T1.task_status = T2.param_cd and T2.param_grp_nm='Status-Task'
        left join rms_param T3 on T1.recon_status= T3.param_cd and T3.param_grp_nm='Status-BRC'
        left join rms_rc_pg T4 on T1.rc_pg_id=T4.rc_pg_id 
--        left join rms_param T4 on T1.txn_type= T4.param_cd and T4.param_grp_nm='RIPL-TxnType'
        where (i_rc_bank_id is null or rc_bank_id = i_rc_bank_id)
        				  and (i_task_no is null or T1.task_no like '%' || i_task_no || '%')
                          and (i_dt_settlement is null or date(T4.dt_settlement) == to_date(i_dt_settlement,'%Y-%m-%d')::Date)
                          and (i_merchant_id is null or T4.merchant_id like '%' || i_merchant_id || '%')
                          and (i_task_status is null or T1.task_status == i_task_status)
                          and (i_dt_upload is null or date(T1.dt_upload) == to_date(i_dt_upload,'%Y-%m-%d')::Date)
                          and (i_recon_status is null or T1.recon_status == i_recon_status)
        order by T4.dt_settlement desc
	
		return o_rc_bank_id,o_task_no, o_dt_settlement, o_merchant_id, o_task_status, o_dt_upload, o_recon_status, total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getbanktxnlisting(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_txn_ref nvarchar(50),
                                        i_acct_no nvarchar(50), i_brn_chn nvarchar(50))
returning nvarchar(50) as txn_ref,
          nvarchar(50) as acct_no,
          nvarchar(50) as brn_chn,
          DateTime year to second as dt_posting,
          decimal(15,5) as credit,
          int as total;

define o_txn_ref            nvarchar(50);
define o_acct_no            nvarchar(50);
define o_brn_chn            nvarchar(50);
define o_dt_posting         DateTime year to second; 
define o_credit             decimal(15,5);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if;

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(1)
             from rms_rc_bank t1
             inner join rms_rc_banktxn t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
             where (i_task_no is null or t1.task_no = i_task_no)
             and (i_txn_ref is null or t2.txn_ref like '%' || i_txn_ref || '%')
             and (i_acct_no is null or t2.acct_no like '%' || i_acct_no || '%')
             and (i_brn_chn is null or t2.brn_chn like '%' || i_brn_chn || '%')
             );

foreach c_getbanktxnlisting for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t2.txn_ref, t2.acct_no, t2.brn_chn, t2.dt_posting, t2.credit
    into o_txn_ref, o_acct_no, o_brn_chn, o_dt_posting, o_credit
    from rms_rc_bank t1
    inner join rms_rc_banktxn t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
    where (i_task_no is null or t1.task_no = i_task_no)
    and (i_txn_ref is null or t2.txn_ref like '%' || i_txn_ref || '%')
    and (i_acct_no is null or t2.acct_no like '%' || i_acct_no || '%')
    and (i_brn_chn is null or t2.brn_chn like '%' || i_brn_chn || '%')

    return o_txn_ref, o_acct_no, o_brn_chn, o_dt_posting, o_credit, total with resume;
end foreach;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getconfig(i_config_cd NVARCHAR(100))
RETURNING NVARCHAR(255) AS config_value;

DEFINE o_config_value NVARCHAR(255);

	FOREACH c_getconfig FOR
		SELECT config_value
		INTO o_config_value
		FROM rms_config
		WHERE (i_config_cd IS NULL OR config_cd = i_config_cd)
		
		RETURN o_config_value WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH

END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getdi(i_page INTEGER,i_size INTEGER,i_di_id int8, i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_txn_type nvarchar(50),
                          i_entity_type nvarchar(50), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_dt_effective date, i_dt_expiry date, 
                          i_item_ref_no nvarchar(30), i_approval_status nvarchar(10), i_dt_approval date, i_status nvarchar(10))
returning int8 as di_id,
          int as fee_detail_pk,
          nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id,
          nvarchar(50) as entity_type,
          nvarchar(20) as entity_no,
          datetime year to second as dt_effective,
          datetime year to second as dt_expiry,
          datetime year to second as dt_termination,
          nvarchar(30) as item_ref_no,
          nvarchar(10) as approval_status,
          datetime year to second as dt_approval,
          int as no_of_yr,
          decimal(16,2) as unit_fee,
          decimal(16,2) as total_fee,
          decimal(16,2) as bal_di_amt,
          datetime year to second as next_calc_dt,
          nvarchar(100) as dt_created,
          nvarchar(100) as dt_modified,
          nvarchar(25) as created_by,
          nvarchar(255) as created_by_nm,
          nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
          nvarchar(255) as modified_by_nm,
          nvarchar(10) as status,
          nvarchar(50) as status_nm_en,
          nvarchar(50) as status_nm_bm,
          nvarchar(50) as txn_type,
          int as total;

define o_di_id int8;
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
define o_entity_type nvarchar(50);
define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
define o_dt_effective datetime year to second;
define o_dt_expiry datetime year to second;
define o_dt_termination datetime year to second; 
define o_item_ref_no nvarchar(30);
define o_approval_status nvarchar(10);
define o_dt_approval datetime year to second;
define o_no_of_yr int;
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_total_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_bal_di_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_next_calc_dt datetime year to second; 
define o_dt_created nvarchar(100);
define o_dt_modified nvarchar(100);
define o_created_by nvarchar(25); 
define o_created_by_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_status nvarchar(10);
define o_status_nm_en nvarchar(50); 
define o_status_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
define o_txn_type nvarchar(50);			
define calculatedPage int;
define total int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedPage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(1) 
             from rms_di t1
             left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.created_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
             left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
             left outer join rms_param t4 on t1.status = t4.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t5 on t1.approval_status = t5.param_cd
             left join rms_param T6 on T1.entity_type= T6.param_cd and T6.param_grp_nm='EntityType'
             left outer join rms_param t7 on t1.txn_type = t7.param_cd
             where (i_di_id is null or di_id = i_di_id)
             and (i_fee_detail_id is null or fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id || '%')
             and (i_txn_type is null or t1.txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
             and (i_entity_type is null or entity_type like '%' || i_entity_type || '%' )
             and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
             and (i_dt_effective is null or dt_effective = i_dt_effective)
             and (i_dt_expiry is null or dt_expiry = i_dt_expiry)
             and (i_item_ref_no is null or item_ref_no like '%' || i_item_ref_no || '%')
             and (i_approval_status is null or approval_status like '%' || i_approval_status || '%')
             and (i_dt_approval is null or dt_approval = i_dt_approval)
             and (i_status is null or t1.status like '%' || i_status || '%')
             and t4.param_grp_nm = 'DI-Status'
             and t5.param_grp_nm = 'DI-ApprovalStatus'
             and t7.param_grp_nm = 'DI-TxnType'
             
            );

foreach c_getdi for
    select skip calculatedPage limit i_size 
    		t1.di_id, 
    		t1.fee_detail_pk, 
    		t1.fee_detail_id, 
    		t6.nm_en, 
    		t1.entity_no, 
    		t1.dt_effective, 
    		t1.dt_expiry, 
    		t1.dt_termination,
            t1.item_ref_no, 
            t5.nm_en, 
            t1.dt_approval, 
            t1.no_of_yr, 
            t1.unit_fee, 
            t1.total_fee, 
            t1.bal_di_amt,
            t1.next_calc_dt, 
            TO_CHAR(T1.dt_created, '%d %b %Y %H:%M:%S'),
            TO_CHAR(T1.dt_modified, '%d %b %Y %H:%M:%S'),
            t1.created_by, 
            t2.nm, 
            t1.modified_by, 
            t3.nm,
            t1.status, 
            t4.nm_en, 
            t4.nm_bm, 
            t1.txn_type
           
    into 	o_di_id, 
    		o_fee_detail_pk, 
    		o_fee_detail_id, 
    		o_entity_type, 
    		o_entity_no, 
    		o_dt_effective, 
    		o_dt_expiry, 
    		o_dt_termination,
         	o_item_ref_no, 
          	o_approval_status, 
         	o_dt_approval, 
          	o_no_of_yr, 
         	o_unit_fee, 
         	o_total_fee, 
         	o_bal_di_amt,
         	o_next_calc_dt, 
        	o_dt_created, 
        	o_dt_modified, 
         	o_created_by, 
         	o_created_by_nm, 
         	o_modified_by, 
         	o_modified_by_nm,
         	o_status, 
         	o_status_nm_en, 
         	o_status_nm_bm, 
         	o_txn_type
    from rms_di t1
             left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.created_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
             left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
             left outer join rms_param t4 on t1.status = t4.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t5 on t1.approval_status = t5.param_cd
             left join rms_param T6 on T1.entity_type= T6.param_cd and T6.param_grp_nm='EntityType'
             left outer join rms_param t7 on t1.txn_type = t7.param_cd
             where (i_di_id is null or di_id = i_di_id)
             and (i_fee_detail_id is null or fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id || '%')
             and (i_txn_type is null or txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
             and (i_entity_type is null or entity_type like '%' || i_entity_type || '%' )
             and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
             and (i_dt_effective is null or dt_effective = i_dt_effective)
             and (i_dt_expiry is null or dt_expiry = i_dt_expiry)
             and (i_item_ref_no is null or item_ref_no like '%' || i_item_ref_no || '%')
             and (i_approval_status is null or approval_status like '%' || i_approval_status || '%')
             and (i_dt_approval is null or dt_approval = i_dt_approval)
             and (i_status is null or t1.status like '%' || i_status || '%')
             and t4.param_grp_nm = 'DI-Status'
             and t5.param_grp_nm = 'DI-ApprovalStatus'
             and t7.param_grp_nm = 'DI-TxnType'
     order by T1.dt_modified desc
     
                 

return o_di_id, 
	   o_fee_detail_pk, 
	   o_fee_detail_id, 
	   o_entity_type, 
	   o_entity_no, 
	   o_dt_effective, 
	   o_dt_expiry, 
	   o_dt_termination,
       o_item_ref_no, 
       o_approval_status, 
       o_dt_approval, 
       o_no_of_yr, 
       o_unit_fee, 
       o_total_fee, 
       o_bal_di_amt,
       o_next_calc_dt, 
       o_dt_created, 
       o_dt_modified, 
       o_created_by, 
       o_created_by_nm, 
       o_modified_by, 
       o_modified_by_nm,
       o_status, 
       o_status_nm_en, 
       o_status_nm_bm, 
       o_txn_type, 
       total WITH RESUME;

end foreach

end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getdiagequeuerpt()

returning integer;

define o_count integer;

	select count(1) into o_count 
	from rms_rpt_di_age 
	where status = "P" or status = "I";

	return o_count with resume;

end procedure;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getdiaginglistingrpt(i_page int, i_size int, i_rpt_di_age_id int8, i_p_dt_req date, i_p_tmn_status int, i_p_ent_ty nvarchar(1), 
                               i_p_ent_nm nvarchar(200), i_p_txn_ty nvarchar(10), i_p_status nvarchar(10), 
							   i_p_dt_exp_fr date, i_p_dt_exp_to date,
							   i_p_dt_eff_fr date, i_p_dt_eff_to date,
							   i_p_dt_app_fr date, i_p_dt_app_to date,
							   i_p_dt_tmn_fr date, i_p_dt_tmn_to date,
							   i_created_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by nvarchar(25),
							   i_status nvarchar(10), i_p_email nvarchar(255), i_p_file_type nvarchar(5),
							   i_p_file_size int, i_p_file_nm nvarchar(255), i_p_batch_no nvarchar(30), i_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25))
								
returning	int8 as rpt_di_age_id,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_req,
			int as p_tmn_status,
			nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty,
			nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm,
			nvarchar(10) as p_txn_ty,
			nvarchar(10) as p_status,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_to,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(10) as status,
			nvarchar(50) as p_email,
			nvarchar(50) as p_file_type,
			int as p_file_size,
			nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,
			nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no,
			nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no,
			nvarchar(10) as task_id,
			int as total;	
			
define o_rpt_di_age_id		int8;
define o_p_dt_req           datetime year to second;
define o_p_tmn_status		int;
define o_p_ent_ty			nvarchar(1);
define o_p_ent_nm		    nvarchar(100);
define o_p_txn_ty		    nvarchar(10);
define o_p_status	        nvarchar(10);
define o_p_dt_exp_fr	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_exp_to 	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_to		datetime year to second;
define o_dt_created			datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified		datetime year to second;
define o_created_by			nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by		nvarchar(25);
define o_status				nvarchar(10);
define o_p_email			nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_type		nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_size		int;
define o_p_file_nm		    nvarchar(255);
define o_p_batch_no		    nvarchar(30);
define o_p_fms_ref_no		nvarchar(25);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;


if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;

    let total = (select count(1)
                    from rms_rpt_di_age t1
                            		where (i_rpt_di_age_id is null or t1.rpt_di_age_id = i_rpt_di_age_id)		
									and (i_p_dt_req is null or t1.p_dt_req <= i_p_dt_req)
							        and (i_p_tmn_status is null or t1.p_tmn_status = i_p_tmn_status)
							        and (i_p_ent_ty is null or t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
							        and (i_p_ent_nm is null or t1.p_ent_nm like '%' || i_p_ent_nm ||'%')
							        and (i_p_status is null or t1.p_status = i_p_status)
							        and (i_p_dt_exp_fr is null or t1.p_dt_exp_fr >= i_p_dt_exp_fr)
							        and (i_p_dt_exp_to is null or t1.p_dt_exp_to <= i_p_dt_exp_to)
							        and (i_p_dt_eff_fr is null or t1.p_dt_eff_fr >= i_p_dt_eff_fr)
							        and (i_p_dt_eff_to is null or t1.p_dt_eff_to <= i_p_dt_eff_to)
							        and (i_p_dt_app_fr is null or t1.p_dt_app_fr >= i_p_dt_app_fr)
							        and (i_p_dt_app_to is null or t1.p_dt_app_to <= i_p_dt_app_to)
							        and (i_p_dt_tmn_fr is null or t1.p_dt_tmn_fr >= i_p_dt_tmn_fr)
							        and (i_p_dt_tmn_to is null or t1.p_dt_tmn_to <= i_p_dt_tmn_to)
							        and (i_created_by is null or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
							        and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
							        and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
							        and (i_p_email is null or t1.p_email = i_p_email)
							        and (i_p_file_type is null or t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type)
							        and (i_p_file_size is null or t1.p_file_size = i_p_file_size)
							        and (i_p_file_nm is null or t1.p_file_nm like '%' || i_p_file_nm ||'%')
							        and (i_p_batch_no is null or t1.p_batch_no like '%' || i_p_batch_no ||'%')
							        and (i_p_fms_ref_no is null or t1.p_fms_ref_no like '%' || i_p_fms_ref_no ||'%')	
                          );
                         
	foreach c_getdiaging for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.rpt_di_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_tmn_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm, t1.p_txn_ty, t1.p_status,
		t1.p_dt_exp_fr, t1.p_dt_exp_to, t1.p_dt_eff_fr, t1.p_dt_eff_to, t1.p_dt_app_fr, t1.p_dt_app_to, t1.p_dt_tmn_fr,t1.p_dt_tmn_to,
	    t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm, 
	    t1.p_batch_no, t1.p_fms_ref_no
		into o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm,
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no
		from rms_rpt_di_age t1
		where (i_rpt_di_age_id is null or t1.rpt_di_age_id = i_rpt_di_age_id)		
		and (i_p_dt_req is null or t1.p_dt_req <= i_p_dt_req)
        and (i_p_tmn_status is null or t1.p_tmn_status = i_p_tmn_status)
        and (i_p_ent_ty is null or t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
        and (i_p_ent_nm is null or t1.p_ent_nm like '%' || i_p_ent_nm ||'%')
        and (i_p_status is null or t1.p_status = i_p_status)
        and (i_p_dt_exp_fr is null or t1.p_dt_exp_fr >= i_p_dt_exp_fr)
        and (i_p_dt_exp_to is null or t1.p_dt_exp_to <= i_p_dt_exp_to)
        and (i_p_dt_eff_fr is null or t1.p_dt_eff_fr >= i_p_dt_eff_fr)
        and (i_p_dt_eff_to is null or t1.p_dt_eff_to <= i_p_dt_eff_to)
        and (i_p_dt_app_fr is null or t1.p_dt_app_fr >= i_p_dt_app_fr)
        and (i_p_dt_app_to is null or t1.p_dt_app_to <= i_p_dt_app_to)
        and (i_p_dt_tmn_fr is null or t1.p_dt_tmn_fr >= i_p_dt_tmn_fr)
        and (i_p_dt_tmn_to is null or t1.p_dt_tmn_to <= i_p_dt_tmn_to)
        and (i_created_by is null or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
        and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
        and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
        and (i_p_email is null or t1.p_email = i_p_email)
        and (i_p_file_type is null or t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type)
        and (i_p_file_size is null or t1.p_file_size = i_p_file_size)
        and (i_p_file_nm is null or t1.p_file_nm like '%' || i_p_file_nm ||'%')
        and (i_p_batch_no is null or t1.p_batch_no like '%' || i_p_batch_no ||'%')
        and (i_p_fms_ref_no is null or t1.p_fms_ref_no like '%' || i_p_fms_ref_no ||'%')
		order by t1.dt_created desc
		
		return o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_di_age_id,6,'0'),total with resume;	
		
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getdiagingrpt(i_rpt_di_age_id int8)
								
returning	int8 as rpt_di_age_id,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_req,
			int as p_tmn_status,
			nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty,
			nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm,
			nvarchar(10) as p_txn_ty,
			nvarchar(10) as p_status,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_to,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(10) as status,
			nvarchar(50) as p_email,
			nvarchar(50) as p_file_type,
			int as p_file_size,
			nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,
			nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no,
			nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no,
			nvarchar(10) as task_id;
			
define o_rpt_di_age_id		int8;
define o_p_dt_req           datetime year to second;
define o_p_tmn_status		int;
define o_p_ent_ty			nvarchar(1);
define o_p_ent_nm		    nvarchar(100);
define o_p_txn_ty		    nvarchar(10);
define o_p_status	        nvarchar(10);
define o_p_dt_exp_fr	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_exp_to 	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_to		datetime year to second;
define o_dt_created			datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified		datetime year to second;
define o_created_by			nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by		nvarchar(25);
define o_status				nvarchar(10);
define o_p_email			nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_type		nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_size		int;
define o_p_file_nm		    nvarchar(255);
define o_p_batch_no		    nvarchar(30);
define o_p_fms_ref_no		nvarchar(25);

	foreach c_getdiaging for
		select t1.rpt_di_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_tmn_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm, t1.p_txn_ty, t1.p_status,
		t1.p_dt_exp_fr, t1.p_dt_exp_to, t1.p_dt_eff_fr, t1.p_dt_eff_to, t1.p_dt_app_fr, t1.p_dt_app_to, t1.p_dt_tmn_fr,t1.p_dt_tmn_to,
	    t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm, 
	    t1.p_batch_no, t1.p_fms_ref_no
		into o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm,
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no
		from rms_rpt_di_age t1
		where t1.rpt_di_age_id = i_rpt_di_age_id	
		
		return o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_di_age_id,6,'0') with resume;	
		
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getExpiredMTTPG(daysLimit INTEGER, expiredString nvarchar(25))
	returning integer as mtt_pg_id, integer as mtt_id, datetime year to fraction(5) as pymt_submit_dt, nvarchar(7) as pg_txn_type, nvarchar(3) as pg_pymt_method,
		nvarchar(3) as pg_service_id, nvarchar(20) as pg_pymt_id, nvarchar(100) as pg_pymt_desc, decimal(16,2) as pg_pymt_amt, nvarchar(3) as pg_curr_cd,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_b4tax_amt, decimal(16,2) as pg_tax_amt, nvarchar(2) as pg_lang_cd, nvarchar(30) as pg_txn_id, nvarchar(30) as pg_issuing_bank,
		nvarchar(12) as pg_auth_cd, integer as pg_txn_status, nvarchar(255) as pg_txn_msg, nvarchar(100) as pg_hash_value, nvarchar(100) as pg_hash_value2,
		nvarchar(100) as pg_qhash_value, integer as pg_txn_exists, nvarchar(255) as pg_query_desc, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by
		, decimal(16,2) as pg_refund_amt
		, nvarchar(255) as pg_bank_refno
		, nvarchar(255) as pg_session_id
		, nvarchar(3) as pg_token_type
		, nvarchar(50) as pg_token
		, datetime year to fraction(5) as pg_resp_time
		, nvarchar(19) as pg_cardno_mask
		, nvarchar(30) as pg_cardholder
		, nvarchar(10) as pg_cardtype
		, nvarchar(6) as pg_cardexp;
		 
			DEFINE o_mtt_pg_id integer;
			DEFINE o_mtt_id integer;
			DEFINE o_pymt_submit_dt datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_type nvarchar(7);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_service_id nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_id nvarchar(20);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_desc nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_curr_cd nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_b4tax_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_tax_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_lang_cd nvarchar(2);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_id nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_issuing_bank nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_auth_cd nvarchar(12);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_status integer;
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_msg nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_hash_value nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_hash_value2 nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_qhash_value nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_exists integer;
			DEFINE o_pg_query_desc nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
			DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
			DEFINE o_pg_refund_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_bank_refno nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_session_id nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_token_type nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_token nvarchar(50);
			DEFINE o_pg_resp_time datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardno_mask nvarchar(19);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardholder nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardtype nvarchar(10);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardexp nvarchar(6);
		
	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT mtt_pg_id, mtt_id, pymt_submit_dt, pg_txn_type, pg_pymt_method, pg_service_id, pg_pymt_id, pg_pymt_desc
        , pg_pymt_amt, pg_curr_cd, pg_b4tax_amt, pg_tax_amt, pg_lang_cd, pg_txn_id, pg_issuing_bank, pg_auth_cd, pg_txn_status
        , pg_txn_msg, pg_hash_value, pg_hash_value2, pg_qhash_value, pg_txn_exists, pg_query_desc, dt_created, dt_modified
        , created_by, modified_by, pg_refund_amt, pg_bank_refno, pg_session_id, pg_token_type, pg_token, pg_resp_time, pg_cardno_mask
        , pg_cardholder, pg_cardtype, pg_cardexp
        INTO o_mtt_pg_id, o_mtt_id, o_pymt_submit_dt, o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_pg_pymt_id, o_pg_pymt_desc
        , o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_pg_b4tax_amt, o_pg_tax_amt, o_pg_lang_cd, o_pg_txn_id, o_pg_issuing_bank, o_pg_auth_cd, o_pg_txn_status
        , o_pg_txn_msg, o_pg_hash_value, o_pg_hash_value2, o_pg_qhash_value, o_pg_txn_exists, o_pg_query_desc, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified
        , o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_pg_refund_amt, o_pg_bank_refno, o_pg_session_id, o_pg_token_type, o_pg_token, o_pg_resp_time
        , o_pg_cardno_mask, o_pg_cardholder, o_pg_cardtype, o_pg_cardexp
        FROM rms_mtt_pg
        where pg_txn_status = 1 
        	and ((current-pymt_submit_dt)::INTERVAL DAY(9) TO DAY::char(10)::INT) < daysLimit 
        	and LOWER(pg_txn_msg) like '%' || LOWER(expiredString) || '%'
		
		RETURN o_mtt_pg_id, o_mtt_id, o_pymt_submit_dt, o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_pg_pymt_id, o_pg_pymt_desc
        , o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_pg_b4tax_amt, o_pg_tax_amt, o_pg_lang_cd, o_pg_txn_id, o_pg_issuing_bank, o_pg_auth_cd, o_pg_txn_status
        , o_pg_txn_msg, o_pg_hash_value, o_pg_hash_value2, o_pg_qhash_value, o_pg_txn_exists, o_pg_query_desc, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified
        , o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_pg_refund_amt, o_pg_bank_refno, o_pg_session_id, o_pg_token_type, o_pg_token, o_pg_resp_time
        , o_pg_cardno_mask, o_pg_cardholder, o_pg_cardtype, o_pg_cardexp WITH RESUME;
	END foreach
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfeedetailitems(fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), fee_grp_id int, ss_cd nvarchar(100),
										last_sync_dt datetime year to fraction(5), exclude_deleted int)
returning nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id, 
		integer as fee_grp_id, 
		nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_en, 
		nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_bm, 
        decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, 
        date as promo_startdt, 
        date as promo_enddt, 
        decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
        nvarchar(10) as tax_cd,
        integer as  allow_otc, 
        nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, 
        integer as ll_start_day, 
        integer as ll_start_mth, 
		integer as ll_end_day, 
		integer as ll_end_mth, 
		nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, 
		nvarchar(100) as ss_cd,
		nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,
		nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
		nvarchar(50) as tax_cd_nm_en,
		nvarchar(50) as tax_cd_nm_bm,
		decimal(16,2) as tax_pct,
		nvarchar(10) as status;
 
	define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_fee_grp_id integer;
	define o_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100);
	define o_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_promo_startdt date;
	define o_promo_enddt date;
	define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_tax_cd nvarchar(10);
	define o_allow_otc integer;
	define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_ll_start_day integer;
	define o_ll_start_mth integer;
	define o_ll_end_day integer;
	define o_ll_end_mth integer;
	define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
	define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	define o_fee_grp_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_fee_grp_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define o_tax_cd_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_tax_cd_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define o_tax_pct decimal(16,2);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
 
foreach c_getfeedetailitems for
 
        SELECT t1.fee_detail_id, t1.fee_grp_id, t1.fee_detail_nm_e, t1.fee_detail_nm_b, t1.unit_fee, t1.promo_startdt, t1.promo_enddt, t1.promo_fee,
        t3.tax_cd , t1.allow_otc, t1.ll_parent_id, t1.ll_start_day, t1.ll_start_mth, t1.ll_end_day, t1.ll_end_mth, t1.ledger_cd, t1.ss_cd,
        t2.fee_grp_nm_en, t2.fee_grp_nm_bm, t3.tax_cd_nm_en, t3.tax_cd_nm_bm, t3.tax_pct, t1.status
        INTO o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd,
      	o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_tax_cd_nm_en, o_tax_cd_nm_bm, o_tax_pct, o_status
        FROM rms_mft t1
        left outer join rms_fee_group t2 on t1.fee_grp_id = t2.fee_grp_id
        left outer join rms_tax_code t3 on t1.tax_cd_id = t3.tax_cd_id
        WHERE  (fee_detail_id IS NULL OR t1.fee_detail_id LIKE '%' || fee_detail_id || '%')
        			AND (fee_grp_id IS NULL OR t1.fee_grp_id = fee_grp_id)
        			AND (ss_cd IS NULL OR t1.ss_cd LIKE '%' || ss_cd || '%')
        			AND (last_sync_dt IS NULL OR t1.dt_modified >= last_sync_dt)
        			AND (exclude_deleted <> 1 OR (exclude_deleted = 1 AND t1.status = 'A'))
		RETURN o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd,
      	o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_tax_cd_nm_en, o_tax_cd_nm_bm, o_tax_pct, o_status WITH RESUME;
end foreach
 
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getFeeGroup()
	returning integer as fee_grp_id,nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
	DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_created, DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_grp_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_fee_grp_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define total integer;

	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_fee_group
        WHERE status = 'A');

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT  fee_grp_id, fee_grp_nm_en, fee_grp_nm_bm, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status
        INTO o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status
        FROM rms_fee_group WHERE status = 'A'

		
		RETURN o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfeegroup_v2(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_fee_grp_nm_en nvarchar(50), i_fee_grp_nm_bm nvarchar(50),
									i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_status nvarchar(10))
returning int as fee_grp_id,
        nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,
		nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
		datetime year to second as dt_modified, 
		nvarchar(25) as modified_by, 
		nvarchar(10) as status,
		nvarchar(50) as status_en,
		nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
		integer as total;

        
    define o_fee_grp_id int;
	define o_fee_grp_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_fee_grp_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define o_status_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_status_bm nvarchar(50);
	define total integer;
	define calculatedpage integer;

    if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
        raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
    end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_fee_group t1
					left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
					left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
        			where (i_fee_grp_nm_en is null or t1.fee_grp_nm_en like '%' || i_fee_grp_nm_en || '%')
        					and (i_fee_grp_nm_bm is null or t1.fee_grp_nm_bm like '%' || i_fee_grp_nm_bm || '%')
       						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        					and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        					and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        					and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                            and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
        			);

	foreach c_getfeegroup for
        select  skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.fee_grp_id, t1.fee_grp_nm_en, t1.fee_grp_nm_bm, t1.dt_modified, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t3.nm_en, t3.nm_bm
        into o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm
        from rms_fee_group t1
        left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
        where (i_fee_grp_nm_en is null or t1.fee_grp_nm_en like '%' || i_fee_grp_nm_en || '%')
        		and (i_fee_grp_nm_bm is null or t1.fee_grp_nm_bm like '%' || i_fee_grp_nm_bm || '%')
       			and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        		and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        		and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        		and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
        order by t1.fee_grp_nm_en
	
		return o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm, total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfms(i_page int, i_size int, i_fms_cd nvarchar(50), i_modified_by nvarchar(25),i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second,
                 i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_status nvarchar(10))
returning int as fms_id,
            nvarchar(25) as fms_cd,
            int as cong_led_cnt,
            nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
            datetime year to second as  dt_modified,
            int as is_active,
            int as mft_total,
            int as total;

define o_fms_id int;
define o_fms_cd nvarchar(25);
define o_cong_led_cnt int;
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define o_is_active int;
define calculatedpage int;
define total int;
define o_mft_total int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(*)
             from (
                 select t1.fms_id, t1.fms_cd, t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.is_active, t1.dt_modified
                 from rms_fms t1
                 left outer join rms_fms_ledger t2 on t1.fms_id = t2.fms_id
                 left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
                 where (i_fms_cd is null or t1.fms_cd like '%' || i_fms_cd || '%')
                   and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by like '%' || t3.nm || '%')
                   and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
                   and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
                   and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
                 group by t1.fms_id, t1.fms_cd, t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.is_active, t1.dt_modified
             ) as subquery);

LET o_mft_total = (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM rms_mft where status = 'A');

foreach c_getfms for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.fms_id, t1.fms_cd,  count(case when t2.found = 'F' then 1 else null end), 
        t1.modified_by, t1.is_active, t1.dt_modified
    into o_fms_id, o_fms_cd, o_cong_led_cnt, o_modified_by, o_is_active, o_dt_modified
    from rms_fms t1
    left outer join rms_fms_ledger t2 on t1.fms_id = t2.fms_id
    left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
    where (i_fms_cd is null or t1.fms_cd like '%' || i_fms_cd || '%')
        and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by like '%' || t3.nm || '%')
        and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
    group by t1.fms_id, t1.fms_cd, t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.is_active, t1.dt_modified
    order by t1.fms_id
    	
    return o_fms_id, o_fms_cd, o_cong_led_cnt, o_modified_by, o_dt_modified, o_is_active,o_mft_total, total with resume;
end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsaccount(
    i_page integer,
    i_size integer,
    i_acct_nm nvarchar(50),
    i_acct_type nvarchar(25),
    i_acct_cd nvarchar(10),
    i_modified_by nvarchar(25),
    i_dt_modified datetime year to second,
    i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second,
    i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second
)
returning
    integer as fms_acct_id,
    nvarchar(50) as acct_nm,
    nvarchar(25) as acct_type,
    nvarchar(10) as acct_cd,
    nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
    datetime year to second as dt_modified,
    integer as total;
 
define o_fms_acct_id integer;
define o_acct_nm nvarchar(50);
define o_acct_type nvarchar(25);
define o_acct_cd nvarchar(10);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define total integer;
define calculatedpage integer;
 
if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_size < 1) then
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null or invalid integer";
end if;
 
let calculatedpage = (i_page - 1) * i_size;

let total = (
    select count(1)
    from rms_fms_acct t1
    where (i_acct_nm is null or t1.acct_nm like '%' || i_acct_nm || '%')
        and (i_acct_type is null or t1.acct_type like '%' || i_acct_type || '%')
        and (i_acct_cd is null or t1.acct_cd like '%' || i_acct_cd || '%')
        and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
        and (i_dt_modified is null or date(t1.dt_modified) = date(i_dt_modified))
        and ((i_dt_modified_fr is null and i_dt_modified_to is null) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is not null and i_dt_modified_to is not null and 
              t1.dt_modified between i_dt_modified_fr and i_dt_modified_to) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is not null and i_dt_modified_to is null and
              t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is null and i_dt_modified_to is not null and
              t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to))
);
 
foreach c_getfmsaccount for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size
        t1.fms_acct_id, t1.acct_nm, t1.acct_type, t1.acct_cd, t1.modified_by, t1.dt_modified
    into o_fms_acct_id, o_acct_nm, o_acct_type, o_acct_cd, o_modified_by, o_dt_modified
    from rms_fms_acct t1
    where (i_acct_nm is null or t1.acct_nm like '%' || i_acct_nm || '%')
        and (i_acct_type is null or t1.acct_type like '%' || i_acct_type || '%')
        and (i_acct_cd is null or t1.acct_cd like '%' || i_acct_cd || '%')
        and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
        and (i_dt_modified is null or date(t1.dt_modified) = date(i_dt_modified))
        and ((i_dt_modified_fr is null and i_dt_modified_to is null) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is not null and i_dt_modified_to is not null and 
              t1.dt_modified between i_dt_modified_fr and i_dt_modified_to) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is not null and i_dt_modified_to is null and
              t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr) or
             (i_dt_modified_fr is null and i_dt_modified_to is not null and
              t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to))
    order by t1.acct_nm
 
    return o_fms_acct_id, o_acct_nm, o_acct_type, o_acct_cd, o_modified_by, o_dt_modified, total with resume;
end foreach;
 
end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsari()

returning nvarchar(100) as type,nvarchar(100) as link_branch,decimal(16,2) as amt,nvarchar(100) as cust,nvarchar(100) as rms_batch_no, date as dt_sent,nvarchar(255) as desc,
            nvarchar(100) as attr_ext_sys, nvarchar(100) as coa1,nvarchar(100) as coa2,nvarchar(100) as branch,int as qty,nvarchar(100) as sub_acct,nvarchar(100) as txn_desc,
            decimal(16,2) as unit_price, nvarchar(30) as rcpt_no,nvarchar(100) as payee_info,nvarchar(100) as ent_nm,nvarchar(100) as ent_no,nvarchar(100) as ent_ty,
            decimal(16,2) as item_amt,nvarchar(100) as pymt_mode,decimal(16,2) as item_tax_amt;

define o_type           nvarchar(100);
define o_link_branch    nvarchar(100);
define o_amt            decimal(16,2);
define o_cust           nvarchar(100);
define o_rms_batch_no   nvarchar(100);
define o_dt_sent        date;
define o_desc           nvarchar(255);
define o_attr_ext_sys   nvarchar(100);
define o_coa1           nvarchar(100);
define o_coa2           nvarchar(100);
define o_branch         nvarchar(100);
define o_qty            int;
define o_sub_acct       nvarchar(100);
define o_txn_desc       nvarchar(100);
define o_unit_price     decimal(16,2);
define o_rcpt_no        nvarchar(30);
define o_payee_info     nvarchar(100);
define o_ent_nm         nvarchar(100);
define o_ent_no         nvarchar(100);
define o_ent_ty         nvarchar(100);
define o_item_amt       decimal(16,2);
define o_pymt_mode      nvarchar(100);
define o_item_tax_amt   decimal(16,2);

foreach c_ari for
    select t1.type,t1.link_branch,t1.amt,t1.cust,t1.rms_batch_no,t1.dt_sent,t1.desc,t1.attr_ext_sys,
            t2.coa1,t2.coa2,t2.branch,t2.qty,t2.sub_acct,t2.txn_desc,t2.unit_price,t2.rcpt_no,
            t2.payee_info,t2.ent_nm,t2.ent_no,t2.ent_ty,t2.item_amt,t2.pymt_mode,t2.item_tax_amt
    into o_type,o_link_branch,o_amt,o_cust,o_rms_batch_no,o_dt_sent,o_desc,o_attr_ext_sys,
            o_coa1,o_coa2,o_branch,o_qty,o_sub_acct,o_txn_desc,o_unit_price,o_rcpt_no,
            o_payee_info,o_ent_nm,o_ent_no,o_ent_ty,o_item_amt,o_pymt_mode,o_item_tax_amt
    from rms_fms_ari_h t1
    inner join rms_fms_ari_b t2 on t1.ari_hid = t2.ari_hid
    where t1.fms_ref_no is null
    or t1.resp_status <> 200

    return o_type,o_link_branch,o_amt,o_cust,o_rms_batch_no,o_dt_sent,o_desc,o_attr_ext_sys,
            o_coa1,o_coa2,o_branch,o_qty,o_sub_acct,o_txn_desc,o_unit_price,o_rcpt_no,
            o_payee_info,o_ent_nm,o_ent_no,o_ent_ty,o_item_amt,o_pymt_mode,o_item_tax_amt with resume;
    
end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsarr()
returning 
	int8 as arr_hid,
	nvarchar(20) as type,
	nvarchar(30) as branch,
	datetime year to second as dt_sent,
	nvarchar(10) as cash_acct, 
	decimal(15,5) as pymt_amt, 
	nvarchar(10) as pymt_method, 
	nvarchar(30) as cust, 
	nvarchar(40) as rms_batch_no,
	nvarchar(15) as fms_ref_no, 
	nvarchar(20) as doc_type_b,
	decimal(15,5) as amt, 
	nvarchar(20) as doc_type_c, 
	nvarchar(20) as entity_type, 
	nvarchar(50) as offset_subacct
;
	
define o_arr_hid int8;
define o_type nvarchar(20);
define o_branch nvarchar(30);
define o_dt_sent datetime year to second;
define o_cash_acct nvarchar(10);
define o_pymt_amt decimal(15,5);
define o_pymt_method nvarchar(10);
define o_cust nvarchar(30);
define o_rms_batch_no nvarchar(40);
define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(15);
define o_doc_type_b nvarchar(20);
define o_amt decimal(15,5);
define o_doc_type_c nvarchar(20);
define o_entity_type nvarchar(20);
define o_offset_subacct nvarchar(50);

foreach c_arr for 
	select 
		t1.arr_hid, t1.type, t1.branch, t1.dt_sent, t1.cash_acct, t1.pymt_amt, t1.pymt_method, t1.cust, t1.rms_batch_no,
		t2.fms_ref_no, t2.doc_type,
		t3.amt, t3.doc_type, t3.entity_type, t3.offset_subacct
	into 
		o_arr_hid,
		o_type,
		o_branch,
		o_dt_sent,
		o_cash_acct,
		o_pymt_amt,
		o_pymt_method,
		o_cust,
		o_rms_batch_no,
		o_fms_ref_no,
		o_doc_type_b,
		o_amt,
		o_doc_type_c,
		o_entity_type,
		o_offset_subacct
	from rms_fms_arr_h t1
		left join rms_fms_arr_b t2 on t1.arr_hid = t2.arr_hid
		left join rms_fms_arr_c t3 on t1.arr_hid = t3.arr_hid
	where t1.fms_ref_no is null 
		and (t1.resp_status!='200' or t1.resp_status is null)
	return 
		o_arr_hid,
		o_type,
		o_branch,
		o_dt_sent,
		o_cash_acct,
		o_pymt_amt,
		o_pymt_method,
		o_cust,
		o_rms_batch_no,
		o_fms_ref_no,
		o_doc_type_b,
		o_amt,
		o_doc_type_c,
		o_entity_type,
		o_offset_subacct
		with resume;
end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
		
create or replace procedure sp_getfmscrmemo()
returning 
    int8 as crmemo_hid,
    nvarchar(20) as type,
    nvarchar(30) as link_branch,
    decimal(15,5) as amt,
    nvarchar(30) as cust,
    nvarchar(40) as rms_batch_no,
    datetime year to second as dt_sent,
    nvarchar(255) as desc,
    nvarchar(255) as attr_ext_sys,
    nvarchar(20) as fms_ref_no,
    nvarchar(20) as doc_ty,
    nvarchar(30) as acct,
    nvarchar(30) as branch,
    int as qty,
    nvarchar(50) as sub_acct,
    nvarchar(255) as txn_desc,
    decimal(15,5) as unit_price,
--    nvarchar(30) as rcpt_no,
--    nvarchar(255) as payee_info,
    nvarchar(50) as ent_nm,
    nvarchar(50) as ent_no,
    nvarchar(20) as ent_ty,
--    decimal(15,5) as item_amt,
--    decimal(15,5) as pymt,
--    decimal(15,5) as item_tax_amt,
    nvarchar(50) as coa1,
    nvarchar(50) as coa2
;

	define o_crmemo_hid int8;
	define o_type nvarchar(20);
	define o_link_branch nvarchar(30);
	define o_amt decimal(15,5);
	define o_cust nvarchar(30);
	define o_rms_batch_no nvarchar(40);
	define o_dt_sent datetime year to second;
	define o_desc nvarchar(255);
	define o_attr_ext_sys nvarchar(255);
	define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_doc_ty nvarchar(20);
	define o_acct nvarchar(30);
	define o_branch nvarchar(30);
	define o_qty int;
	define o_sub_acct nvarchar(50);
	define o_txn_desc nvarchar(255);
	define o_unit_price decimal(15,5);
--	define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(30);
--	define o_payee_info nvarchar(255);
	define o_ent_nm nvarchar(50);
	define o_ent_no nvarchar(50);
	define o_ent_ty nvarchar(20);
--	define o_item_amt decimal(15,5);
--	define o_pymt decimal(15,5);
--	define o_item_tax_amt decimal(15,5);
	define o_coa1 nvarchar(50);
	define o_coa2 nvarchar(50);

	foreach c_crmemo for 
	    select 
	      	t1.crmemo_hid, t1.type, t1.link_branch, t1.amt, t1.cust, t1.rms_batch_no, t1.dt_sent, t1.desc, t1.attr_ext_sys, 
	      	t2.fms_ref_no, t2.doc_ty,
	      	t3.acct, t3.branch, t3.qty, t3.sub_acct, t3.txn_desc, t3.unit_price, t3.ent_nm, t3.ent_no, t3.ent_ty, t3.coa1, t3.coa2
	    into 
	        o_crmemo_hid, o_type, o_link_branch, o_amt, o_cust, o_rms_batch_no, o_dt_sent, o_desc, o_attr_ext_sys, 
	        o_fms_ref_no, o_doc_ty,
	        o_acct, o_branch, o_qty, o_sub_acct, o_txn_desc, o_unit_price, o_ent_nm, o_ent_no, o_ent_ty, o_coa1, o_coa2
	    from rms_fms_crmemo_h t1
	    	left join rms_fms_crmemo_f t2 on t1.crmemo_hid = t2.crmemo_hid
	    	left join rms_fms_crmemo_b t3 on t1.crmemo_hid = t3.crmemo_hid
		where t1.fms_ref_no is null 
			and t1.resp_status <> 200
		return 
		    o_crmemo_hid, o_type, o_link_branch, o_amt, o_cust, o_rms_batch_no, o_dt_sent, o_desc, o_attr_ext_sys, 
		    o_fms_ref_no, o_doc_ty,
		    o_acct, o_branch, o_qty, o_sub_acct, o_txn_desc, o_unit_price, o_ent_nm, o_ent_no, o_ent_ty, o_coa1, o_coa2
		    with resume;
	end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsdia()
returning int8 as audit_id, int8 as di_id, date as dt_txn, decimal(16,2) as bal_di_amt_af, decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, nvarchar(10) as action_type;

define o_audit_id       int8;
define o_di_id          int8;
define o_dt_txn        	date;
define o_bal_di_amt_af 	decimal(16,2);
define o_unit_fee       decimal(16,2);
define o_action_type    nvarchar(10);

    foreach c_dia for

    select t1.audit_id, t1.di_id, t1.dt_txn, t1.bal_di_amt_af, t2.unit_fee, t1.action_type
    into o_audit_id, o_di_id, o_dt_txn, o_bal_di_amt_af, o_unit_fee, o_action_type
	from rms_di_a t1
    left join rms_di t2 on t1.di_id = t2.di_id
    where t1.in_fms_posting = 0
    and (t1.action_type like '%T' or t1.action_type like '%A')
    and t1.dt_txn <= today

    return o_audit_id, o_di_id, o_dt_txn, o_bal_di_amt_af, o_unit_fee, o_action_type with resume;

    end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsdoc(i_fms_id int8)
returning nvarchar(255) as file_nm,

			nvarchar(5) as file_type,
			int as file_size_kb,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			int as total;
			
define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);

define o_file_type nvarchar(5);
define o_file_size_kb int;
define o_dt_created datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define calculatedpage int;
define total int;


let total = (
				select count(1)
				from rms_fms_doc
				where (i_fms_id is null or fms_id = i_fms_id)
