			);

foreach c_getfmsdoc for
	select file_nm, file_type, file_size_kb, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by
	into	o_file_nm, o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by
	from rms_fms_doc
	where (i_fms_id is null or fms_id = i_fms_id)
		order by dt_modified desc
		
	return o_file_nm, o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by, total with resume;
end foreach


end procedure
GO
	   
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsdrmemo()
returning 
    int8 as drmemo_hid,
    nvarchar(20) as type,
    nvarchar(30) as link_branch,
    decimal(15,5) as amt,
    nvarchar(30) as cust,
    nvarchar(40) as rms_batch_no,
    datetime year to second as dt_sent,
    nvarchar(255) as desc,
    nvarchar(255) as attr_ext_sys,
    nvarchar(20) as fms_ref_no,
    nvarchar(20) as doc_ty,
    nvarchar(30) as acct,
    nvarchar(30) as branch,
    int as qty,
    nvarchar(50) as sub_acct,
    nvarchar(255) as txn_desc,
    decimal(15,5) as unit_price,
--    nvarchar(30) as rcpt_no,
--    nvarchar(255) as payee_info,
    nvarchar(50) as ent_nm,
    nvarchar(50) as ent_no,
    nvarchar(20) as ent_ty,
--    decimal(15,5) as item_amt,
--    decimal(15,5) as pymt,
--    decimal(15,5) as item_tax_amt,
    nvarchar(50) as coa1,
    nvarchar(50) as coa2
;

	define o_drmemo_hid int8;
	define o_type nvarchar(20);
	define o_link_branch nvarchar(30);
	define o_amt decimal(15,5);
	define o_cust nvarchar(30);
	define o_rms_batch_no nvarchar(40);
	define o_dt_sent datetime year to second;
	define o_desc nvarchar(255);
	define o_attr_ext_sys nvarchar(255);
	define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_doc_ty nvarchar(20);
	define o_acct nvarchar(30);
	define o_branch nvarchar(30);
	define o_qty int;
	define o_sub_acct nvarchar(50);
	define o_txn_desc nvarchar(255);
	define o_unit_price decimal(15,5);
--	define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(30);
--	define o_payee_info nvarchar(255);
	define o_ent_nm nvarchar(50);
	define o_ent_no nvarchar(50);
	define o_ent_ty nvarchar(20);

--	define o_pymt decimal(15,5);
--	define o_item_tax_amt decimal(15,5);
	define o_coa1 nvarchar(50);
	define o_coa2 nvarchar(50);

	foreach c_drmemo for 
	    select

	    into

	    from rms_fms_drmemo_h t1

		    with resume;
	end foreach;

end procedure;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getfmsfilecontent(i_fms_id int8, i_file_nm VARCHAR(255))
returning blob as file_content;

    -- Declare a variable to store the count of records with the given document name
    DEFINE o_file_content BLOB;

    -- Check if the document name exists in the fms_doc table
    SELECT file_content INTO o_file_content
    FROM rms_fms_doc
    WHERE file_nm = i_file_nm 
    AND fms_id = i_fms_id;

    -- Set the output parameter based on the count
    return o_file_content;
END procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getfmsfilecontent(i_file_nm VARCHAR(255))
returning blob as file_content;

    -- Declare a variable to store the count of records with the given document name
    DEFINE o_file_content BLOB;

    -- Check if the document name exists in the fms_doc table
    SELECT file_content INTO o_file_content
    FROM rms_fms_doc
    WHERE file_nm = i_file_nm;

    -- Set the output parameter based on the count
    return o_file_content;
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsjn()
returning nvarchar(30) as branch_id, lvarchar(256) as desc,  nvarchar(10) as ledger_id,
nvarchar(2) as module, DATE as dt_txn, lvarchar(256) as attr_ext_ref_no,lvarchar(256) as attr_ext_sys,
nvarchar(10) as acct1, nvarchar(30) as branch1, decimal(16,2) as credit1, decimal(16,2) as debit1, nvarchar(30) as sub_acct1, lvarchar(256) as txn_desc1,
nvarchar(10) as acct2, nvarchar(30) as branch2, decimal(16,2) as credit2, decimal(16,2) as debit2, nvarchar(30) as sub_acct2, lvarchar(256) as txn_desc2;

define o_branch_id nvarchar(30); 
define o_desc lvarchar(256);
define o_ledger_id nvarchar(10);
define o_module nvarchar(2);
define o_dt_txn DATE;
define o_attr_ext_ref_no lvarchar(256);
define o_attr_ext_sys lvarchar(256);
define o_acct1 nvarchar(10);
define o_branch1 nvarchar(30);
define o_credit1 decimal(16,2);
define o_debit1  decimal(16,2);
define o_sub_acct1  nvarchar(30);
define o_txn_desc1  lvarchar(256);
define o_acct2 nvarchar(10);
define o_branch2 nvarchar(30);
define o_credit2 decimal(16,2);
define o_debit2 decimal(16,2);
define o_sub_acct2 nvarchar(30);
define o_txn_desc2 lvarchar(256);

foreach c_getfmsjn for     
    select 
        t1.branch_id, t1.desc, t1.ledger_id, t1.module, t1.dt_txn, t1.attr_ext_ref_no, t1.attr_ext_sys,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then acct end) as acct1,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then branch end) as branch1,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then credit end) as credit1,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then debit end) as debit1,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then sub_acct end) as sub_acct1,
        max(case when row_num = 1 then txn_desc end) as txn_desc1,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then acct end) as acct2,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then branch end) as branch2,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then credit end) as credit2,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then debit end) as debit2,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then sub_acct end) as sub_acct2,
        max(case when row_num = 2 then txn_desc end) as txn_desc2
    into o_branch_id, o_desc, o_ledger_id, o_module, o_dt_txn, o_attr_ext_ref_no, o_attr_ext_sys, 
         o_acct1, o_branch1, o_credit1, o_debit1, o_sub_acct1, o_txn_desc1,
         o_acct2, o_branch2, o_credit2, o_debit2, o_sub_acct2, o_txn_desc2
    from rms_fms_jn_h t1
    join (
        select 
            jn_hid, acct, branch, credit, debit, sub_acct, txn_desc,
            row_number() over (partition by jn_hid order by acct) as row_num
        from rms_fms_jn_b
    ) as t2 on t1.jn_hid = t2.jn_hid
    where t1.fms_ref_no is null
    and (resp_status <> 200 or resp_status is null)
    group by t2.jn_hid, t1.branch_id, t1.desc, t1.ledger_id, t1.module, t1.dt_txn, t1.attr_ext_ref_no, t1.attr_ext_sys
    order by t2.jn_hid
    
    return o_branch_id, o_desc, o_ledger_id, o_module, o_dt_txn, o_attr_ext_ref_no, o_attr_ext_sys, 
           o_acct1, o_branch1, o_credit1, o_debit1, o_sub_acct1, o_txn_desc1,
           o_acct2, o_branch2, o_credit2, o_debit2, o_sub_acct2, o_txn_desc2 with resume;

end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsledger_v2(
    i_page INTEGER,
    i_size INTEGER,
    i_fms_id INTEGER,
    i_file_index INTEGER,
    i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR (10),
    i_fee_detail_nm_en NVARCHAR (100),
    i_fms_ledger_cd NVARCHAR(50),
    i_found NVARCHAR(2)
)
RETURNING
    NVARCHAR(50) AS fms_ledger_cd,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS fee_detail_id,
    NVARCHAR(100) AS fee_detail_nm_en,
    NVARCHAR(2) AS found,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS fms_cd,
    INTEGER AS mft_total,
    INTEGER AS total;

DEFINE o_fms_ledger_cd NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_en NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_found NVARCHAR(2);
DEFINE o_fms_cd NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE total INTEGER;
DEFINE calculatedpage INT;
DEFINE o_mft_total INTEGER;

IF (i_page IS NULL OR i_page < 1) OR (i_size IS NULL OR i_size < 1) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null or less than 1";
END IF;

-- Calculate total count
LET total = (SELECT COUNT(1)
             FROM rms_fms_ledger t1
             WHERE (i_fms_id IS NULL OR t1.fms_id = i_fms_id)
               AND (i_file_index IS NULL OR t1.file_index = i_file_index)
               AND (i_fee_detail_id IS NULL OR t1.fee_detail_id LIKE '%' || i_fee_detail_id || '%')
               AND (i_fee_detail_nm_en IS NULL OR t1.fee_detail_nm_en LIKE '%' || i_fee_detail_nm_en || '%')
               AND (i_fms_ledger_cd IS NULL OR t1.fms_ledger_cd LIKE '%' || i_fms_ledger_cd || '%')
               AND (i_found IS NULL OR i_found = t1.found)
                AND (t1.status = 'A'));

LET calculatedpage = (i_page - 1) * i_size;

LET o_mft_total = (SELECT COUNT(1) FROM rms_mft);

FOREACH c_getfmsledger FOR
        SELECT SKIP calculatedpage LIMIT i_size
            t1.fms_ledger_cd, 
            t1.fee_detail_id, 
            t1.fee_detail_nm_en,
            t3.fms_cd,
            t1.found
        INTO o_fms_ledger_cd, 
             o_fee_detail_id, 
             o_fee_detail_nm_en,
             o_fms_cd,
             o_found
FROM rms_fms_ledger t1
         LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_fms t3 ON t3.fms_id = t1.fms_id
         LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_fms_doc t2 ON t2.file_index = t1.file_index
         LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_mft t4 ON t4.fee_detail_id = t1.fee_detail_id
WHERE (i_fms_id IS NULL OR t1.fms_id = i_fms_id)
  AND (i_file_index IS NULL OR t1.file_index = i_file_index)
  AND (i_fee_detail_id IS NULL OR t1.fee_detail_id LIKE '%' || i_fee_detail_id || '%')
  AND (i_fee_detail_nm_en IS NULL OR t1.fee_detail_nm_en LIKE '%' || i_fee_detail_nm_en || '%')
  AND (i_fms_ledger_cd IS NULL OR t1.fms_ledger_cd LIKE '%' || i_fms_ledger_cd || '%')
  AND (i_found IS NULL OR i_found= t1.found )
  AND (t1.status = 'A')
ORDER BY t1.fee_detail_id

RETURN 
       o_fms_ledger_cd,
       o_fee_detail_id,
       o_fee_detail_nm_en,
       o_found,
       o_fms_cd,
       o_mft_total,
       total WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsmtt()
returning int8 as mtt_pg_id, decimal(16,2) as pg_pymt_amt, int as qty, nvarchar(100) as item_desc,
            decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, nvarchar(100) as rcpt_no, nvarchar(100) as cust_nm, nvarchar(100) as entity_nm, nvarchar(100) as entity_no,
            nvarchar(100) as entity_type, decimal(16,2) as gross_amt, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_id, nvarchar(100) as pg_pymt_method,
            decimal(16,2) as tax_amt,nvarchar(100) as customer,nvarchar(100) as item_ref_no, nvarchar(100) as cp_no;

define o_mtt_pg_id int8;
define o_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_qty int;
define o_item_desc nvarchar(250);
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(30);
define o_cust_nm nvarchar(250);
define o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
define o_entity_no nvarchar(100);
define o_entity_type nvarchar(1);
define o_gross_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(100);
define o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(50);
define o_tax_amt decimal(16,2);

define o_product nvarchar(100);
define o_coa1 nvarchar(100);
define o_customer nvarchar(100);
define o_item_ref_no nvarchar(100);
define o_cp_no nvarchar(100);

define ari_limit nvarchar(100);
define temp_date date;

    -- get limit per payment
    select config_value
    into ari_limit
    from rms_config
    where config_cd = 'FMS_ARI_Details';

    -- filter in rms_fms_arrb's mtt record
    -- get the most earliest date
    select min(date(pg_resp_time)) as resp_time
    into temp_date
    from rms_mtt_pg
    where (in_fms_posting = 0 or in_fms_posting is null)
    and pg_txn_status=0
    and date(pg_resp_time) <= today-1;

    -- customer field
    select acct_cd
    into o_customer
    from rms_fms_acct
    where acct_nm ="AR Invoice's RMS PG MID Account ID";

foreach c_ari for
    -- filter out the limit
    SELECT t1.mtt_pg_id,
       t1.pg_pymt_amt,
       t2.qty,
       t2.item_desc,
       t2.unit_fee,
       t4.rcpt_no,
       t3.cust_nm,
       t2.entity_nm,
       t2.entity_no,
       t2.entity_type,
       t2.gross_amt,
       t2.fee_detail_id,
       t1.pg_pymt_method,
       t2.tax_amt,
       t2.item_ref_no,
       t2.cp_no
    into o_mtt_pg_id,o_pg_pymt_amt,o_qty,o_item_desc,o_unit_fee,o_rcpt_no,o_cust_nm,o_entity_nm,o_entity_no,o_entity_type
        ,o_gross_amt,o_fee_detail_id,o_pg_pymt_method,o_tax_amt,o_item_ref_no,o_cp_no
    FROM (
        SELECT FIRST ari_limit
            mtt_pg_id,
            mtt_id,
            pg_pymt_amt,
            pg_pymt_method,
            pg_resp_time
        FROM rms_mtt_pg
        WHERE DATE(pg_resp_time) = temp_date
          AND (in_fms_posting = 0 OR in_fms_posting IS NULL)
          AND pg_txn_status = 0
        ORDER BY pg_resp_time
    ) t1
    INNER JOIN rms_mtt_item t2 ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
    INNER JOIN rms_mtt t3 ON t1.mtt_id = t3.mtt_id
    LEFT JOIN rms_mtt_rcpt t4 ON t1.mtt_pg_id = t4.mtt_pg_id
    ORDER BY t1.pg_resp_time

    return o_mtt_pg_id,o_pg_pymt_amt,o_qty,o_item_desc,o_unit_fee,o_rcpt_no,o_cust_nm,o_entity_nm,o_entity_no,o_entity_type
    ,o_gross_amt,o_fee_detail_id,o_pg_pymt_method,o_tax_amt,o_customer,o_item_ref_no,o_cp_no with resume;

end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsrcbank()
returning 
    int8 as rc_bank_id,
    int8 as rc_pg_id,
    decimal(16,2) as credit,
    decimal(16,2) as mdr_amt,
    int8 as mtt_pg_id,
    nvarchar(10) as acct_cd,
    nvarchar(10) as cust;

define o_rc_bank_id int8;
define o_rc_pg_id int8;
define o_credit decimal(16,2);
define o_mdr_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_mtt_pg_id int8;
define o_acct_cd nvarchar(10);
define o_cust nvarchar(10);

let o_acct_cd = (select first 1 acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'AR Receipt''s Cash Account');
let o_cust = (select first 1 acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'AR Invoice''s RMS PG MID Account ID');

foreach c_arr for

   select 
    p1.rc_bank_id, 
    p1.rc_pg_id, 
    sum(p1.credit) over() as total_credit,
    p1.mdr_amt, 
    p1.mtt_pg_id
    into o_rc_bank_id, o_rc_pg_id, o_credit, o_mdr_amt, o_mtt_pg_id
    from
    (
        select 
            t1.rc_bank_id, 
            t1.rc_pg_id, 
            t2.credit, 
            t3.mdr_amt, 
            t4.mtt_pg_id
        from rms_rc_bank t1
        left join rms_rc_banktxn t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
        left join rms_rc_pgtxn t3 on t3.rc_pg_id = t1.rc_pg_id
        left join rms_mtt_pg t4 on t3.mtt_pg_id = t4.mtt_pg_id
        where (t1.in_fms_posting = 0 or t1.in_fms_posting is null)
        and t1.dt_created < today
        and t1.recon_status = 'SBSR'
        and t4.mtt_pg_id is not null
        group by t1.rc_bank_id, t1.rc_pg_id, t2.credit, t3.mdr_amt, t4.mtt_pg_id
        order by t4.mtt_pg_id
    ) p1
    order by p1.mtt_pg_id

    return o_rc_bank_id, o_rc_pg_id, o_credit, o_mdr_amt, o_mtt_pg_id, o_acct_cd, o_cust with resume;
end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
		
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getfmsrcpgmtt()
RETURNING  
    int8 AS rc_pg_id,
    nvarchar(3) as pg_pymt_method,
    int8 as mtt_pg_id,
    int as qty,
    nvarchar(150) as item_desc,
    decimal(16,2) as unit_fee,
    nvarchar(100) as entity_nm,
    nvarchar(20) as entity_no,
    nvarchar(1) as entity_type,
    decimal(16,2) as gross_amt,
    nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id,
    decimal(16,2) as tax_amt,
    nvarchar(20) as rcpt_no,
    nvarchar(255) as cust_nm,
    decimal(16,2) as pg_pymt_amt;

   	define o_mtt_pg_id int8;
    define o_rc_pg_id INT8;
	define o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(3);
	define o_qty int;
	define o_item_desc nvarchar(150);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
	define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_entity_type nvarchar(1);
	define o_gross_amt decimal(16,2);
	define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_tax_amt decimal(16,2);
	define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_cust_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2);

				  
									   
				   
	   
																										
																			 
																					   
					  
																		   
															   
														
														
												   
								   
									  
							   
																 
					
   
    FOREACH c_arr for
        SELECT 
		    t1.rc_pg_id,
		    t2.pg_pymt_method,
		    t2.mtt_pg_id,
		    t4.qty, 
		    t4.item_desc, 
		    t4.unit_fee, 
		    t4.entity_nm, 
		    t4.entity_no,
		    t4.entity_type, 
		    t4.gross_amt, 
		    t4.fee_detail_id, 
		    t4.tax_amt,
		    t5.rcpt_no, 
		    t6.cust_nm,
		    SUM(t2.pg_pymt_amt) AS pg_pymt_amt
        INTO 
            o_rc_pg_id, 
            o_pg_pymt_method, 
            o_mtt_pg_id,
            o_qty,
            o_item_desc,
            o_unit_fee,
            o_entity_nm,
            o_entity_no,
            o_entity_type,
            o_gross_amt,
            o_fee_detail_id,
            o_tax_amt,
            o_rcpt_no,
            o_cust_nm,
            o_pg_pymt_amt
        FROM 
            rms_rc_pg t1
        left join 
        	rms_mtt_pg t2 on t1.dt_settlement = date(t2.pymt_submit_dt)
        inner join 
        	rms_rc_pgmtt t3 on t2.mtt_pg_id =t3.mtt_pg_id 
        INNER JOIN 
        	rms_mtt_item t4 on t2.mtt_id = t4.mtt_id
        left JOIN 
        	rms_mtt_rcpt t5 on t2.mtt_id = t5.mtt_id
        INNER JOIN 
        	rms_mtt t6 on t2.mtt_id = t6.mtt_id
        WHERE 
            t1.dt_settlement < TODAY
            AND t1.recon_status = 'SSSCR'
            AND t3.found_in_pg = 0
            and (t3.in_fms_posting = 0 or t3.in_fms_posting is null)
        GROUP BY 
		    t1.rc_pg_id,
		    t2.pg_pymt_method,
		    t2.mtt_pg_id,
		    t4.qty, 
		    t4.item_desc, 
		    t4.unit_fee, 
		    t4.entity_nm, 
		    t4.entity_no,
		    t4.entity_type, 
		    t4.gross_amt, 
		    t4.fee_detail_id, 
		    t4.tax_amt,
		    t5.rcpt_no, 
		    t6.cust_nm
        ORDER BY 
            t1.rc_pg_id
           
        RETURN 
            o_rc_pg_id, 
            o_pg_pymt_method, 
            o_mtt_pg_id,
            o_qty,
            o_item_desc,
            o_unit_fee,
            o_entity_nm,
            o_entity_no,
            o_entity_type,
            o_gross_amt,
            o_fee_detail_id,
            o_tax_amt,
            o_rcpt_no,
            o_cust_nm,
            o_pg_pymt_amt
			WITH RESUME;
    END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
	   
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getfmsrcpgtxn()
RETURNING  
    int8 AS rc_pg_id,
    nvarchar(3) as pg_pymt_method,
    int8 as mtt_pg_id,
    int as qty,
    nvarchar(150) as item_desc,
    decimal(16,2) as unit_fee,
    nvarchar(100) as entity_nm,
    nvarchar(20) as entity_no,
    nvarchar(1) as entity_type,
    decimal(16,2) as gross_amt,
    nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id,
    decimal(16,2) as tax_amt,
    nvarchar(20) as rcpt_no,
    nvarchar(255) as cust_nm,
    decimal(16,2) as pg_pymt_amt;

   	define o_mtt_pg_id int8;
    define o_rc_pg_id INT8;
	define o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(3);
	define o_qty int;
	define o_item_desc nvarchar(150);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
	define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_entity_type nvarchar(1);
	define o_gross_amt decimal(16,2);
	define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_tax_amt decimal(16,2);
	define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_cust_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2);

									   
				   
	   
				 
				   
						 
					  
					
			   
					 
					
					 
					
					   
					 
						 
				  
				   
				 
			  
						 
					
														 
					
													
					
												  
					
												  
					
											 
			   
									 
										  
								   
																	 
		
   
    FOREACH c_arr for
        SELECT 
		    t1.rc_pg_id,
		    t3.pg_pymt_method,
		    t3.mtt_pg_id,
		    t4.qty, 
		    t4.item_desc, 
		    t4.unit_fee, 
		    t4.entity_nm, 
		    t4.entity_no,
		    t4.entity_type, 
		    t4.gross_amt, 
		    t4.fee_detail_id, 
		    t4.tax_amt,
		    t5.rcpt_no, 
		    t6.cust_nm,
		    SUM(t3.pg_pymt_amt) AS pg_pymt_amt
        INTO 
            o_rc_pg_id, 
            o_pg_pymt_method, 
            o_mtt_pg_id,
            o_qty,
            o_item_desc,
            o_unit_fee,
            o_entity_nm,
            o_entity_no,
            o_entity_type,
            o_gross_amt,
            o_fee_detail_id,
            o_tax_amt,
            o_rcpt_no,
            o_cust_nm,
            o_pg_pymt_amt
        FROM 
            rms_rc_pg t1
        INNER JOIN 
            rms_rc_pgtxn t2 ON t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
        INNER JOIN 
            rms_mtt_pg t3 ON t2.mtt_pg_id = t3.mtt_pg_id
        INNER JOIN 
        	rms_mtt_item t4 on t3.mtt_id = t4.mtt_id
        INNER JOIN 
        	rms_mtt_rcpt t5 on t3.mtt_id = t5.mtt_id
        INNER JOIN 
        	rms_mtt t6 on t3.mtt_id = t6.mtt_id
        WHERE 
            t1.dt_created < TODAY
            AND t1.recon_status = 'SSSCR'
								  
            AND (t2.in_fms_posting = 0 or t2.in_fms_posting is null)
        GROUP BY 
		    t1.rc_pg_id,
		    t3.pg_pymt_method,
		    t3.mtt_pg_id,
		    t4.qty, 
		    t4.item_desc, 
		    t4.unit_fee, 
		    t4.entity_nm, 
		    t4.entity_no,
		    t4.entity_type, 
		    t4.gross_amt, 
		    t4.fee_detail_id, 
		    t4.tax_amt,
		    t5.rcpt_no, 
		    t6.cust_nm
        ORDER BY 
            t1.rc_pg_id
           
        RETURN 
            o_rc_pg_id, 
            o_pg_pymt_method, 
            o_mtt_pg_id,
            o_qty,
            o_item_desc,
            o_unit_fee,
            o_entity_nm,
            o_entity_no,
            o_entity_type,
            o_gross_amt,
            o_fee_detail_id,
            o_tax_amt,
            o_rcpt_no,
            o_cust_nm,
            o_pg_pymt_amt
			WITH RESUME;
    END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsricpa()
returning int8 as audit_id,
int8 as ricp_id,
date as dt_txn,
decimal(16,2) as accr_amt_af,
nvarchar(10) as action_type;

define o_audit_id int8;

define o_ricp_id int8;

define o_dt_txn date;

define o_accr_amt_af decimal(16,2);

define o_action_type nvarchar(10);

foreach c_dia for
    select
	t1.audit_id,
	t1.ricp_id,
	t1.dt_txn,
	t1.accr_amt_af,
	t1.action_type
    into
	o_audit_id,
	o_ricp_id,
	o_dt_txn,
	o_accr_amt_af,
	o_action_type
from
	rms_ricp_a t1
where
	(t1.in_fms_posting = 0
		or t1.in_fms_posting is null)
	and t1.dt_txn <= today
	and ( t1.action_type like '%I'
		or t1.action_type like '%WO'
		or t1.action_type like '%C'
		or t1.action_type like '%V')

    return o_audit_id,
	o_ricp_id,
	o_dt_txn,
	o_accr_amt_af,
	o_action_type with resume;
end foreach;
end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfmsripla()
returning int8 as audit_id,
int8 as ripl_id,
date as dt_txn,
decimal(16,2) as accr_amt_af,
nvarchar(10) as action_type;

define o_audit_id int8;

define o_ripl_id int8;

define o_dt_txn date;

define o_accr_amt_af decimal(16,2);

define o_action_type nvarchar(10);

foreach c_dia for
    select
	t1.audit_id,
	t1.ripl_id,
	t1.dt_txn,
	t1.accr_amt_af,
	t1.action_type
    into
	o_audit_id,
	o_ripl_id,
	o_dt_txn,
	o_accr_amt_af,
	o_action_type
from
	rms_ripl_a t1
where
	(t1.in_fms_posting = 0
		or t1.in_fms_posting is null)
	and t1.dt_txn <= today
	and ( t1.action_type like '%R'
		or t1.action_type like '%RP'
		or t1.action_type like '%I'
		or t1.action_type like '%WO')

    return o_audit_id,
	o_ripl_id,
	o_dt_txn,
	o_accr_amt_af,
	o_action_type with resume;
end foreach;
end procedure;

create or replace procedure sp_getfullricpidsbycpno (i_cp_no nvarchar(20), i_status nvarchar(10))
returning integer as ricp_id, nvarchar(20) as txn_type, nvarchar(1) as entity_type,nvarchar(20) as entity_no, nvarchar(5) as calendar_yr,
nvarchar(20) as cp_no, nvarchar(20) as cp_act_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sect_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sub_sect_id, date as dt_issuance, date as dt_expiry,
date as dt_void, date as dt_cancel, date as dt_writeoff, decimal as cp_amt, decimal as accr_amt, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as cp_tier, decimal as cp_tier_amt;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_txn_type nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_entity_type nvarchar(1); 
	DEFINE o_entity_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_calendar_yr nvarchar(5); 
	DEFINE o_cp_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_act_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_dt_issuance date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_expiry date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_void date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_cancel date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_writeoff date; 
	DEFINE o_cp_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_accr_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10); 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier integer; 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier_amt decimal;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id,txn_type,entity_type,entity_no,calendar_yr,cp_no,cp_act_id,cp_sect_id,cp_sub_sect_id,dt_issuance,
		dt_expiry,dt_void,dt_cancel,dt_writeoff,cp_amt,accr_amt,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,cp_tier,
		cp_tier_amt
		INTO o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt
		FROM rms_ricp WHERE status = i_status and cp_no=i_cp_no
   		
		RETURN o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getfullricpidsbyfilter (i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_no nvarchar(20), i_status nvarchar(10))
returning integer as ricp_id, nvarchar(20) as txn_type, nvarchar(1) as entity_type,nvarchar(20) as entity_no, nvarchar(5) as calendar_yr,
nvarchar(20) as cp_no, nvarchar(20) as cp_act_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sect_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sub_sect_id, date as dt_issuance, date as dt_expiry,
date as dt_void, date as dt_cancel, date as dt_writeoff, decimal as cp_amt, decimal as accr_amt, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as cp_tier, decimal as cp_tier_amt;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_txn_type nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_entity_type nvarchar(1); 
	DEFINE o_entity_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_calendar_yr nvarchar(5); 
	DEFINE o_cp_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_act_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_dt_issuance date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_expiry date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_void date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_cancel date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_writeoff date; 
	DEFINE o_cp_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_accr_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10); 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier integer; 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier_amt decimal;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id,txn_type,entity_type,entity_no,calendar_yr,cp_no,cp_act_id,cp_sect_id,cp_sub_sect_id,dt_issuance,
		dt_expiry,dt_void,dt_cancel,dt_writeoff,cp_amt,accr_amt,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,cp_tier,
		cp_tier_amt
		INTO o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt
		FROM rms_ricp WHERE status = i_status and entity_type=i_entity_type and entity_no=i_entity_no and cp_no=i_cp_no
   		
		RETURN o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getMasterFeeTable(i_page INTEGER,i_size INTEGER	)
returning integer as fee_detail_pk, nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id, integer as fee_grp_id, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_en, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_bm, 
        decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, date as promo_startdt, date as promo_enddt, decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
        integer as tax_cd_id, integer as  allow_otc, nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, integer as ll_start_day, integer as ll_start_mth, 
		integer as ll_end_day, integer as ll_end_mth, nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, nvarchar(100) as ss_cd, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_fee_detail_pk integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_promo_startdt date;
	define o_promo_enddt date;
	define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_tax_cd_id integer;
	define o_allow_otc integer;
	define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_ll_start_day integer;
	define o_ll_start_mth integer;
	define o_ll_end_day integer;
	define o_ll_end_mth integer;
	define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
	define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define calculatedPage integer;
	define total integer;

	let calculatedPage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
    let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_mft
        WHERE status = 'A');

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT skip calculatedPage limit i_size fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_en, fee_detail_nm_bm, unit_fee, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
        tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd, dt_created, dt_modified,
        created_by, modified_by, status
        INTO o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status 
        FROM rms_mft 

		
		RETURN o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, total WITH RESUME;
       
	END foreach
end procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getMasterFeeTableWFWithFilter (i_wf_id integer, i_status nvarchar(10), i_assign_to nvarchar(100))
returning integer as wf_id, integer as fee_detail_pk, integer as fee_grp_id, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_en, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_bm, 
          decimal(16,2) as fee_amt, date as promo_startdt, date as promo_enddt, decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
          nvarchar(10) as tax_cd, integer as  allow_otc, nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, integer as ll_start_day, integer as ll_start_mth, 
		  integer as ll_end_day, integer as ll_end_mth, nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, nvarchar(100) as ss_cd, date as effective_date, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		  datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as row_count;

		DEFINE o_wf_id integer;
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_pk integer;
		DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100);
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100);
		define o_fee_amt decimal(16,2);
		define o_promo_startdt date;
		define o_promo_enddt date;
		define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
		define o_tax_cd nvarchar(10);
		define o_allow_otc integer;
		define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
		define o_ll_start_day integer;
		define o_ll_start_mth integer;
		define o_ll_end_day integer;
		define o_ll_end_mth integer;
		define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
		define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	    define o_effective_date date;
		define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
		define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
		define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
		define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
		define o_status nvarchar(10);
		Define row_count integer;

	
	 select t0.wf_id, t0.fee_detail_pk, t0.fee_grp_id, t0.fee_detail_nm_en, t0.fee_detail_nm_bm, t0.fee_amt, t0.promo_startdt, t0.promo_enddt, t0.promo_fee,
     t0.tax_cd, t0.allow_otc, t0.ll_parent_id, t0.ll_start_day, t0.ll_start_mth, t0.ll_end_day, t0.ll_end_mth, t0.ledger_cd, t0.ss_cd, t0.effective_date, t0.dt_created, t0.dt_modified,
     t0.created_by, t0.modified_by, t0.status 
     INTO o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_fee_amt, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
     o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_effective_date, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
     o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status 
     from rms_mft_wf as t0 inner join rms_mft_wfhist as t1 on t0.wf_id=t1.wf_id
     where t0.wf_id=i_wf_id and t0.status=i_status and t1.assign_to=i_assign_to limit 1;


	select count(1) into row_count from rms_mft_wf where wf_id=i_wf_id;


	
		RETURN o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_fee_amt, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_effective_date, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, row_count;

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmasterfeetablewithfilter(i_fee_detail_pk INTEGER)
returning integer as fee_detail_pk, nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id, integer as fee_grp_id, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_e, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_b, 
        decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, date as promo_startdt, date as promo_enddt, decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
        integer as tax_cd_id, integer as  allow_otc, nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, integer as ll_start_day, integer as ll_start_mth, 
		integer as ll_end_day, integer as ll_end_mth, nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, nvarchar(100) as ss_cd, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status;

	DEFINE o_fee_detail_pk integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_e nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_b nvarchar(100);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_promo_startdt date;
	define o_promo_enddt date;
	define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_tax_cd_id integer;
	define o_allow_otc integer;
	define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_ll_start_day integer;
	define o_ll_start_mth integer;
	define o_ll_end_day integer;
	define o_ll_end_mth integer;
	define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
	define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_e, fee_detail_nm_b, unit_fee, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
        tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd, dt_created, dt_modified,
        created_by, modified_by, status
        INTO o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_e, o_fee_detail_nm_b, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status 
        FROM rms_mft where fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk

		
		RETURN o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_e, o_fee_detail_nm_b, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status WITH RESUME;
       
	END foreach
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmft(i_page int, i_size int,i_fee_detail_pk int, i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_unit_fee_fr decimal, i_unit_fee_to decimal, i_ss_cd nvarchar(100), i_tax_cd nvarchar(10),
                           i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_modified_by nvarchar(25),
                           i_status nvarchar(10))
returning int as fee_detail_pk,
                            nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id,
                            int as fee_grp_id,
                            nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,
                            nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
                            nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_e,
                            nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_b,
                            decimal(16,2) as unit_fee,
                            date as promo_start_dt,
                            date as promo_end_dt,
                            decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
                            int as tax_cd_id,
                            nvarchar(10) as tax_cd,
                            int as allow_otc,
                            nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id,
                            int as ll_start_day,
                            int as ll_end_day,
                            int as ll_start_mth,
                            int as ll_end_mth,
                            nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd,
                            nvarchar(100) as ss_cd,
                            datetime year to second as dt_modified,
                            datetime year to second as dt_created,
                            nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
                            nvarchar(25) as created_by,
                            nvarchar(255) as modified_by_nm,
                            nvarchar(255) as created_by_nm,
                            nvarchar(10) as status,
                            int as total;
                            
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
define o_fee_grp_id int;
define o_fee_grp_nm_en nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_grp_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_detail_e  nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_detail_b  nvarchar(100);
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_promo_start_dt date;
define o_promo_end_dt date;
define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_tax_cd_id int;
define o_tax_cd nvarchar(10);
define o_allow_otc int;
define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
define o_ll_start_day int;
define o_ll_end_day int;
define o_ll_start_mth int;
define o_ll_end_mth int;
define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
define o_ss_cd  nvarchar(100);
define o_dt_modified  datetime year to second;
define o_dt_created datetime year to second;
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_created_by_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_status nvarchar(10);
define calculatedpage integer;
define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (
                        select count(1)
                        from rms_mft t1
                        left outer join rms_fee_group t2 on t1.fee_grp_id = t2.fee_grp_id
                        left outer join rms_tax_code t3 on t1.tax_cd_id = t3.tax_cd_id
                        left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.modified_by = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
                        left outer join rms_user t5 on t1.created_by = t5.ssm4uuserrefno
                        where (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
                        and (i_unit_fee_fr is null or t1.unit_fee >= i_unit_fee_fr)
                        and (i_unit_fee_to is null or t1.unit_fee <= i_unit_fee_to)
                        --and (i_ss_cd is null or t1.ss_cd = i_ss_cd)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
                        and (i_tax_cd is null or t3.tax_cd = i_tax_cd)
                        and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t4.ssm4uuserrefno like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
        				and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
                        and (i_status is null or t1.status like '%' || i_status || '%')
);

foreach c_getmft for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.fee_detail_pk, t1.fee_detail_id, t1.fee_grp_id, t2.fee_grp_nm_en, t2.fee_grp_nm_bm, t1.fee_detail_nm_e, t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
	                t1.unit_fee, t1.promo_startdt, t1.promo_enddt, t1.promo_fee, t1.tax_cd_id, t3.tax_cd, t1.allow_otc, t1.ll_parent_id,
	                t1.ll_start_day, t1.ll_start_mth, t1.ll_end_day, t1.ll_end_mth, t1.ledger_cd, t1.ss_cd, t1.dt_modified, t1.dt_created, t1.modified_by, t1.created_by, t4.nm, t5.nm ,t1.status
	 into o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_fee_detail_e, o_fee_detail_b,
	            o_unit_fee, o_promo_start_dt, o_promo_end_dt, o_promo_fee, o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id,
	            o_ll_start_day, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_modified, o_dt_created, o_modified_by, o_created_by, o_modified_by_nm, o_created_by_nm,
	            o_status
	 from rms_mft t1
     left outer join rms_fee_group t2 on t1.fee_grp_id = t2.fee_grp_id
     left outer join rms_tax_code t3 on t1.tax_cd_id = t3.tax_cd_id
     left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.modified_by = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
     left outer join rms_user t5 on t1.created_by = t5.ssm4uuserrefno
     where (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
    -- and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id)
     and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
     and (i_unit_fee_fr is null or t1.unit_fee >= i_unit_fee_fr)
     and (i_unit_fee_to is null or t1.unit_fee <= i_unit_fee_to)
    -- and (i_ss_cd is null or t1.ss_cd = i_ss_cd)
     and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
     and (i_tax_cd is null or t3.tax_cd = i_tax_cd)
    -- and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t4.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
     and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t4.ssm4uuserrefno like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
     and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
     and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)     
     and (i_status is null or t1.status like '%' || i_status || '%')
order by t1.dt_modified desc,t1.fee_detail_id

    return o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_grp_nm_en, o_fee_grp_nm_bm, o_fee_detail_e, o_fee_detail_b,
	            o_unit_fee, o_promo_start_dt, o_promo_end_dt, o_promo_fee, o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id,
	            o_ll_start_day, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_modified, o_dt_created, o_modified_by,o_created_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_created_by_nm, o_status, total with resume;
end foreach


end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getMFTDetail(i_fee_detail_pk INTEGER)
returning integer as fee_detail_pk, nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id, integer as fee_grp_id, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_en, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_bm, 
        decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, date as promo_startdt, date as promo_enddt, decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
        integer as tax_cd_id, integer as  allow_otc, nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, integer as ll_start_day, integer as ll_start_mth, 
		integer as ll_end_day, integer as ll_end_mth, nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, nvarchar(100) as ss_cd, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_fee_detail_pk integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100);
	define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_promo_startdt date;
	define o_promo_enddt date;
	define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
	define o_tax_cd_id integer;
	define o_allow_otc integer;
	define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
	define o_ll_start_day integer;
	define o_ll_start_mth integer;
	define o_ll_end_day integer;
	define o_ll_end_mth integer;
	define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
	define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define total integer;

    let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_mft
        WHERE  fee_detail_pk=i_fee_detail_pk);

	
        SELECT  fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_en, fee_detail_nm_bm, unit_fee, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
        tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd, dt_created, dt_modified,
        created_by, modified_by, status
        INTO o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status 
        FROM rms_mft WHERE  fee_detail_pk=i_fee_detail_pk;

		
		RETURN o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_en, o_fee_detail_nm_bm, o_unit_fee, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
        o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, total;
       

end procedure
GO

remarks:
mftwf - master table fee workflow
