create or replace procedure sp_getmftwf(i_page int, i_size int, i_wf_id int8, i_fee_detail_pk int, i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_assign_to nvarchar(25),i_status nvarchar(10),
								i_created_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by_nm nvarchar(50),
								i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second,
								i_dt_created_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_created_to datetime year to second,
								i_dt_effective_fr date, i_dt_effective_to date, 
								i_ss_cd nvarchar(100), i_wf_is_in_prg nvarchar(2))
returning	int8 as wf_id,
			int as fee_detail_pk,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_id,
			int as fee_grp_id,
			nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,
			nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_e,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_b,
			decimal(16,2) as fee_amt,
			date as promo_startdt,
			date as promo_enddt,
			decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
			int as tax_cd_id,
			nvarchar(10) as tax_cd,
			int as allow_otc,
			nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id,
			int as ll_start_day,
			int as ll_end_day,
			int as ll_start_mth,
			int as ll_end_mth,
			nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd,
			nvarchar(100) as ss_cd,
			nvarchar(50) as ss_nm,
			date as effective_date,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(50) as created_by_nm,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(50) as modified_by_nm,
			nvarchar(10) as status,
			nvarchar(50) as status_en,
			nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
			nvarchar(25) as assign_to,
			nvarchar(50) as assign_to_nm,
			nvarchar(50) as action,
			nvarchar(100) as r_fee_det_nm,
			decimal(16,2) as r_fee_amt,
			nvarchar(100) as r_ss_cd,
			date as r_promo_startdt,
			date as r_promo_enddt,
			int as r_ll_required,
			lvarchar(500) as r_add_notes,
			nvarchar(10) as mft_status,
			decimal(16,2) as r_promo_fee,
			nvarchar(10) as task_id,
			int as total;	
			
define o_wf_id 				int8;
define o_fee_detail_pk      int;
define o_fee_detail_id 		nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_grp_id			int;
define o_fee_grp_nm_en		nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_grp_nm_bm		nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_detail_nm_e	nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_detail_nm_b	nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_amt 			decimal(16,2);
define o_promo_startdt		date;
define o_promo_enddt		date;
define o_promo_fee			decimal(16,2);
define o_tax_cd_id			int;
define o_tax_cd				nvarchar(10);
define o_allow_otc			int;
define o_ll_parent_id		nvarchar(10);
define o_ll_start_day		int;
define o_ll_end_day			int;
define o_ll_start_mth		int;
define o_ll_end_mth			int;
define o_ledger_cd			nvarchar(50);
define o_ss_cd				nvarchar(100);
define o_ss_nm          	nvarchar(50);
define o_effective_date		date;
define o_dt_created			datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified		datetime year to second;
define o_created_by			nvarchar(25);
define o_created_by_nm 		nvarchar(50);
define o_modified_by		nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by_nm		nvarchar(50);
define o_status				nvarchar(10);
define o_status_en			nvarchar(50);
define o_status_bm			nvarchar(50);
define o_assign_to			nvarchar(25);	
define o_assign_to_nm		nvarchar(50);
define o_action				nvarchar(50);
define o_r_fee_det_nm		nvarchar(100);
define o_r_fee_amt			decimal(16,2);
define o_r_ss_cd			nvarchar(100);
define o_r_promo_startdt	date;
define o_r_promo_enddt		date;
define o_r_ll_required		int;
define o_r_add_notes		lvarchar(500);
define o_mft_status			nvarchar(10);
define o_r_promo_fee		decimal(16,2);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
--l for listing, t for in progress only, f for all status
--i_wf_is_in_prg='t' or 'f' is for detail page, i_wf_is_in_prg='lt' or 'lf' is for listing page

if i_wf_is_in_prg = 't' then

    let total = (select count(1)
                    from rms_mft_wf t1
                    left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
                            where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
                            --and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
                            and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                            and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
                            and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
                            and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
                            and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
                            and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
                            and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
                            and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
                            and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
                            and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
                            and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
                            and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
                            and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
                            and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
                    and t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD')
                    );

	foreach c_getmftwf1 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		t1.fee_detail_id,
		t1.fee_grp_id, t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e ,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm,
		t1.effective_date,t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,
		t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.status,t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status,
		t1.r_promo_fee
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm ,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		left outer join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
					    and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
						and (t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD'))
		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
	return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
	o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
	o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,o_effective_date,
	o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
	o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee,
	'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0')  ,total with resume;	
		
	end foreach

elif i_wf_is_in_prg = 'f' then
let total = (select count(1)
					from rms_mft_wf t1
                    join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
					left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
					where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
        		);
				
	foreach c_getmftwf2 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		t1.fee_detail_id,
		t1.fee_grp_id,t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm ,t1.effective_date,
		t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm ,t1.status, t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status,
		t1.r_promo_fee
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
		return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
			o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee,
			'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0'), total with resume;
			
	end foreach	
	
elif i_wf_is_in_prg = 'lt' then
	
	let total = (select count(1)
                    from rms_mft_wf t1
                    left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
                            where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
                            --and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
                            and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                            and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
                            and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
                            and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
                            and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
                            and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
                            and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
                           -- and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
                            and ((t1.fee_detail_id is null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.r_fee_det_nm like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')) 
                            or (t1.fee_detail_id is not null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')))
                            and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
                            and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
                            and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
                            and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
                            and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
                            and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
                    and t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD')
                    );

	foreach c_getmftwf3 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		case when t1.fee_detail_id is null then t1.r_fee_det_nm else t1.fee_detail_id end,
		t1.fee_grp_id, t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e ,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm,
		t1.effective_date,t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,
		t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.status,t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status,
		t1.r_promo_fee
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm ,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		left outer join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
					    and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
				     -- and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
                        and ((t1.fee_detail_id is null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.r_fee_det_nm like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')) 
                        or (t1.fee_detail_id is not null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')))
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
						and (t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD'))

		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
	return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
	o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
	o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,o_effective_date,
	o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
	o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee,
	'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0')  ,total with resume;	
		
	end foreach

else -- i_wf_is_in_prg = 'lf' then

let total = (select count(1)
					from rms_mft_wf t1
                    join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
					left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
					where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						--and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and ((t1.fee_detail_id is null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.r_fee_det_nm like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')) 
                        or (t1.fee_detail_id is not null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')))
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
        		);
				
	foreach c_getmftwf4 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		case when t1.fee_detail_id is null then t1.r_fee_det_nm else t1.fee_detail_id end,
		t1.fee_grp_id,t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm ,t1.effective_date,
		t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm ,t1.status, t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status,
		t1.r_promo_fee
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						--and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and ((t1.fee_detail_id is null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.r_fee_det_nm like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')) 
                        or (t1.fee_detail_id is not null and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')))
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
		return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
			o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status, o_r_promo_fee,
			'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0'), total with resume;
			
	end foreach	
	
end if 

end procedure
GO
/*
remarks:
mftwf - master table fee workflow

*/
create or replace procedure sp_getmftwf_feedetid(i_page int, i_size int, i_wf_id int8, i_fee_detail_pk int, i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_assign_to nvarchar(25),i_status nvarchar(10),
								i_created_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by_nm nvarchar(50),
								i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second,
								i_dt_created_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_created_to datetime year to second,
								i_dt_effective_fr date, i_dt_effective_to date, 
								i_ss_cd nvarchar(100), i_wf_is_in_prg boolean)
returning	int8 as wf_id,
			int as fee_detail_pk,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_id,
			int as fee_grp_id,
			nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_en,
			nvarchar(50) as fee_grp_nm_bm,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_e,
			nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_b,
			decimal(16,2) as fee_amt,
			date as promo_startdt,
			date as promo_enddt,
			decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
			int as tax_cd_id,
			nvarchar(10) as tax_cd,
			int as allow_otc,
			nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id,
			int as ll_start_day,
			int as ll_end_day,
			int as ll_start_mth,
			int as ll_end_mth,
			nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd,
			nvarchar(100) as ss_cd,
			nvarchar(50) as ss_nm,
			date as effective_date,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(50) as created_by_nm,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(50) as modified_by_nm,
			nvarchar(10) as status,
			nvarchar(50) as status_en,
			nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
			nvarchar(25) as assign_to,
			nvarchar(50) as assign_to_nm,
			nvarchar(50) as action,
			nvarchar(100) as r_fee_det_nm,
			decimal(16,2) as r_fee_amt,
			nvarchar(100) as r_ss_cd,
			date as r_promo_startdt,
			date as r_promo_enddt,
			int as r_ll_required,
			nvarchar(255) as r_add_notes,
			nvarchar(10) as mft_status,
			nvarchar(10) as task_id,
			int as total;	
			
define o_wf_id 				int8;
define o_fee_detail_pk      int;
define o_fee_detail_id 		nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_grp_id			int;
define o_fee_grp_nm_en		nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_grp_nm_bm		nvarchar(50);
define o_fee_detail_nm_e	nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_detail_nm_b	nvarchar(100);
define o_fee_amt 			decimal(16,2);
define o_promo_startdt		date;
define o_promo_enddt		date;
define o_promo_fee			decimal(16,2);
define o_tax_cd_id			int;
define o_tax_cd				nvarchar(10);
define o_allow_otc			int;
define o_ll_parent_id		nvarchar(10);
define o_ll_start_day		int;
define o_ll_end_day			int;
define o_ll_start_mth		int;
define o_ll_end_mth			int;
define o_ledger_cd			nvarchar(50);
define o_ss_cd				nvarchar(100);
define o_ss_nm          	nvarchar(50);
define o_effective_date		date;
define o_dt_created			datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified		datetime year to second;
define o_created_by			nvarchar(25);
define o_created_by_nm 		nvarchar(50);
define o_modified_by		nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by_nm		nvarchar(50);
define o_status				nvarchar(10);
define o_status_en			nvarchar(50);
define o_status_bm			nvarchar(50);
define o_assign_to			nvarchar(25);	
define o_assign_to_nm		nvarchar(50);
define o_action				nvarchar(50);
define o_r_fee_det_nm		nvarchar(100);
define o_r_fee_amt			decimal(16,2);
define o_r_ss_cd			nvarchar(100);
define o_r_promo_startdt	date;
define o_r_promo_enddt		date;
define o_r_ll_required		int;
define o_r_add_notes		nvarchar(255);
define o_mft_status			nvarchar(10);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;

if i_wf_is_in_prg = 't' then

    let total = (select count(1)
                    from rms_mft_wf t1
                    left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
                            where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
                            --and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
                            and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                            and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
                            and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
                            and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
                            and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
                            and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
                            and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
                            and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
                            and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
                            and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
                            and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
                            and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
                            and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
                            and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
                    and t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD')
                    );

	foreach c_getmftwf1 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		case when t1.fee_detail_id is null then t1.r_fee_det_nm else t1.fee_detail_id end,
		t1.fee_grp_id, t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e ,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm,
		t1.effective_date,t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,
		t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm, t1.status,t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm ,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		left outer join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
					    and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
						and (t1.status not in ('EFT','C','RJ-RHOD','RJ-FA','RJ-FHOD'))
		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
	return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
	o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
	o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,o_effective_date,
	o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
	o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status,
	'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0')  ,total with resume;	
		
	end foreach

else
let total = (select count(1)
					from rms_mft_wf t1
                    join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
					left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
					where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
        		);
				
	foreach c_getmftwf2 for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.fee_detail_pk, 
		case when t1.fee_detail_id is null then t1.r_fee_det_nm else t1.fee_detail_id end,
		t1.fee_grp_id,t7.fee_grp_nm_en, t7.fee_grp_nm_bm,t1.fee_detail_nm_e,t1.fee_detail_nm_b,
		t1.fee_amt,t1.promo_startdt,t1.promo_enddt,t1.promo_fee,t1.tax_cd_id, t5.tax_cd,t1.allow_otc,t1.ll_parent_id,
		t1.ll_start_day,t1.ll_end_day,t1.ll_start_mth,t1.ll_end_mth,t1.ledger_cd,t1.ss_cd, t6.ss_nm ,t1.effective_date,
		t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by, t8.nm,t1.modified_by, t3.nm ,t1.status, t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm,t1.assign_to, t4.nm, t1.action,
		t1.r_fee_det_nm, t1.r_fee_amt, t1.r_ss_cd, t1.r_promo_startdt, t1.r_promo_enddt, t1.r_ll_required, t1.r_add_notes, t1.mft_status
		into o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd,o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by, o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm,o_action,
			o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status
		from rms_mft_wf t1
		join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
		left outer join rms_user t3 on t1.modified_by = t3.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_user t4 on t1.assign_to = t4.ssm4uuserrefno
		left outer join rms_tax_code t5 on t1.tax_cd_id = t5.tax_cd_id
		left outer join rms_ss t6 on t1.ss_cd = t6.ss_cd
		left outer join rms_fee_group t7 on t1.fee_grp_id = t7.fee_grp_id
		left outer join rms_user t8 on t1.created_by = t8.ssm4uuserrefno
		where (i_wf_id is null or t1.wf_id = i_wf_id)
						--and (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = t1.ss_cd)
					    and (i_fee_detail_pk is null or t1.fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk)
                        and (i_ss_cd is null or ',' || t1.ss_cd || ',' like '%' || ',' || i_ss_cd || ','  || '%')
						and (i_assign_to is null or i_assign_to = '' or t1.assign_to = i_assign_to)
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
						and (i_modified_by_nm is null or t3.nm like '%' || i_modified_by_nm || '%')
						and (i_created_by is null or i_created_by = '' or t1.created_by = i_created_by)
						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%')
						and (i_fee_detail_id is null or t1.fee_detail_id like '%' || i_fee_detail_id ||'%')
						and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        				and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        				and (i_dt_created_fr is null or t1.dt_created >= i_dt_created_fr)
        				and (i_dt_created_to is null or t1.dt_created <= i_dt_created_to)
        				and (i_dt_effective_fr is null or t1.effective_date >= i_dt_effective_fr)
        				and (i_dt_effective_to is null or t1.effective_date <= i_dt_effective_to)
		order by t1.dt_modified desc
		
		return o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id,o_fee_grp_nm_en,o_fee_grp_nm_bm,o_fee_detail_nm_e,o_fee_detail_nm_b,
			o_fee_amt,o_promo_startdt,o_promo_enddt,o_promo_fee,o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd,o_allow_otc,o_ll_parent_id,
			o_ll_start_day,o_ll_end_day,o_ll_start_mth,o_ll_end_mth,o_ledger_cd,o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm,
			o_effective_date,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_created_by_nm,o_modified_by,o_modified_by_nm,o_status, o_status_en,o_status_bm,
			o_assign_to,o_assign_to_nm, o_action, o_r_fee_det_nm, o_r_fee_amt, o_r_ss_cd, o_r_promo_startdt, o_r_promo_enddt, o_r_ll_required, o_r_add_notes, o_mft_status,
			'MA'||lpad(o_wf_id,6,'0'), total with resume;
			
	end foreach	
end if

end procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getMFTWFByStatusAndEffDate (i_status nvarchar(10))
returning int8 as wf_id, integer as fee_detail_pk, nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id, integer as fee_grp_id, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_e, nvarchar(100) as fee_detail_nm_b, 
          decimal(16,2) as fee_amt, date as promo_startdt, date as promo_enddt, decimal(16,2) as promo_fee,
          integer as tax_cd_id, integer as  allow_otc, nvarchar(10) as ll_parent_id, integer as ll_start_day, integer as ll_start_mth, 
		  integer as ll_end_day, integer as ll_end_mth, nvarchar(50) as ledger_cd, nvarchar(100) as ss_cd, date as effective_date, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		  datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, nvarchar(25) as assign_to, nvarchar(50) as action;

		DEFINE o_wf_id int8;
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_pk integer;
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
		DEFINE o_fee_grp_id integer;
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_e nvarchar(100);
		DEFINE o_fee_detail_nm_b nvarchar(100);
		define o_fee_amt decimal(16,2);
		define o_promo_startdt date;
		define o_promo_enddt date;
		define o_promo_fee decimal(16,2);
		define o_tax_cd_id integer;
		define o_allow_otc integer;
		define o_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10);
		define o_ll_start_day integer;
		define o_ll_start_mth integer;
		define o_ll_end_day integer;
		define o_ll_end_mth integer;
		define o_ledger_cd nvarchar(50);
		define o_ss_cd nvarchar(100);
	    define o_effective_date date;
		define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
		define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
		define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
		define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
		define o_status nvarchar(10);
		define o_assign_to nvarchar(25);
		define o_action nvarchar(50);

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
	 select t0.wf_id, t0.fee_detail_pk, t0.fee_detail_id, t0.fee_grp_id, t0.fee_detail_nm_e, t0.fee_detail_nm_b, t0.fee_amt, t0.promo_startdt, t0.promo_enddt, t0.promo_fee,
     t0.tax_cd_id, t0.allow_otc, t0.ll_parent_id, t0.ll_start_day, t0.ll_start_mth, t0.ll_end_day, t0.ll_end_mth, t0.ledger_cd, t0.ss_cd, t0.effective_date, t0.dt_created, t0.dt_modified,
     t0.created_by, t0.modified_by, t0.status , t0.assign_to, t0.action
     INTO o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_e, o_fee_detail_nm_b, o_fee_amt, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
     o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_effective_date, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
     o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_assign_to, o_action
     from rms_mft_wf as t0
     where t0.status = i_status and TODAY >= effective_date


		RETURN o_wf_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_fee_grp_id, o_fee_detail_nm_e, o_fee_detail_nm_b, o_fee_amt, o_promo_startdt, o_promo_enddt, o_promo_fee,
     o_tax_cd_id, o_allow_otc, o_ll_parent_id, o_ll_start_day, o_ll_start_mth, o_ll_end_day, o_ll_end_mth, o_ledger_cd, o_ss_cd, o_effective_date, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
     o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_assign_to, o_action WITH RESUME;
    END foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmftwfdoc(i_page int, i_size int, i_wf_id int8, i_status nvarchar(10))
returning   int8 as wf_id,
            nvarchar(255) as file_nm,
		--	blob as file_content,
			nvarchar(5) as file_type,
			int as file_size_kb,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			int as total;
			
define o_wfdoc_id int8;
define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
--define o_file_content blob;
define o_file_type nvarchar(5);
define o_file_size_kb int;
define o_dt_created datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define calculatedpage int;
define total int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (
				select count(1)
				from rms_mft_wfdoc
				where (i_wf_id is null or wf_id = i_wf_id)
					and (i_status is null or status = i_status)
			);

--foreach c_getmftwfdoc for
	--select skip calculatedpage limit i_size file_nm, file_content, file_type, file_size_kb, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by
	--into	o_file_nm, o_file_content,o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by
	--from rms_mft_wfdoc
	--where (i_wf_id is null or wf_id = i_wf_id)
	--	and (i_status is null or status = i_status) 
	--	order by dt_modified desc
		
	--return o_file_nm, o_file_content,o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by, total with resume;
--end foreach

foreach c_getmftwfdoc for
	select skip calculatedpage limit i_size wfdoc_id, file_nm, file_type, file_size_kb, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by
	into  o_wfdoc_id,o_file_nm,o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by
	from rms_mft_wfdoc
	where (i_wf_id is null or wf_id = i_wf_id)
		and (i_status is null or status = i_status) 
		order by dt_modified desc
		
	return o_wfdoc_id,o_file_nm,o_file_type,o_file_size_kb,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by, total with resume;
end foreach


end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmftwfdocfilecontent(i_wfdoc_id int8)
returning blob as file_content;

    DEFINE o_file_content BLOB;

    SELECT file_content INTO o_file_content
    FROM rms_mft_wfdoc
    WHERE wfdoc_id = i_wfdoc_id;

    -- Set the output parameter based on the count
    return o_file_content;
END procedure

create or replace procedure sp_getmftwfhis(i_page int, i_size int, i_wf_id int8, i_status nvarchar(10))
returning 	nvarchar(50) as action,
			datetime year to second as dt_activity,
			nvarchar(25) as act_by,
			nvarchar(25) as assign_to,
			lvarchar(500) as remark,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(50) as status_en,
			nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
			int as total;
			
define o_action nvarchar(50);
define o_dt_activity datetime year to second;
define o_act_by nvarchar(25);
define o_assign_to nvarchar(25);
define o_remark lvarchar(500);
define o_dt_created datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
define o_status_en nvarchar(50);
define o_status_bm nvarchar(50);
define calculatedpage int;
define total int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (
				select count(1)
				from rms_mft_wfhist t1
                join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd
				where (i_wf_id is null or wf_id = i_wf_id)
                and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
                and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
			);

foreach c_getmftwfhis for
	select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.action,t1.dt_activity,t1.act_by,t1.assign_to,t1.remark,t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by,t1.modified_by,t2.nm_en, t2.nm_bm
	into	o_action, o_dt_activity,o_act_by,o_assign_to,o_remark,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status_en, o_status_bm
	from rms_mft_wfhist t1
	join rms_param t2 on t1.status = t2.param_cd
	where (i_wf_id is null or wf_id = i_wf_id)
	and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status) 
	and t2.param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT'
	order by t1.dt_activity desc 
	
	return o_action, o_dt_activity,o_act_by,o_assign_to,o_remark,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status_en, o_status_bm, total with resume;
end foreach


end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmftwfhistwithed(i_page integer,i_size integer, i_wf_id integer)
returning integer as wf_id,nvarchar(50) as action, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_activity, nvarchar(25) as act_by,
	nvarchar(25) as assign_to, nvarchar(200) as remark, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified,
    nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, date as effective_date, integer as total;
	
	define o_wf_id integer;
	define o_action nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_activity datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_act_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_assign_to nvarchar(25);
	define o_remark nvarchar(200);
	define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define o_effective_date date;
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) from rms_mft_wfhist
        where status = 'a' and wf_id=i_wf_id);
       
       foreach cursor1 for
        select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.wf_id, t1.action, t1.dt_activity, t1.act_by, t1.assign_to, t1.remark,
        t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t0.effective_date
        into o_wf_id, o_action, o_dt_activity, o_act_by, o_assign_to, o_remark, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status , o_effective_date
        from rms_mft_wfhist as t1 inner join rms_mft_wf as t0 on t1.wf_id=t0.wf_id
        where t1.status = 'a' and t1.wf_id=i_wf_id
		
		return o_wf_id, o_action, o_dt_activity, o_act_by, o_assign_to, o_remark, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified,
        o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_effective_date, total with resume;
       
	end foreach
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmtt(i_orn_no NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNING INT AS mtt_id,NVARCHAR(20) AS orn_no,DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND as orn_dt,NVARCHAR(255) AS cust_nm,
	NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_1, NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_2,NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_3,
	NVARCHAR(15) AS cust_postcode,NVARCHAR(50) AS cust_city,NVARCHAR(50) AS cust_state,NVARCHAR(100) AS cust_email,NVARCHAR(15) AS cust_phone,
	DECIMAL(16,2) AS total_amt,nvarchar(10) as order_status,lvarchar(2000) as ss_return_url;
--RETURNING INT AS mtt_id,NVARCHAR(20) AS orn_no,NVARCHAR(255) AS cust_nm,
--	NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_1, NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_2,NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_addr_3,
--	NVARCHAR(15) AS cust_postcode,NVARCHAR(50) AS cust_city,NVARCHAR(50) AS cust_state,NVARCHAR(15) AS cust_phone,
--	DECIMAL(16,2) AS total_amt;

DEFINE o_mtt_id INT;
DEFINE o_orn_no NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_cust_nm NVARCHAR(255);
DEFINE o_cust_addr_1 NVARCHAR(150);
DEFINE o_cust_addr_2 NVARCHAR(150);
DEFINE o_cust_addr_3 NVARCHAR(150);
DEFINE o_cust_postcode NVARCHAR(15);
DEFINE o_cust_city NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_cust_state NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_cust_email NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_cust_phone NVARCHAR(15);
DEFINE o_total_amt DECIMAL(16,2);
define o_orn_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
define o_order_status nvarchar(10);
define o_ss_return_url lvarchar(2000);

FOREACH cursor1 FOR
	SELECT FIRST 1 mtt_id,orn_no,cust_nm,cust_addr_1,cust_addr_2,cust_addr_3,cust_postcode,cust_city,cust_state,cust_email,cust_phone,total_amt,orn_dt,order_status,ss_return_url
	INTO o_mtt_id, o_orn_no,o_cust_nm,o_cust_addr_1,o_cust_addr_2,o_cust_addr_3,o_cust_postcode,o_cust_city,o_cust_state,o_cust_email, o_cust_phone,o_total_amt,o_orn_dt,o_order_status,o_ss_return_url
	FROM rms_mtt
	WHERE orn_no = i_orn_no
	RETURN o_mtt_id, o_orn_no,o_orn_dt,o_cust_nm,o_cust_addr_1,o_cust_addr_2,o_cust_addr_3,o_cust_postcode,o_cust_city,o_cust_state,o_cust_email,o_cust_phone,o_total_amt,o_order_status,o_ss_return_url;
END foreach

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmttdetails( 
	i_ss_cd nvarchar(10),
    i_orn_no nvarchar(20),
	i_total_amt decimal ,
	i_order_status nvarchar(20) ,
	i_rcpt_no nvarchar(20))
returning 
    nvarchar(10)                                    as rms_type ,
	nvarchar(10)                                    as ss_cd ,
	nvarchar(20)                                    as orn_no ,
	datetime year to second                         as orn_dt ,
	nvarchar(45)                                    as cust_ip ,
	nvarchar(255)                                   as cust_nm ,
	nvarchar(150)                                   as cust_addr_1 ,
	nvarchar(150)                                   as cust_addr_2 ,
	nvarchar(150)                                   as cust_addr_3 ,
	nvarchar(15)                                    as cust_postcode ,
	nvarchar(50)                                    as cust_city ,
	nvarchar(50)                                    as cust_state ,
	nvarchar(150)                                   as cust_email ,
	nvarchar(15)                                    as cust_phone ,
	decimal                                         as total_amt ,
	nvarchar(20)                                    as order_status;
define o_rms_type nvarchar(10);
define o_ss_cd nvarchar(10); 
define o_orn_no nvarchar(20); 
define o_orn_dt datetime year to second ; 
define o_cust_ip nvarchar(45) ; 
define o_cust_nm nvarchar(255) ; 
define o_cust_addr_1 nvarchar(150) ; 
define o_cust_addr_2 nvarchar(150) ; 
define o_cust_addr_3 nvarchar(150) ; 
define o_cust_postcode nvarchar(15) ; 
define o_cust_city nvarchar(50) ; 
define o_cust_state nvarchar(50) ; 
define o_cust_email nvarchar(150) ; 
define o_cust_phone nvarchar(15) ; 
define o_total_amt decimal ; 
define o_order_status nvarchar(20);
select
	t1.rms_type ,
	t1.ss_cd ,
	t1.orn_no ,
	t1.orn_dt ,
	t1.cust_ip ,
	t1.cust_nm ,
	t1.cust_addr_1 ,
	t1.cust_addr_2 ,
	t1.cust_addr_3 ,
	t1.cust_postcode ,
	t1.cust_city ,
	t4.nm_en ,
	t1.cust_email ,
	t1.cust_phone ,
	t1.total_amt ,
	t3.nm_en 
into
	o_rms_type ,
	o_ss_cd ,
	o_orn_no ,
	o_orn_dt ,
	o_cust_ip ,
	o_cust_nm ,
	o_cust_addr_1 ,
	o_cust_addr_2 ,
	o_cust_addr_3 ,
	o_cust_postcode ,
	o_cust_city ,
	o_cust_state ,
	o_cust_email ,
	o_cust_phone ,
	o_total_amt ,
	o_order_status 
from
	rms_mtt t1 
	join rms_mtt_rcpt t2 on t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
    join rms_param t3 on t1.order_status = t3.param_cd and t3.param_grp_nm = 'OrderStatus'
    inner join rms_param t4 on t1.cust_state = t4.param_cd and t4.param_grp_nm = 'State'
where
    (i_ss_cd is null or upper(t1.ss_cd) = upper(i_ss_cd))
    and (i_orn_no is null or t1.orn_no = i_orn_no) 
    and (i_total_amt is null or t1.total_amt = i_total_amt)
    and (i_order_status is null or upper(t3.nm_en) = upper(i_order_status))
    and (i_rcpt_no is null or t2.rcpt_no = i_rcpt_no);
return 
    o_rms_type ,
	o_ss_cd ,
	o_orn_no ,
	o_orn_dt ,
	o_cust_ip ,
	o_cust_nm ,
	o_cust_addr_1 ,
	o_cust_addr_2 ,
	o_cust_addr_3 ,
	o_cust_postcode ,
	o_cust_city ,
	o_cust_state ,
	o_cust_email ,
	o_cust_phone ,
	o_total_amt ,
	o_order_status; 
end
	procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getmttitem(i_mtt_id int)
RETURNING INT as mtt_item_id,
			INT as line_no,
			nvarchar(150) as item_desc,
			int as qty, 
			decimal(16,2) as unit_fee, 
			decimal(16,2) as tax_amt, 
			decimal(16,2) as disc_amt,
			decimal(16,2) as gross_amt,
			nvarchar(10) as fee_detail_id,
			nvarchar(30) as item_ref_no,
			nvarchar(50) as grant_cd,
			decimal(16,2) as tax_pct,
			decimal(16,2) as net_amt,
			nvarchar(1) as entity_type,
			nvarchar(20) as entity_no,
			nvarchar(100) as entity_nm,
			nvarchar(20) as cp_no,
			INT as cp_tier,
			decimal(16,2) as cp_tier_amt,
			decimal(16,2) as cp_tier_discpct;
 
DEFINE o_mtt_item_id int;
DEFINE o_line_no int;
DEFINE o_item_desc nvarchar(150);
DEFINE o_qty int;
DEFINE o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_tax_amt decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_disc_amt decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_gross_amt decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
DEFINE o_item_ref_no nvarchar(30);
DEFINE o_grant_cd nvarchar(50);
DEFINE o_tax_pct decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_net_amt decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_entity_type nvarchar(1);
DEFINE o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
DEFINE o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
DEFINE o_cp_no nvarchar(20);
DEFINE o_cp_tier INT;
DEFINE o_cp_tier_amt decimal(16,2);
DEFINE o_cp_tier_discpct decimal(16,2);
 
FOREACH cursor1 FOR
	SELECT mtt_item_id,line_no,item_desc,qty,unit_fee,tax_amt,disc_amt,gross_amt,fee_detail_id,item_ref_no,grant_cd,tax_pct,net_amt,entity_type,entity_no,entity_nm,cp_no,cp_tier,cp_tier_amt,cp_tier_discpct
	INTO o_mtt_item_id,o_line_no,o_item_desc,o_qty,o_unit_fee,o_tax_amt,o_disc_amt,o_gross_amt,o_fee_detail_id,o_item_ref_no,o_grant_cd,o_tax_pct,o_net_amt,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_entity_nm,o_cp_no,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt,o_cp_tier_discpct
	FROM rms_mtt_item
	WHERE status='A'
	and mtt_id = i_mtt_id
	order by line_no
	RETURN o_mtt_item_id,o_line_no,o_item_desc,o_qty,o_unit_fee,o_tax_amt,o_disc_amt,o_gross_amt,o_fee_detail_id,o_item_ref_no,o_grant_cd,o_tax_pct,o_net_amt,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_entity_nm,o_cp_no,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt,o_cp_tier_discpct with resume;
END foreach
 
END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE
	OR
REPLACE
	PROCEDURE sp_getmttitem_details(i_mtt_item_id int8) 

returning 
    nvarchar(10)                                    AS fee_detail_id,
	nvarchar(30)                                    AS item_ref_no,
	nvarchar(150)                                   AS item_desc,
	integer                                         AS qty,
	decimal                                         AS unit_fee,
	decimal                                         AS gross_amt,
	nvarchar(50)                                    AS grant_cd,
	decimal                                         AS disc_amt,
	decimal                                         AS tax_pct,
	decimal                                         AS tax_amt,
	decimal                                         AS net_amt,
	nvarchar(30)                                     AS entity_type,
	nvarchar(20)                                    AS entity_no,
	nvarchar(100)                                   AS entity_nm,
	nvarchar(20)                                    AS cp_no,
	integer                                         AS cp_tier,
	decimal                                         AS cp_tier_amt,
	decimal                                         AS cp_tier_discpct;

define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
define o_item_ref_no  nvarchar(30);
define o_item_desc nvarchar(150);
define o_qty integer;
define o_unit_fee decimal;
define o_gross_amt decimal;
define o_grant_cd nvarchar(50);
define o_disc_amt decimal;
define o_tax_pct decimal;
define o_tax_amt decimal;
define o_net_amt decimal;
define o_entity_type nvarchar(30);
define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
define o_entity_nm nvarchar(100);
define o_cp_no nvarchar(20);
define o_cp_tier integer;
define o_cp_tier_amt decimal;
define o_cp_tier_discpct decimal;

SELECT
	fee_detail_id,
	item_ref_no,
	item_desc,
	qty,
	unit_fee, 
	gross_amt,
	grant_cd,
	disc_amt,
	tax_pct,
	tax_amt,
	net_amt,
	t2.nm_en,
	entity_no,
	entity_nm,
	cp_no,
	cp_tier,
	cp_tier_amt,
	cp_tier_discpct

INTO
	o_fee_detail_id,
	o_item_ref_no,
	o_item_desc,
	o_qty,
	o_unit_fee, 
	o_gross_amt,
	o_grant_cd,
	o_disc_amt,
	o_tax_pct,
	o_tax_amt,
	o_net_amt,
	o_entity_type,
	o_entity_no,
	o_entity_nm,
	o_cp_no,
	o_cp_tier,
	o_cp_tier_amt,
	o_cp_tier_discpct

FROM
	rms_mtt_item t1
    inner join rms_param t2 on t1.entity_type = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'EntityType'
WHERE
    mtt_item_id = i_mtt_item_id;

RETURN 
	o_fee_detail_id,
	o_item_ref_no,
	o_item_desc,
	o_qty,
	o_unit_fee, 
	o_gross_amt,
	o_grant_cd,
	o_disc_amt,
	o_tax_pct,
	o_tax_amt,
	o_net_amt,
	o_entity_type,
	o_entity_no,
	o_entity_nm,
	o_cp_no,
	o_cp_tier,
	o_cp_tier_amt,
	o_cp_tier_discpct;
END
	PROCEDURE

CREATE  OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getmttlisting(
    i_page INT, i_size INT,
    i_ss_cd_list NVARCHAR(255), -- Assuming a comma-separated list of ss_cd values
    i_orn_no NVARCHAR(20),
    i_orn_dt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_orn_dt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_total_amt DECIMAL(16,2), i_order_status NVARCHAR(10),
    i_rcpt_no NVARCHAR(20), i_rcpt_dt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_rcpt_dt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND
)
RETURNING NVARCHAR(10) AS ss_cd,
          NVARCHAR(20) AS orn_no,
          DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS orn_dt,
          DECIMAL(16,2) AS total_amt,
          NVARCHAR(30) AS order_status,
          NVARCHAR(20) AS rcpt_no,
          DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS rcpt_dt,
          INT AS total,
          INT AS mtt_id;

DEFINE o_mtt_id INT;
DEFINE o_ss_cd NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_orn_no NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_total_amt DECIMAL(16,2);
DEFINE o_orn_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_order_status NVARCHAR(30);
DEFINE o_rcpt_no NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_rcpt_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE calculatedpage INT;
DEFINE total INT;

IF (i_page IS NULL OR i_page < 1) OR (i_size IS NULL OR i_page < 1) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null or less than 1";
END IF;

LET calculatedpage = (i_page - 1) * i_size;

LET total = (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM (
        SELECT t1.ss_cd, t1.orn_no, t1.orn_dt, t1.total_amt, t1.order_status,
               t2.rcpt_no, t2.rcpt_dt
        FROM rms_mtt t1
        LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_mtt_rcpt t2 ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
        WHERE (i_ss_cd_list IS NULL OR ',' || i_ss_cd_list || ',' LIKE '%,' || t1.ss_cd || ',%')
          AND (i_orn_no IS NULL OR t1.orn_no LIKE '%' || i_orn_no || '%')
          AND (i_orn_dt_fr IS NULL OR t1.orn_dt >= i_orn_dt_fr)
          AND (i_orn_dt_to IS NULL OR t1.orn_dt <= i_orn_dt_to)
          AND (i_total_amt IS NULL OR t1.total_amt = i_total_amt)
          AND (i_order_status IS NULL OR t1.order_status = i_order_status )
          AND (i_rcpt_no IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_no LIKE '%' || i_rcpt_no || '%')
          AND (i_rcpt_dt_fr IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_dt >= i_rcpt_dt_fr)
          AND (i_rcpt_dt_to IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_dt <= i_rcpt_dt_to)
        GROUP BY t1.ss_cd, t1.orn_no, t1.orn_dt, t1.total_amt, t1.order_status,
                 t2.rcpt_no, t2.rcpt_dt
    ) AS subquery
);

FOREACH c_getmtt FOR
    SELECT SKIP calculatedpage LIMIT i_size
           UPPER(t1.ss_cd), t1.orn_no, t1.orn_dt, t1.total_amt, t3.nm_en,--t1.order_status,
           t2.rcpt_no, t2.rcpt_dt, t1.mtt_id
    INTO o_ss_cd, o_orn_no, o_orn_dt, o_total_amt, o_order_status, o_rcpt_no, o_rcpt_dt, o_mtt_id
    FROM rms_mtt t1
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_mtt_rcpt t2 ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
    left join rms_param t3 on t1.order_status=t3.param_cd and t3.param_grp_nm ='OrderStatus'
    WHERE (i_ss_cd_list IS NULL OR ',' || i_ss_cd_list || ',' LIKE '%,' || t1.ss_cd || ',%')
      AND (i_orn_no IS NULL OR t1.orn_no LIKE '%' || i_orn_no || '%')
      AND (i_orn_dt_fr IS NULL OR t1.orn_dt >= i_orn_dt_fr)
      AND (i_orn_dt_to IS NULL OR t1.orn_dt <= i_orn_dt_to)
      AND (i_total_amt IS NULL OR t1.total_amt = i_total_amt)
      AND (i_order_status IS NULL OR t1.order_status= i_order_status)
      AND (i_rcpt_no IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_no LIKE '%' || i_rcpt_no || '%')
      AND (i_rcpt_dt_fr IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_dt >= i_rcpt_dt_fr)
      AND (i_rcpt_dt_to IS NULL OR t2.rcpt_dt <= i_rcpt_dt_to)
    GROUP BY t1.ss_cd, t1.orn_no, t1.orn_dt, t1.total_amt,t3.nm_en,-- t1.order_status,
             t2.rcpt_no, t2.rcpt_dt, t1.mtt_id
RETURN o_ss_cd, o_orn_no, o_orn_dt, o_total_amt, o_order_status, o_rcpt_no, o_rcpt_dt, total, o_mtt_id WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE
	OR
REPLACE
	PROCEDURE sp_getmttlistingitem(i_mtt_id int8) 

returning
    nvarchar(150)                                   AS item_desc ,
	nvarchar(30)                                    AS item_ref_no ,
	integer                                         AS qty,
	decimal                                         AS unit_fee ,
	decimal                                         AS gross_amt ,
	decimal                                         AS disc_amt,
	decimal                                         AS tax_amt,
    integer                                         AS mtt_item_id;

define o_item_desc nvarchar(150);
define o_item_ref_no nvarchar(30); 
define o_qty integer; 
define o_unit_fee decimal; 
define o_gross_amt decimal ; 
define o_disc_amt decimal ; 
define o_tax_amt decimal ;
define o_mtt_item_id integer; 

FOREACH c_mtt_item FOR
SELECT
	item_desc ,
	item_ref_no ,
	qty ,
	unit_fee ,
	gross_amt ,
	disc_amt ,
	tax_amt,
    mtt_item_id

INTO
	o_item_desc ,
	o_item_ref_no ,
	o_qty ,
	o_unit_fee ,
	o_gross_amt ,
	o_disc_amt ,
	o_tax_amt,
    o_mtt_item_id

FROM
	rms_mtt t1 
		JOIN rms_mtt_item t2 
		ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id 
WHERE
    t1.mtt_id = i_mtt_id

RETURN 
	o_item_desc ,
	o_item_ref_no ,
	o_qty ,
	o_unit_fee ,
	o_gross_amt ,
	o_disc_amt ,
	o_tax_amt,
    o_mtt_item_id WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH;
END
	PROCEDURE

create
	or
replace
	procedure sp_getmttpg(i_mtt_id int8) 

returning 
datetime year to second as pymt_submit_dt, 
nvarchar(20) as pg_pymt_id, 
decimal as pg_pymt_amt, 
nvarchar(30) as pg_txn_status,
integer as mtt_pg_id;

define o_pymt_submit_dt datetime year to second;
define o_pg_pymt_id nvarchar(20); 
define o_pg_pymt_amt decimal; 
define o_pg_txn_status nvarchar(30);
define o_mtt_pg_id integer; 

foreach c_mtt_pg for
select 
	pymt_submit_dt ,
	pg_pymt_id ,
	pg_pymt_amt ,
	t3.nm_en,
    mtt_pg_id

into
	o_pymt_submit_dt ,
	o_pg_pymt_id ,
	o_pg_pymt_amt ,
	o_pg_txn_status,
    o_mtt_pg_id

from
        rms_mtt t1 
		join rms_mtt_pg t2 on t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
        inner join rms_param t3 on t2.pg_txn_status = t3.param_cd and param_grp_nm = 'pgtxn-status'
where
    t1.mtt_id = i_mtt_id

return 
	o_pymt_submit_dt ,
	o_pg_pymt_id ,
	o_pg_pymt_amt ,
	o_pg_txn_status,
    o_mtt_pg_id with resume;
end foreach; 
end
	procedure

CREATE
	OR
REPLACE
	PROCEDURE sp_getmttpg_details(i_mtt_pg_id int8) 

returning 
datetime year to second as pymt_submit_dt, 
nvarchar(30) as pg_pymt_method,
nvarchar(20) as pg_pymt_id, 
nvarchar(100) as pg_pymt_desc,
decimal as pg_pymt_amt, 
nvarchar(3) as pg_curr_cd,
decimal as pg_tax_amt,
decimal as pg_b4tax_amt,
nvarchar(30) as pg_txn_id,
nvarchar(50) as pg_txn_status;

define o_pymt_submit_dt datetime year to second;
define o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(30);
define o_pg_pymt_id nvarchar(20);
define o_pg_pymt_desc nvarchar(100);
define o_pg_pymt_amt decimal; 
define o_pg_curr_cd nvarchar(3);
define o_pg_tax_amt decimal;
define o_pg_b4tax_amt decimal;
define o_pg_txn_id nvarchar(30);
define o_pg_txn_status nvarchar(50); 

SELECT 
	pymt_submit_dt ,
    t3.nm_en,
	pg_pymt_id ,
    pg_pymt_desc,
	pg_pymt_amt ,
    pg_curr_cd,
    pg_tax_amt,
    pg_b4tax_amt,
    pg_txn_id,
	t2.nm_en

INTO
	o_pymt_submit_dt ,
    o_pg_pymt_method,
	o_pg_pymt_id ,
    o_pg_pymt_desc,
	o_pg_pymt_amt ,
    o_pg_curr_cd,
    o_pg_tax_amt,
    o_pg_b4tax_amt,
    o_pg_txn_id,
	o_pg_txn_status 

FROM
    rms_mtt_pg t1
    inner join rms_param t2 on t1.pg_txn_status = t2.param_cd and t2.param_grp_nm = 'PGTxn-Status'
    inner join rms_param t3 on t1.pg_pymt_method = t3.param_cd and t3.param_grp_nm = 'PGPaymentMethod'
WHERE
    mtt_pg_id = i_mtt_pg_id;

RETURN 
	o_pymt_submit_dt ,
    o_pg_pymt_method,
	o_pg_pymt_id ,
    o_pg_pymt_desc,
	o_pg_pymt_amt ,
    o_pg_curr_cd,
    o_pg_tax_amt,
    o_pg_b4tax_amt,
    o_pg_txn_id,
	o_pg_txn_status; 
END
	PROCEDURE
