create or replace procedure sp_getMTTPGToCheck()
	returning integer as mtt_pg_id, integer as mtt_id, datetime year to fraction(5) as pymt_submit_dt, nvarchar(7) as pg_txn_type, nvarchar(3) as pg_pymt_method,
		nvarchar(3) as pg_service_id, nvarchar(20) as pg_pymt_id, nvarchar(100) as pg_pymt_desc, decimal(16,2) as pg_pymt_amt, nvarchar(3) as pg_curr_cd,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_b4tax_amt, decimal(16,2) as pg_tax_amt, nvarchar(2) as pg_lang_cd, nvarchar(30) as pg_txn_id, nvarchar(30) as pg_issuing_bank,
		nvarchar(12) as pg_auth_cd, integer as pg_txn_status, nvarchar(255) as pg_txn_msg, nvarchar(100) as pg_hash_value, nvarchar(100) as pg_hash_value2,
		nvarchar(100) as pg_qhash_value, integer as pg_txn_exists, nvarchar(255) as pg_query_desc, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
		datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by
		, decimal(16,2) as pg_refund_amt
		, nvarchar(255) as pg_bank_refno
		, nvarchar(255) as pg_session_id
		, nvarchar(3) as pg_token_type
		, nvarchar(50) as pg_token
		, datetime year to fraction(5) as pg_resp_time
		, nvarchar(19) as pg_cardno_mask
		, nvarchar(30) as pg_cardholder
		, nvarchar(10) as pg_cardtype
		, nvarchar(6) as pg_cardexp;
		 
			DEFINE o_mtt_pg_id integer;
			DEFINE o_mtt_id integer;
			DEFINE o_pymt_submit_dt datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_type nvarchar(7);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_service_id nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_id nvarchar(20);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_desc nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_curr_cd nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_b4tax_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_tax_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_lang_cd nvarchar(2);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_id nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_issuing_bank nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_auth_cd nvarchar(12);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_status integer;
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_msg nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_hash_value nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_hash_value2 nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_qhash_value nvarchar(100);
			DEFINE o_pg_txn_exists integer;
			DEFINE o_pg_query_desc nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
			DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
			DEFINE o_pg_refund_amt decimal(16,2);
			DEFINE o_pg_bank_refno nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_session_id nvarchar(255);
			DEFINE o_pg_token_type nvarchar(3);
			DEFINE o_pg_token nvarchar(50);
			DEFINE o_pg_resp_time datetime year to fraction(5);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardno_mask nvarchar(19);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardholder nvarchar(30);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardtype nvarchar(10);
			DEFINE o_pg_cardexp nvarchar(6);
		
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select pg.mtt_pg_id, pg.mtt_id, pg.pymt_submit_dt, pg.pg_txn_type, pg.pg_pymt_method, pg.pg_service_id, pg.pg_pymt_id
		, pg.pg_pymt_desc, pg.pg_pymt_amt, pg.pg_curr_cd, pg.pg_b4tax_amt, pg.pg_tax_amt, pg.pg_lang_cd, pg.pg_txn_id, pg.pg_issuing_bank
		, pg.pg_auth_cd, pg.pg_txn_status, pg.pg_txn_msg, pg.pg_hash_value, pg.pg_hash_value2, pg.pg_qhash_value, pg.pg_txn_exists
		, pg.pg_query_desc,pg.dt_created, pg.dt_modified, pg.created_by, pg.modified_by, pg.pg_refund_amt, pg.pg_bank_refno, pg.pg_session_id
		, pg.pg_token_type, pg.pg_token, pg.pg_resp_time, pg.pg_cardno_mask, pg.pg_cardholder, pg.pg_cardtype, pg.pg_cardexp
        INTO o_mtt_pg_id, o_mtt_id, o_pymt_submit_dt, o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_pg_pymt_id, o_pg_pymt_desc
        , o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_pg_b4tax_amt, o_pg_tax_amt, o_pg_lang_cd, o_pg_txn_id, o_pg_issuing_bank, o_pg_auth_cd, o_pg_txn_status
        , o_pg_txn_msg, o_pg_hash_value, o_pg_hash_value2, o_pg_qhash_value, o_pg_txn_exists, o_pg_query_desc, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified
        , o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_pg_refund_amt, o_pg_bank_refno, o_pg_session_id, o_pg_token_type, o_pg_token, o_pg_resp_time
        , o_pg_cardno_mask, o_pg_cardholder, o_pg_cardtype, o_pg_cardexp
		from (select *, row_number() over(partition by mtt_id order by dt_created desc) as rownum from rms_mtt_pg) pg 
			left outer join (select mtt_id, order_status from rms_mtt) mtt on pg.mtt_id = mtt.mtt_id
		where (pg.rownum = 1 or pg.pg_txn_exists is null) AND (pg.pg_txn_status = 2 or mtt.order_status = 'PIP' or mtt.order_status = 'PP')
		
		
		RETURN o_mtt_pg_id, o_mtt_id, o_pymt_submit_dt, o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_pg_pymt_id, o_pg_pymt_desc
        , o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_pg_b4tax_amt, o_pg_tax_amt, o_pg_lang_cd, o_pg_txn_id, o_pg_issuing_bank, o_pg_auth_cd, o_pg_txn_status
        , o_pg_txn_msg, o_pg_hash_value, o_pg_hash_value2, o_pg_qhash_value, o_pg_txn_exists, o_pg_query_desc, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified
        , o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_pg_refund_amt, o_pg_bank_refno, o_pg_session_id, o_pg_token_type, o_pg_token, o_pg_resp_time
        , o_pg_cardno_mask, o_pg_cardholder, o_pg_cardtype, o_pg_cardexp WITH RESUME;
	END foreach
end procedure
GO
CREATE
	OR
REPLACE
	PROCEDURE sp_getmttrcpt(i_mtt_id int8) 

returning 
nvarchar(20) as rcpt_no,
datetime year to second as rcpt_dt,
integer as rcpt_reprint,
datetime year to second as dt_modified;

define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(20);
define o_rcpt_dt datetime year to second;
define o_rcpt_reprint integer;
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;

SELECT 
	rcpt_no ,
	rcpt_dt ,
    rcpt_reprint,
	t2.dt_modified

INTO
	o_rcpt_no ,
	o_rcpt_dt ,
    o_rcpt_reprint,
	o_dt_modified

FROM
    rms_mtt t1 join rms_mtt_rcpt t2 on t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id

WHERE
    t2.mtt_id = i_mtt_id;

RETURN 
	o_rcpt_no ,
	o_rcpt_dt ,
    o_rcpt_reprint,
	o_dt_modified;
END
	PROCEDURE
GO
																			 

				  

					   

							  
				   
								 
															  

							

			  
  
/*
remarks on shortcut:
nm - name
en - english
bm - bahasa malaysia
i - input
o - output 
c - cursor
*/

create or replace procedure sp_getparam (i_page integer,i_size integer, i_param_cd nvarchar(50), i_param_grp_nm nvarchar(50))

	returning 	nvarchar(50) as param_cd,
				nvarchar(50) as nm_en,
				nvarchar(50) as nm_bm,
				integer as total;
				
	define o_param_cd nvarchar(50);
	define o_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;
	
if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;	
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_param
					where (i_param_cd is null or i_param_cd = '' or param_cd = i_param_cd)
       						and (i_param_grp_nm is null or param_grp_nm = i_param_grp_nm)
       						and status = upper('a')
				);

	foreach c_getparam for	
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size param_cd, nm_en, nm_bm
		into o_param_cd, o_nm_en, o_nm_bm
		from rms_param
		where (i_param_cd is null or i_param_cd = '' or param_cd = i_param_cd)
	       		and (i_param_grp_nm is null or param_grp_nm = i_param_grp_nm)
	       		and status = upper('a')
	   	order by seq	
	
		return o_param_cd, o_nm_en, o_nm_bm,total with resume;
	end foreach
	
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getpendingdiagingrpt()
								
returning	int8 as rpt_di_age_id,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_req,
			int as p_tmn_status,
			nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty,
			nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm,
			nvarchar(10) as p_txn_ty,
			nvarchar(10) as p_status,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_exp_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_eff_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_app_to,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_fr,
			datetime year to second as p_dt_tmn_to,
			datetime year to second as dt_created,
			datetime year to second as dt_modified,
			nvarchar(25) as created_by,
			nvarchar(25) as modified_by,
			nvarchar(10) as status,
			nvarchar(50) as p_email,
			nvarchar(50) as p_file_type,
			int as p_file_size,
			nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,
			nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no,
			nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no,
			nvarchar(10) as task_id;
			
define o_rpt_di_age_id		int8;
define o_p_dt_req           datetime year to second;
define o_p_tmn_status		int;
define o_p_ent_ty			nvarchar(1);
define o_p_ent_nm		    nvarchar(100);
define o_p_txn_ty		    nvarchar(10);
define o_p_status	        nvarchar(10);
define o_p_dt_exp_fr	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_exp_to 	    datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_eff_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_app_to		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_fr		datetime year to second;
define o_p_dt_tmn_to		datetime year to second;
define o_dt_created			datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified		datetime year to second;
define o_created_by			nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by		nvarchar(25);
define o_status				nvarchar(10);
define o_p_email			nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_type		nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_size		int;
define o_p_file_nm		    nvarchar(255);
define o_p_batch_no		    nvarchar(30);
define o_p_fms_ref_no		nvarchar(25);

	foreach c_getpendingdiagingrpt for
		select t1.rpt_di_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_tmn_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm, t1.p_txn_ty, t1.p_status,
		t1.p_dt_exp_fr, t1.p_dt_exp_to, t1.p_dt_eff_fr, t1.p_dt_eff_to, t1.p_dt_app_fr, t1.p_dt_app_to, t1.p_dt_tmn_fr,t1.p_dt_tmn_to,
	    t1.dt_created,t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm, 
	    t1.p_batch_no, t1.p_fms_ref_no
		into o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm,
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no
		from rms_rpt_di_age t1
		where t1.status = 'P' or t1.status = 'I'	
		
		return o_rpt_di_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_tmn_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm, o_p_txn_ty, o_p_status, 
		o_p_dt_exp_fr, o_p_dt_exp_to, o_p_dt_eff_fr, o_p_dt_eff_to, o_p_dt_app_fr, o_p_dt_app_to, o_p_dt_tmn_fr,o_p_dt_tmn_to,
	    o_dt_created,o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_di_age_id,6,'0') with resume;	
		
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getpendingdiagingrptbyid(i_rpt_di_age_id INT8)

returning integer;

define o_count integer;

	select count(1) into o_count 
	from rms_rpt_di_age 
	where status = "P"
	and rpt_di_age_id = i_rpt_di_age_id;

	return o_count with resume;

end procedure;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getpendingriplagingrpt ()
RETURNING
    INT8 AS rpt_ripl_age_id,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_req,
    INT AS p_imp_status,
    INT AS p_exp_status,
    NVARCHAR(1) AS p_ent_ty,
    NVARCHAR(100) AS p_ent_nm,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_created,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_modified,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS status,
    nvarchar(50) as p_email,
	nvarchar(50) as p_file_type,
	int as p_file_size,
	nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,
	nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no,
	nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no,
	nvarchar(10) as task_id;

DEFINE o_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8;
DEFINE o_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_imp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_exp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1);
DEFINE o_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_status NVARCHAR(10);
define o_p_email nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_type nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_size int;
define o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_p_batch_no	nvarchar(30);
define o_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);




FOREACH c_getriplaging FOR
    select t1.rpt_ripl_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_imp_status, t1.p_exp_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm,
           t1.p_dt_due_fr, t1.p_dt_due_to, t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr, t1.p_dt_rcpt_to, t1.p_dt_imp_fr, t1.p_dt_imp_to,
           t1.p_dt_wo_fr, t1.p_dt_wo_to, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by,
           t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm, 
	       t1.p_batch_no, t1.p_fms_ref_no
    INTO o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
         o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
         o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
         o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm,
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no
    FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
    
    where t1.status = 'P' or t1.status = 'I'
      

    RETURN o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
           o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
           o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
           o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 
	       o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_ripl_age_id,6,'0') with resume;
END FOREACH


	
END PROCEDURE
GO

returning integer;

define o_count integer;

	select count(1) into o_count 
	from rms_rpt_ripl_age 
	where status = "P"
	and rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id;

	return o_count with resume;

end procedure;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getpendingrptricpagerq() returning  
integer as rpt_ricp_age_id, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req, integer as p_exp_status, integer as p_can_v_status, nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty, 
nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_fr, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, nvarchar(255) as p_email, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_to, nvarchar(5) as file_type, integer as p_file_size,
nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no, nvarchar(8) as task_id;

	DEFINE o_rpt_ricp_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_exp_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_can_v_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_ent_ty nvarchar(1);
	DEFINE o_p_ent_nm nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
	define o_task_id nvarchar(8);

	FOREACH c_getpendingrptricpagerq FOR
        select rpt_ricp_age_id,p_dt_req,p_exp_status,p_can_v_status,p_ent_ty,p_ent_nm,p_dt_iss_fr,p_dt_iss_to,
				p_dt_exp_fr,p_dt_exp_to,p_dt_wo_fr,p_dt_wo_to,p_dt_can_fr,p_dt_can_to,p_dt_void_fr,
				p_dt_void_to,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,p_email,p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				p_dt_rcpt_to,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,p_batch_no,p_fms_ref_no,'RG' || lpad(rpt_ricp_age_id,6,'0')
        INTO o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id
        FROM rms_rpt_ricp_age where status = 'P' or status = 'I'
		
		RETURN o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getpendingrptumage() returning 
integer as rpt_um_age_id,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req,nvarchar(30) as p_txn_id
,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified
,nvarchar(25) as created_by,nvarchar(25) as modified_by,nvarchar(10) as status
,nvarchar(50) as p_rcpt_no,nvarchar(50) as p_stmt_no,nvarchar(10) as p_recon_status
,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_fr,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_to
,integer as p_dup,nvarchar(255) as p_email,nvarchar(5) as p_file_type,integer as p_file_size
,nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm, nvarchar(8) as task_id, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no;

	DEFINE o_rpt_um_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_txn_id nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_rcpt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_stmt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_recon_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dup integer;
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_task_id nvarchar(8);
	define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);

	FOREACH c_getpendingrptumage FOR
        SELECT rpt_um_age_id,p_dt_req,p_txn_id,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,
				p_rcpt_no,p_stmt_no,p_recon_status,p_dt_stmt_fr,p_dt_stmt_to,p_dup,p_email,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,
				'RG' || lpad(rpt_um_age_id,6,'0'), p_batch_no, p_fms_ref_no
        INTO o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,
			o_p_file_nm, o_task_id, o_batch_no, o_fms_ref_no
        FROM rms_rpt_um_age where status = 'P' or status = 'I'
		
		RETURN o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,
			o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm, o_task_id, o_batch_no, o_fms_ref_no WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getpermissions()
	returning  nvarchar(255) as module_nm, lvarchar(max) as function_nm, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;
	DEFINE o_module_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_function_nm lvarchar(max);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE total integer;

	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_perm
        WHERE status = 'A');

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT module_nm, sp_group_concat(function_nm) as function_nm , status
        INTO o_module_nm, o_function_nm, o_status
        FROM (SELECT module_nm, perm_cd, function_nm, status FROM rms_perm WHERE status = 'A' ORDER BY perm_cd)
        GROUP BY module_nm, status
        ORDER BY module_nm

		RETURN o_module_nm, o_function_nm, o_status, total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getpermissionsbyid()
	returning integer as perm_id, nvarchar(25) as perm_cd, nvarchar(255) as module_nm,
    nvarchar(100) as function_nm, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

    DEFINE o_perm_id integer;
	DEFINE o_perm_cd nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_module_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_function_nm lvarchar(max);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE total integer;

	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_perm
        WHERE status = 'A');

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT perm_id, perm_cd, module_nm, function_nm, status
        INTO o_perm_id, o_perm_cd, o_module_nm, o_function_nm, o_status
        FROM rms_perm WHERE status = 'A'

		RETURN o_perm_id, o_perm_cd, o_module_nm, o_function_nm, o_status, total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getpgdetaillisting(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_task_no nvarchar(30), 
                                    i_txn_date date, i_txn_type nvarchar(25), i_fnd_rms nvarchar(3), 
                                    i_txn_id nvarchar(30), i_txn_cd nvarchar(25), i_sub_cri nvarchar(25))
returning nvarchar(100) as dt_txn,
          nvarchar(30) as txn_id,
          nvarchar(25) as txn_type,
          nvarchar(25) as txn_cd,
          nvarchar(3) as found_in_rms,
          nvarchar(25) as sub_criteria,
          decimal(15,2) as txn_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as mdr_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as sst_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as net_amt,
          int as total;

define o_txn_date           nvarchar(100);
define o_txn_id             nvarchar(30);
define o_txn_type           nvarchar(25);
define o_txn_cd             nvarchar(25);
define c_fnd_in_rms         int;
define o_fnd_in_rms         nvarchar(3);
define o_sub_cri            nvarchar(25);
define o_txn_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_mdr_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_sst_amt            decimal(15,2);
define o_net_amt            decimal(15,2);
define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;
define o_rc_pg_id           int8;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if;

--temp set to null
let i_txn_date = null;
let o_rc_pg_id = null;









select rc_pg_id
into o_rc_pg_id
from rms_rc_pg
where task_no = i_task_no;

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(1)
             from rms_rc_pgtxn t1
             where (o_rc_pg_id is null or t1.rc_pg_id = o_rc_pg_id)
             and (i_txn_date is null or t1.dt_txn = i_txn_date)
             and (i_txn_type is null or t1.txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
             and (i_fnd_rms is null or t1.found_in_rms = i_fnd_rms)
             and (i_txn_id is null or t1.txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
             and (i_txn_cd is null or t1.txn_cd like '%' || i_txn_cd || '%')
             and (i_sub_cri is null or t1.sub_criteria like '%' || i_sub_cri || '%')
             );

foreach c_getpgdetaillisting for
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size TO_CHAR(t1.dt_txn, '%d/%m/%Y'), t1.txn_id, t1.txn_type, t1.txn_cd, 
            case when t1.found_in_rms = 1 then 'Yes'
                else 'No'
            end found_in_rms, 
           t1.sub_criteria,
           t1.txn_amt, t1.mdr_amt, t1.sst_amt, t1.net_amt
    into o_txn_date, o_txn_id, o_txn_type, o_txn_cd, o_fnd_in_rms, 
         o_sub_cri, 
         o_txn_amt, o_mdr_amt, o_sst_amt, o_net_amt 
    from rms_rc_pgtxn t1
    where (o_rc_pg_id is null or t1.rc_pg_id = o_rc_pg_id)
            and (i_txn_date is null or t1.dt_txn = i_txn_date)
            and (i_txn_type is null or t1.txn_type like '%' || i_txn_type || '%')
            and (i_fnd_rms is null or t1.found_in_rms = i_fnd_rms)
            and (i_txn_id is null or t1.txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
            and (i_txn_cd is null or t1.txn_cd like '%' || i_txn_cd || '%')
            and (i_sub_cri is null or t1.sub_criteria like '%' || i_sub_cri || '%')

    return o_txn_date, o_txn_id, o_txn_type, o_txn_cd, o_fnd_in_rms, 
           o_sub_cri,
           o_txn_amt, o_mdr_amt, o_sst_amt, o_net_amt, total with resume;

end foreach;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getpgdoc()
returning int8 as rc_pg_id,
            nvarchar(255) as file_nm,
			blob as file_content;

define o_exist int;
define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_file_content blob;
define o_rc_pg_id int8;

define o_file_type nvarchar(5);
define o_file_size_kb int;
define o_dt_created datetime year to second;
define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);

--on exception
--	rollback work;
--end exception;
--
--begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pg
where task_status = 'O'
and recon_status = 'PE';

if o_exist > 0 then

    -- create a temporary table
    create temp table temppg (
        rc_pg_id int8
    );

    -- select related fields
    insert into temppg (rc_pg_id)
    select rc_pg_id
    from rms_rc_pg
    where task_status = 'O'
    and recon_status = 'PE';

    foreach c_getpgdoc for
        select rc_pg_id,file_nm, file_content
        into    o_rc_pg_id,o_file_nm, o_file_content
        from rms_rc_pgdoc
        where rc_pg_id in (select rc_pg_id from temppg)

        return  o_rc_pg_id,o_file_nm, o_file_content with resume;
    end foreach

drop table temppg;

end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getPGReconDetail(i_task_id nvarchar(25))
returning 
		integer as pg_txn_settlement_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_total_txn_settlement_amt,
        integer as pg_txn_adj_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_total_txn_adj_amt,
        decimal(16,2) as pg_total_txn_other,
        integer as pg_found_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_found_total,
        integer as pg_not_found_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_not_found_total,
        integer as pg_sam_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_sam_total,
        integer as pg_snm_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_snm_total,
        integer as pg_txf_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_txf_total,
        integer as pg_matched_no,
		decimal(16,2) as pg_matched_total,
        integer as rms_txn_no,
        integer as rms_paid_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_paid_total,
        integer as rms_failed_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_failed_total,
        integer as rms_rcpt_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_rcpt_total,
        integer as rms_sam_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_sam_total,
        integer as rms_snm_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_snm_total,
        integer as rms_txf_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_txf_total,
        integer as rms_cip_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_cip_total,
        integer as rms_ncp_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_ncp_total,
        integer as rms_nfp_no,
		decimal(16,2) as rms_nfp_total,
        nvarchar(25) as task_id,
		nvarchar(100) as recon_status,
        nvarchar(100) as dt_statement,
		nvarchar(100) as dt_settlement_char,
        nvarchar(255) as remarks,
        nvarchar(100) as task_status;

    -- payment gateway settlement summary
    define pg_txn_settlement_no integer;
    define pg_total_txn_settlement_amt decimal(16,2);
    define pg_txn_adj_no integer;
    define pg_total_txn_adj_amt decimal(16,2);
    define pg_total_txn_other decimal(16,2);

    -- discrepancy check  based on payment gateway settlement
    define pg_matched_no integer;
    define pg_matched_total decimal(16,2);
    define pg_found_no integer;
    define pg_found_total decimal(16,2);
    define pg_not_found_no integer;
    define pg_not_found_total decimal(16,2);
    define pg_sam_no integer;
    define pg_sam_total decimal(16,2);
    define pg_snm_no integer;
    define pg_snm_total decimal(16,2);
    define pg_txf_no integer;
    define pg_txf_total decimal(16,2);

    -- rms source system summary
    define rms_txn_no integer;
    define rms_paid_no integer;
    define rms_paid_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_failed_no integer;
    define rms_failed_total decimal(16,2);

    -- discrepancy check based on rms source system
    define rms_rcpt_no integer;
    define rms_rcpt_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_sam_no integer;
    define rms_sam_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_snm_no integer;
    define rms_snm_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_txf_no integer;
    define rms_txf_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_cip_no integer;
    define rms_cip_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_ncp_no integer;
    define rms_ncp_total decimal(16,2);
    define rms_nfp_no integer;
    define rms_nfp_total decimal(16,2);

    -- reconciliation task
    define task_id nvarchar(25);
    define recon_status nvarchar(100);
    define o_dt_statement nvarchar(100);
    define dt_settlement_char nvarchar(100);
    define o_dt_settlement date;
    define o_remarks nvarchar(255);
    define task_status nvarchar(100);

    -- get dt_settlement
    let o_dt_settlement =(select dt_settlement
                            from rms_rc_pg
                            where task_no = i_task_id);

    -- payment gateway settlement summary
    SELECT 
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd = 'Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS settlement_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd = 'Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS settlement_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd = 'Txn Adjustment' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS adjustment_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd = 'Txn Adjustment' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS adjustment_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd NOT IN ('Settlement', 'Txn Adjustment') THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS other_sum
    into pg_txn_settlement_no,pg_total_txn_settlement_amt,pg_txn_adj_no,pg_total_txn_adj_amt,pg_total_txn_other
    FROM 
        rms_rc_pgtxn a
    left join rms_rc_pg b on a.rc_pg_id=b.rc_pg_id
    WHERE 
        b.task_no = i_task_id;

    -- discrepancy check  based on payment gateway settlement
    SELECT 
        SUM(CASE WHEN found_in_rms = 1 and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS found_in_rms_1_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN found_in_rms = 1 and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS found_in_rms_1_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN found_in_rms = 0 and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS found_in_rms_0_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN found_in_rms = 0 and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS found_in_rms_0_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'SAM' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS sam_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'SAM' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS sam_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'SNM' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS snm_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'SNM' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS snm_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'TXF' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS txf_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN sub_criteria = 'TXF' and txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS txf_sum,
        COUNT(*) AS total_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN txn_cd=='Settlement' THEN txn_amt ELSE 0 END) AS total_sum
    into pg_found_no,pg_found_total,pg_not_found_no,pg_not_found_total,pg_sam_no,pg_sam_total,pg_snm_no,pg_snm_total,pg_txf_no,pg_txf_total,pg_matched_no,pg_matched_total
    FROM 
        rms_rc_pg
    INNER JOIN 
        rms_rc_pgtxn ON rms_rc_pg.rc_pg_id = rms_rc_pgtxn.rc_pg_id
    WHERE 
        rms_rc_pg.task_no = i_task_id
        and rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_cd=='Settlement';
    
    -- rms source system summary

    select COUNT(*) as total_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN t2.order_status = 'P' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as paid_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN t2.order_status = 'P' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) as paid_total,
    SUM(CASE WHEN t2.order_status = 'F' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as fail_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN t2.order_status = 'F' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) as fail_total
    into rms_txn_no,rms_paid_no,rms_paid_total,rms_failed_no,rms_failed_total
    from rms_mtt_pg t1
    inner join rms_mtt t2 on t1.mtt_id=t2.mtt_id
    where date(pg_resp_time) = o_dt_settlement;

    -- discrepancy check based on rms source system
    SELECT 
        COUNT(*) AS total_count,
        SUM(pg_pymt_amt) AS total_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'SAM' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS sam_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'SAM' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS sam_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'SNM' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS snm_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'SNM' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS snm_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'TXF' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS txf_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'TXF' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS txf_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'CIP' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS cip_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'CIP' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS cip_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'NCP' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS ncp_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'NCP' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS ncp_sum,
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'NFP' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS nfp_count, --NFP
        SUM(CASE WHEN rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'NFP' THEN pg_pymt_amt ELSE 0 END) AS nfp_sum --NFP
    INTO rms_rcpt_no,rms_rcpt_total,rms_sam_no,rms_sam_total,rms_snm_no,rms_snm_total,rms_txf_no,rms_txf_total,rms_cip_no,rms_cip_total,rms_ncp_no,rms_ncp_total,rms_nfp_no,rms_nfp_total
    FROM 
        rms_mtt_pg
    INNER JOIN 
        rms_rc_pgmtt ON rms_rc_pgmtt.mtt_pg_id = rms_mtt_pg.mtt_pg_id
    --INNER JOIN 
    --    rms_mtt_rcpt ON rms_mtt_rcpt.mtt_pg_id = rms_mtt_pg.mtt_pg_id
    WHERE 
        --date(rms_mtt_rcpt.rcpt_dt) = o_dt_settlement
        date(pg_resp_time) = o_dt_settlement
        and rms_rc_pgmtt.status='A';

    -- reconciliation task
    select task_no,b.nm_en,TO_CHAR(dt_statement, '%d %b %Y'),TO_CHAR(dt_settlement, '%d %b %Y'),remarks,c.nm_en
    into task_id,recon_status,o_dt_statement,dt_settlement_char,o_remarks,task_status
    from rms_rc_pg a
    left join rms_param b on a.recon_status=b.param_cd and b.param_grp_nm = 'Status-PGRC'
    left join rms_param c on a.task_status=c.param_cd and c.param_grp_nm = 'Status-Task'
    where task_no = i_task_id;

	return pg_txn_settlement_no,pg_total_txn_settlement_amt,pg_txn_adj_no,pg_total_txn_adj_amt,pg_total_txn_other,
    pg_found_no,pg_found_total,pg_not_found_no,pg_not_found_total,pg_sam_no,pg_sam_total,pg_snm_no,pg_snm_total,pg_txf_no,pg_txf_total,pg_matched_no,pg_matched_total,
    rms_txn_no,rms_paid_no,rms_paid_total,rms_failed_no,rms_failed_total,
    rms_rcpt_no,rms_rcpt_total,rms_sam_no,rms_sam_total,rms_snm_no,rms_snm_total,rms_txf_no,rms_txf_total,rms_cip_no,rms_cip_total,rms_ncp_no,rms_ncp_total,rms_nfp_no,rms_nfp_total,
    task_id,recon_status,o_dt_statement,dt_settlement_char,o_remarks,task_status;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getPGReconList(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_task_id nvarchar(25), i_file_nm nvarchar(255), i_dt_settlement_fr nvarchar(100),i_dt_settlement_to nvarchar(100), 
                            i_dt_uploaded_fr nvarchar(100),i_dt_uploaded_to nvarchar(100),
                            i_merchant_id nvarchar(25), i_task_status nvarchar(25), i_recon_status nvarchar(25))
returning 
		nvarchar(25) as i_task_id,
		nvarchar(255) as i_file_nm,
        nvarchar(100) as i_dt_settlement,
        nvarchar(100) as i_dt_uploaded,
		nvarchar(25) as i_merchant_id, 
		nvarchar(50) as i_task_status,
		nvarchar(50) as i_recon_status,
		integer as total;

    define total integer;
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define o_task_id nvarchar(25);
	define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_dt_settlement nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_uploaded nvarchar(100);
	define o_merchant_id nvarchar(25);
	define o_task_status nvarchar(50);
	define o_recon_status nvarchar(50);

    if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
        raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
    end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1)
                from rms_rc_pg a
                left join rms_rc_pgdoc b on a.rc_pg_id=b.rc_pg_id
                where (i_task_id is null or a.task_no like '%' || i_task_id || '%')
                and (i_dt_settlement_fr is null or a.dt_settlement >= to_date(i_dt_settlement_fr,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                and (i_dt_settlement_to is null or a.dt_settlement <= to_date(i_dt_settlement_to,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                and (i_dt_uploaded_fr is null or a.dt_upload >= to_date(i_dt_uploaded_fr,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                and (i_dt_uploaded_to is null or a.dt_upload <= to_date(i_dt_uploaded_to,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                and (i_merchant_id is null or a.merchant_id like '%' || i_merchant_id || '%')
                and (i_task_status is null or a.task_status=i_task_status)
                and (i_recon_status is null or a.recon_status=i_recon_status)
                and (i_file_nm is null or b.file_nm like '%' || i_file_nm || '%')
        			);

	foreach c_getripl for
        
        select skip calculatedpage limit i_size a.task_no, b.file_nm,TO_CHAR(a.dt_settlement, '%d %b %Y'),TO_CHAR(a.dt_upload, '%d %b %Y'),a.merchant_id,c.nm_en,d.nm_en
        into o_task_id, o_file_nm,o_dt_settlement,o_dt_uploaded,o_merchant_id,o_task_status,o_recon_status
        from rms_rc_pg a
        left join rms_rc_pgdoc b on a.rc_pg_id=b.rc_pg_id
        left join rms_param c on a.task_status = c.param_cd and c.param_grp_nm='Status-Task'
        left join rms_param d on a.recon_status = d.param_cd and d.param_grp_nm='Status-PGRC'
        where (i_task_id is null or a.task_no like '%' || i_task_id || '%')
        and (i_dt_settlement_fr is null or a.dt_settlement >= to_date(i_dt_settlement_fr,'%Y-%m-%d'))
        and (i_dt_settlement_to is null or a.dt_settlement <= to_date(i_dt_settlement_to,'%Y-%m-%d'))
        and (i_dt_uploaded_fr is null or a.dt_upload >= to_date(i_dt_uploaded_fr,'%Y-%m-%d'))
        and (i_dt_uploaded_to is null or a.dt_upload <= to_date(i_dt_uploaded_to,'%Y-%m-%d'))
        and (i_merchant_id is null or a.merchant_id like '%' || i_merchant_id || '%')
        and (i_task_status is null or a.task_status=i_task_status)
        and (i_recon_status is null or a.recon_status=i_recon_status)
        and (i_file_nm is null or b.file_nm like '%' || i_file_nm || '%')
        order by a.dt_upload desc
	
		return o_task_id, o_file_nm,o_dt_settlement,o_dt_uploaded,o_merchant_id,o_task_status,o_recon_status,total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getPGSettlementDate()
returning nvarchar (100) as o_dt_settlement;

	define o_dt_settlement nvarchar(100);
 
	foreach c_getPGSettlementDate for	
		select distinct TO_CHAR(t1.dt_settlement, '%d/%m/%Y') as formatted_date
        into o_dt_settlement
		from rms_rc_pg t1
		where t1.task_status = 'CS'
		  and t1.dt_settlement not in (
            select t2.dt_settlement
            from rms_rc_bank t1
            inner join rms_rc_pg t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
            where t1.task_status <> 'CL'
          )

		return o_dt_settlement with resume;
	end foreach;
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getrcbank()
returning int8 as rc_bank_id,
          int8 as rc_bankdoc_id,
          nvarchar(255) as file_nm,      
          nvarchar(25) as file_type;

define o_rc_bank_id int8;
define o_rc_bankdoc_id int8;
define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_file_type nvarchar(25);

foreach c_getrcbank for

    select t1.rc_bank_id, t2.rc_bankdoc_id, t2.file_nm, t2.file_type
    into o_rc_bank_id, o_rc_bankdoc_id, o_file_nm, o_file_type
    from rms_rc_bank t1
    inner join rms_rc_bankdoc t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
    --inner join rms_rc_pg t3 on t1.task_no = t3.task_no
    where t1.task_status = 'O'
    --and t3.task_status = 'PE'
    and t1.recon_status = 'PE'

    return o_rc_bank_id,o_rc_bankdoc_id,o_file_nm,o_file_type with resume;

end foreach;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getrcbankdetails(i_task_no nvarchar(25))
returning nvarchar(255) as file_nm,
          int as total_no_pg_txn,
          decimal(15,2) as total_gross_amt,
          decimal(15,2) as total_mdr,
          decimal(15,2) as total_net_amt,

          int as total_no_bk_txn,
          int as total_bank_txn,
          int as total_pg_file_txn,
          decimal(15,2) as total_pg_disbursed_amt,

          nvarchar(25) as task_no,
          nvarchar(50) as recon_status,
          nvarchar(50) as task_status,
          nvarchar(25) as remarks,
          nvarchar(25) as stmt_no,
          date as dt_settlement;

define o_file_nm nvarchar(255);
define o_total_no_pg_txn int;
define o_total_gross_amt decimal(15,2);
define o_total_mdr decimal(15,2);
define o_total_net_amt decimal(15,2);
define o_total_no_bk_txn int;
define o_total_bank_txn int;
define o_total_pg_file_txn int;
define o_total_pg_disbursed_amt decimal(15,2);
define o_task_no nvarchar(25);
define o_task_status nvarchar(50);
define o_recon_status nvarchar(50);
define o_stmt_no nvarchar(25);
define o_dt_settlement date;
define o_remarks nvarchar(25);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;

-- PG Settlement Summary
-- File name
select t2.file_nm
into o_file_nm
from rms_rc_bank t1
inner join rms_rc_pgdoc t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
where t1.task_no = i_task_no;

-- Total number of txn, Total Gross Amount, Total MDR, Total Net Amount
select count(t2.txn_id), sum(t2.txn_amt), sum(t2.mdr_amt), sum(t2.txn_amt) - ABS(sum(t2.mdr_amt))
into o_total_no_pg_txn, o_total_gross_amt, o_total_mdr,  o_total_net_amt
from rms_rc_bank t1
inner join rms_rc_pgtxn t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
where t1.task_no = i_task_no
and t2.txn_cd = 'Settlement';

-- Bank Statement Summary
-- No of Bank stmt, All Bank Txn
select count(t2.rc_bank_id)
into o_total_no_bk_txn
from rms_rc_bankdoc t1
inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
where t2.task_no = i_task_no;

-- No of Bank stmt, All Bank Txn
select count(t3.rc_banktxn_id)
into o_total_bank_txn
from rms_rc_bankdoc t1
inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
inner join rms_rc_banktxn t3 on t1.rc_bank_id = t3.rc_bank_id
where t2.task_no = i_task_no;

-- Select PG total credit in related
select count(t1.rc_banktxn_id),sum(t1.credit) - ABS(o_total_mdr)
into o_total_pg_file_txn, o_total_pg_disbursed_amt
from rms_rc_banktxn t1
inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
where t2.task_no = i_task_no
and substring(t1.txn_ref from 0 for 14) in (select stmt_no 
                                            from rms_rc_pg t1
                                            inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id);
--and t1.status = 'SBSR';

-- Recon Bank
-- Select rc_bank
select t1.task_no, t4.nm_en, t3.nm_en, t1.remarks, t2.stmt_no, t2.dt_settlement
into o_task_no, o_recon_status, o_task_status, o_remarks, o_stmt_no, o_dt_settlement
from rms_rc_bank t1
left outer join rms_rc_pg t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id
inner join rms_param t3 on t1.task_status = t3.param_cd and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status-Task'
inner join rms_param t4 on t1.recon_status = t4.param_cd and t4.param_grp_nm = 'Status-BRC'
where t1.task_no = i_task_no;

commit work;

return o_file_nm, o_total_no_pg_txn, o_total_gross_amt, o_total_mdr, o_total_net_amt,
        o_total_no_bk_txn, o_total_bank_txn, o_total_pg_file_txn, o_total_pg_disbursed_amt, 
         o_task_no, o_recon_status, o_task_status, o_remarks, o_stmt_no, o_dt_settlement;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getrcbankdoc(i_rc_bankdoc_id int8)
returning blob as file_content;

into o_file_content
from rms_rc_bankdoc
where rc_bankdoc_id = i_rc_bankdoc_id;

return o_file_content;

end procedure;

inner join rms_rc_bank t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id and t2.task_no = i_task_no and t1.file_nm = i_file_nm;

return o_file_content;

end procedure;

into o_file_content
from rms_rc_pg t1 join rms_rc_pgdoc t2 on t1.rc_pg_id = t2.rc_pg_id 
where t1.task_no = i_task_no;

return o_file_content;

end procedure;

create or replace procedure sp_getRICP(
    i_page INTEGER,
    i_size INTEGER,
    i_ricp_id integer,
    i_entity_type nvarchar(50),
    i_entity_no nvarchar(40),
    i_cp_no nvarchar(40),
    i_dt_issuance date,
    i_dt_expiry date,
    i_cp_amt decimal(16,2),
    i_accr_amt decimal(16,2),
    i_cp_tier integer,
    i_cp_tier_amt decimal(16,2),
    i_status nvarchar(10)
)
returning 
    integer as ricp_id,
    nvarchar(20) as txn_type,
    nvarchar(50) as entity_type,
    nvarchar(20) as entity_no,
    nvarchar(20) as calendar_yr,
    nvarchar(20) as cp_no, 
    nvarchar(20) as cp_act_id, 
    nvarchar(20) as cp_sect_id, 
    nvarchar(20) as cp_sub_sect_id, 
    datetime year to second as dt_issuance, 
    datetime year to second as dt_expiry, 
    datetime year to second as dt_void, 
    datetime year to second as dt_cancel, 
    datetime year to second as dt_writeoff, 
    decimal(16,2) as cp_amt, 
    decimal(16,2) as accr_amt, 
    datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
    datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, 
    nvarchar(25) as created_by, 
    nvarchar(25) as modified_by, 	
    nvarchar(50) as status, 
    int as cp_tier, 
    decimal(16,2) as cp_tier_amt,
    int as total;

define o_ricp_id integer;
define o_txn_type nvarchar(20);
define o_entity_type nvarchar(50);
define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
define o_calendar_yr nvarchar(20);
define o_cp_no nvarchar(20);
define o_cp_act_id nvarchar(20); 
define o_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20);
define o_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
define o_dt_issuance datetime year to second;
define o_dt_expiry datetime year to second;
define o_dt_void datetime year to second;
define o_dt_cancel datetime year to second;
define o_dt_writeoff datetime year to second;
define o_cp_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_accr_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
define o_created_by nvarchar(25); 
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25); 	
define o_status nvarchar(50); 
define o_cp_tier int; 
define o_cp_tier_amt decimal(16,2);
define calculatedPage int;
define total int;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_size < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null or invalid integer";
end if

let calculatedPage = (i_page - 1) * i_size;
let total = (select count(1) 
             from rms_ricp t1
             left outer join rms_param t2 on t1.entity_type = t2.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.txn_type = t3.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t4 on t1.status = t4.param_cd
             
              where (i_ricp_id is null or ricp_id=i_ricp_id)
        				  and (i_entity_type is null or entity_type like '%' || i_entity_type || '%')
                          and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no  like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
                          and (i_cp_no is null or cp_no like '%' || i_cp_no || '%')
                          
                          and (i_dt_issuance is null or dt_issuance = i_dt_issuance)
                          and (i_dt_expiry is null or dt_expiry = i_dt_expiry)
                     
                          and (i_cp_amt is null or cp_amt = i_cp_amt)
                          and (i_accr_amt is null or accr_amt = i_accr_amt)
                          and (i_cp_tier is null or cp_tier = i_cp_tier)
                          and (i_cp_tier_amt is null or cp_tier_amt = i_cp_tier_amt)
                          and (i_status is null or t1.status  like '%' || i_status || '%')
                          and t2.param_grp_nm = 'EntityType'
                          and t3.param_grp_nm = 'RICP-TxnType'
                          and t4.param_grp_nm = 'RICP-Status'
                          
                          
                          
         
            );

foreach c_getricp for
    select skip calculatedPage limit i_size 
           t1.ricp_id, 
           t3.nm_en, 
           t2.nm_en,
           t1.entity_no, 
           t1.calendar_yr, 
           t1.cp_no, 
           t1.cp_act_id, 
           t1.cp_sect_id,
           t1.cp_sub_sect_id, 
           t1.dt_issuance, 
           t1.dt_expiry, 
           t1.dt_void, 
           t1.dt_cancel, 
           t1.dt_writeoff, 
           t1.cp_amt,
           t1.accr_amt,
           t1.dt_created, 
           t1.dt_modified, 
           t1.created_by, 
           t1.modified_by,  
           t4.nm_en, 
           t1.cp_tier, 
           t1.cp_tier_amt
    into o_ricp_id, 
         o_txn_type,
         o_entity_type,
         o_entity_no,
         o_calendar_yr,
         o_cp_no,
         o_cp_act_id,
         o_cp_sect_id,
         o_cp_sub_sect_id,
         o_dt_issuance,
         o_dt_expiry,
         o_dt_void,
         o_dt_cancel,
         o_dt_writeoff,
         o_cp_amt,
         o_accr_amt,
         o_dt_created,
         o_dt_modified,
         o_created_by,
         o_modified_by,
         o_status,
         o_cp_tier,
         o_cp_tier_amt
    from rms_ricp t1
             left outer join rms_param t2 on t1.entity_type = t2.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.txn_type = t3.param_cd
             left outer join rms_param t4 on t1.status = t4.param_cd
             
              where (i_ricp_id is null or ricp_id=i_ricp_id)
        				  and (i_entity_type is null or entity_type like '%' || i_entity_type || '%')
                          and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no  like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
                          and (i_cp_no is null or cp_no like '%' || i_cp_no || '%')
                          
                          and (i_dt_issuance is null or dt_issuance = i_dt_issuance)
                          and (i_dt_expiry is null or dt_expiry = i_dt_expiry)
                     
                          and (i_cp_amt is null or cp_amt = i_cp_amt)
                          and (i_accr_amt is null or accr_amt = i_accr_amt)
                          and (i_cp_tier is null or cp_tier = i_cp_tier)
                          and (i_cp_tier_amt is null or cp_tier_amt = i_cp_tier_amt)
                          and (i_status is null or t1.status  like '%' || i_status || '%')
                          and t2.param_grp_nm = 'EntityType'
                          and t3.param_grp_nm = 'RICP-TxnType'
                          and t4.param_grp_nm = 'RICP-Status'
                          order by T1.dt_modified desc
                          
                          
             

return o_ricp_id, 
         o_txn_type,
         o_entity_type,
         o_entity_no,
         o_calendar_yr,
         o_cp_no,
         o_cp_act_id,
         o_cp_sect_id,
         o_cp_sub_sect_id,
         o_dt_issuance,
         o_dt_expiry,
         o_dt_void,
         o_dt_cancel,
         o_dt_writeoff,
         o_cp_amt,
         o_accr_amt,
         o_dt_created,
         o_dt_modified,
         o_created_by,
         o_modified_by,
         o_status,
         o_cp_tier,
         o_cp_tier_amt, 
         total WITH RESUME;

end foreach

end procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getricpidsbycpno (i_cp_no nvarchar(20))
returning integer as ricp_id;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id INTO o_ricp_id FROM rms_ricp
    		WHERE cp_no=i_cp_no
   		RETURN o_ricp_id with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getricpidsbyfilter (i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_no nvarchar(20), i_status nvarchar(10))
returning integer as ricp_id;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id INTO o_ricp_id FROM rms_ricp
    		WHERE status = i_status and entity_type=i_entity_type and entity_no=i_entity_no and cp_no=i_cp_no
   		RETURN o_ricp_id with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getricpidsbyfilterwostatus (i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_no nvarchar(20))
returning integer as ricp_id;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id INTO o_ricp_id FROM rms_ricp
    		WHERE entity_type=i_entity_type and entity_no=i_entity_no and cp_no=i_cp_no
   		RETURN o_ricp_id with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
