create or replace procedure sp_getricpwriteoffs (i_status nvarchar(10))
returning integer as ricp_id, nvarchar(20) as txn_type, nvarchar(1) as entity_type,nvarchar(20) as entity_no, nvarchar(5) as calendar_yr,
nvarchar(20) as cp_no, nvarchar(20) as cp_act_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sect_id, nvarchar(20) as cp_sub_sect_id, date as dt_issuance, date as dt_expiry,
date as dt_void, date as dt_cancel, date as dt_writeoff, decimal as cp_amt, decimal as accr_amt, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as cp_tier, decimal as cp_tier_amt;

	DEFINE o_ricp_id integer;
	DEFINE o_txn_type nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_entity_type nvarchar(1); 
	DEFINE o_entity_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_calendar_yr nvarchar(5); 
	DEFINE o_cp_no nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_act_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20); 
	DEFINE o_dt_issuance date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_expiry date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_void date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_cancel date; 
	DEFINE o_dt_writeoff date; 
	DEFINE o_cp_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_accr_amt decimal; 
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25); 
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10); 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier integer; 
	DEFINE o_cp_tier_amt decimal;
	
	FOREACH cursor1 for
		select ricp_id,txn_type,entity_type,entity_no,calendar_yr,cp_no,cp_act_id,cp_sect_id,cp_sub_sect_id,dt_issuance,
		dt_expiry,dt_void,dt_cancel,dt_writeoff,cp_amt,accr_amt,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,cp_tier,
		cp_tier_amt
		INTO o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt
		FROM rms_ricp WHERE status = i_status and TODAY >= dt_writeoff
   		
		RETURN o_ricp_id,o_txn_type,o_entity_type,o_entity_no,o_calendar_yr,o_cp_no,o_cp_act_id,o_cp_sect_id,o_cp_sub_sect_id,
			o_dt_issuance,o_dt_expiry,o_dt_void,o_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,o_cp_amt,o_accr_amt,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,
			o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_cp_tier,o_cp_tier_amt with resume;
  	end foreach
END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getRIPL(i_page integer, i_size integer, i_ripl_id int8, i_txn_type nvarchar(5), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(40),
                            i_calendar_yr nvarchar(5), i_dt_due nvarchar(100), i_ripl_ctype nvarchar(10),i_status nvarchar(10))
returning 
		int8 as ripl_id,
		nvarchar(50) as txn_type,
        nvarchar(50) as entity_type,
        nvarchar(40) as entity_no,
		nvarchar(5) as calendar_yr, 
		nvarchar(100) as dt_due, 
		nvarchar(100) as dt_impair,
		nvarchar(100) as dt_writeoff,
		nvarchar(10) as company_type,
		decimal (16,2) as o_accr_amt,
		nvarchar (20) as rcpt_no,
		nvarchar (100) as dt_created,
		nvarchar(50) as status,
		integer as total;

    define total integer;
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define o_ripl_id int8;
	define o_txn_type nvarchar(50);
	define o_entity_type nvarchar(50);
	define o_entity_no nvarchar(40);
	define o_calendar_yr nvarchar(5);
	define o_dt_due nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_impair nvarchar(100);
	define o_dt_writeoff nvarchar(100);
	define o_ripl_ctype nvarchar(10);
	define o_accr_amt decimal(16,2);	
	define o_rcpt_no nvarchar(20);
	define o_dt_created nvarchar(100);
	define o_status nvarchar(50);

    if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
        raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
    end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_ripl
        			where (i_ripl_id is null or ripl_id=i_ripl_id)
        				  and (i_txn_type is null or txn_type==i_txn_type)
                          and (i_entity_type is null or entity_type==i_entity_type)
                          and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
                          and (i_calendar_yr is null or calendar_yr like '%' || i_calendar_yr || '%')
                          and (i_ripl_ctype is null or ripl_ctype like '%' || i_ripl_ctype || '%')
                          and (i_dt_due is null or dt_due==to_date(i_dt_due,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                          and (i_status is null or status==i_status)
        			);

	foreach c_getripl for
        select  skip calculatedpage limit i_size T1.ripl_id,T4.nm_en,T3.nm_en,entity_no,calendar_yr,ripl_ctype,TO_CHAR(dt_due, '%d %b %Y'),TO_CHAR(dt_impair, '%d %b %Y'),TO_CHAR(dt_writeoff, '%d %b %Y'),accr_amt,rcpt_no,TO_CHAR(T1.dt_created, '%d %b %Y %H:%M:%S'),T2.nm_en
        into o_ripl_id,o_txn_type, o_entity_type, o_entity_no, o_calendar_yr, o_ripl_ctype, o_dt_due, o_dt_impair, o_dt_writeoff, o_accr_amt, o_rcpt_no, o_dt_created, o_status
        from rms_ripl T1
        left join rms_param T2 on T1.status = T2.param_cd and T2.param_grp_nm='Status-RIPL'
        left join rms_param T3 on T1.entity_type= T3.param_cd and T3.param_grp_nm='EntityType'
        left join rms_param T4 on T1.txn_type= T4.param_cd and T4.param_grp_nm='RIPL-TxnType'
        where (i_ripl_id is null or ripl_id=i_ripl_id)
        		and (i_txn_type is null or (txn_type==i_txn_type))
                and (i_entity_type is null or (entity_type==i_entity_type))
                and (i_entity_no is null or entity_no like '%' || i_entity_no || '%')
                and (i_calendar_yr is null or calendar_yr like '%' || i_calendar_yr || '%')
                and (i_ripl_ctype is null or ripl_ctype like '%' || i_ripl_ctype || '%')
                and (i_dt_due is null or dt_due==to_date(i_dt_due,'%Y-%m-%d'))
                and (i_status is null or (T1.status==i_status ))
        order by T1.dt_modified desc
	
		return o_ripl_id,o_txn_type, o_entity_type, o_entity_no, o_calendar_yr, o_dt_due, o_dt_impair, o_dt_writeoff, o_ripl_ctype, o_accr_amt, o_rcpt_no, o_dt_created, o_status, total with resume;
	end foreach

end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getriplagequeuerpt()

returning integer;

define o_count integer;

	select count(1) into o_count 
	from rms_rpt_ripl_age 
	where status = "P" or status = "I";

	return o_count with resume;

end procedure;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getriplaging (
	i_page int, 
	i_size int,
    i_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8,
    i_p_dt_req DATE,
    i_p_imp_status INT,
    i_p_exp_status INT,
    i_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1),
    i_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(200),
    i_p_dt_due_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_due_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_imp_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_imp_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_wo_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_wo_to DATE,
    i_created_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_status NVARCHAR(10),
    i_p_email NVARCHAR(255),
    i_p_file_type NVARCHAR(5)
)
RETURNING
    INT8 AS rpt_ripl_age_id,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_req,
    INT AS p_imp_status,
    INT AS p_exp_status,
    NVARCHAR(1) AS p_ent_ty,
    NVARCHAR(100) AS p_ent_nm,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_created,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_modified,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS status,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS p_email,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS p_file_type,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS task_id,
    INT AS total;

DEFINE o_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8;
DEFINE o_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_imp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_exp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1);
DEFINE o_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_status NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_p_email NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_p_file_type NVARCHAR(50);
define calculatedpage int;
DEFINE total INT;

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;

LET total = (SELECT COUNT(1)
             FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
             WHERE (i_rpt_ripl_age_id IS NULL OR t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id)
               AND (i_p_dt_req IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_req = i_p_dt_req)
               AND (i_p_imp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_imp_status = i_p_imp_status)
               AND (i_p_exp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_exp_status = i_p_exp_status)
               AND (i_p_ent_ty IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_ty like '%' || i_p_ent_nm ||'%')
               AND (i_p_ent_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_nm = i_p_ent_nm)
               AND (i_p_dt_due_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_fr >= i_p_dt_due_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_due_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_to <= i_p_dt_due_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr >= i_p_dt_rcpt_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_to <= i_p_dt_rcpt_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_imp_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_fr >= i_p_dt_imp_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_imp_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_to <= i_p_dt_imp_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_wo_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_fr >= i_p_dt_wo_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_wo_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_to <= i_p_dt_wo_to)
               AND (i_created_by IS NULL OR t1.created_by = i_created_by)
               AND (i_modified_by IS NULL OR t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
               AND (i_status IS NULL OR t1.status = i_status)
               AND (i_p_email IS NULL OR t1.p_email = i_p_email)
               AND (i_p_file_type IS NULL OR t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type));
			   
if i_size is not null then  

FOREACH c_getriplaging FOR
    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.rpt_ripl_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_imp_status, t1.p_exp_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm,
           t1.p_dt_due_fr, t1.p_dt_due_to, t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr, t1.p_dt_rcpt_to, t1.p_dt_imp_fr, t1.p_dt_imp_to,
           t1.p_dt_wo_fr, t1.p_dt_wo_to, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by,
           t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type
    INTO o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
         o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
         o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
         o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type
    FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
    WHERE (i_rpt_ripl_age_id IS NULL OR t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id)
      AND (i_p_dt_req IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_req <= i_p_dt_req)
      AND (i_p_imp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_imp_status = i_p_imp_status)
      AND (i_p_exp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_exp_status = i_p_exp_status)
      AND (i_p_ent_ty IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
      AND (i_p_ent_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_nm = i_p_ent_nm)
      AND (i_p_dt_due_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_fr = i_p_dt_due_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_due_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_to = i_p_dt_due_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr = i_p_dt_rcpt_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_to = i_p_dt_rcpt_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_fr = i_p_dt_imp_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_to = i_p_dt_imp_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_fr = i_p_dt_wo_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_to = i_p_dt_wo_to)
      AND (i_created_by IS NULL OR t1.created_by = i_created_by)
      AND (i_modified_by IS NULL OR t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
      AND (i_status IS NULL OR t1.status = i_status)
      AND (i_p_email IS NULL OR t1.p_email = i_p_email)
      AND (i_p_file_type IS NULL OR t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type)
    ORDER BY t1.dt_modified DESC

    RETURN o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
           o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
           o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
           o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_ripl_age_id,6,'0'), total WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH

ELSE
foreach c_getriplaging for
	SELECT t1.rpt_ripl_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_imp_status, t1.p_exp_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm,
           t1.p_dt_due_fr, t1.p_dt_due_to, t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr, t1.p_dt_rcpt_to, t1.p_dt_imp_fr, t1.p_dt_imp_to,
           t1.p_dt_wo_fr, t1.p_dt_wo_to, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by,
           t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type
    INTO o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
         o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
         o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
         o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type
    FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
    WHERE (i_rpt_ripl_age_id IS NULL OR t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id)
      AND (i_p_dt_req IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_req <= i_p_dt_req)
      AND (i_p_imp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_imp_status = i_p_imp_status)
      AND (i_p_exp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_exp_status = i_p_exp_status)
      AND (i_p_ent_ty IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
      AND (i_p_ent_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_nm = i_p_ent_nm)
      AND (i_p_dt_due_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_fr = i_p_dt_due_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_due_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_to = i_p_dt_due_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr = i_p_dt_rcpt_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_to = i_p_dt_rcpt_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_fr = i_p_dt_imp_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_to = i_p_dt_imp_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_fr = i_p_dt_wo_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_to = i_p_dt_wo_to)
      AND (i_created_by IS NULL OR t1.created_by = i_created_by)
      AND (i_modified_by IS NULL OR t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
      AND (i_status IS NULL OR t1.status = i_status)
      AND (i_p_email IS NULL OR t1.p_email = i_p_email)
      AND (i_p_file_type IS NULL OR t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type)
    ORDER BY t1.dt_modified DESC
	
	RETURN o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
           o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
           o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
           o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_ripl_age_id,6,'0'), total WITH RESUME;

	end foreach
end if
	
END PROCEDURE
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE sp_getriplaginglistingrpt (
    i_page int, 
    i_size int,
    i_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8,
    i_p_dt_req DATE,
    i_p_imp_status INT,
    i_p_exp_status INT,
    i_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1),
    i_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(200),
    i_p_dt_due_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_due_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_imp_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_imp_to DATE,
    i_p_dt_wo_fr DATE,
    i_p_dt_wo_to DATE,
    i_created_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_status NVARCHAR(10),
    i_p_email NVARCHAR(255), 
    i_p_file_type NVARCHAR(5),							   
    i_p_file_size int, 
    i_p_file_nm NVARCHAR(255)
)
RETURNING
    INT8 AS rpt_ripl_age_id,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_req,
    INT AS p_imp_status,
    INT AS p_exp_status,
    NVARCHAR(1) AS p_ent_ty,
    NVARCHAR(100) AS p_ent_nm,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_created,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_modified,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS status,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS p_email,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS p_file_type,
    int AS p_file_size,
    NVARCHAR(255) AS p_file_nm,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS task_id,
    INT AS total;

DEFINE o_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8;
DEFINE o_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_imp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_exp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1);
DEFINE o_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_status NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_p_email NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_p_file_type NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_p_file_size INT;
DEFINE o_p_file_nm NVARCHAR(255);
DEFINE calculatedpage INT;
DEFINE total INT;

IF (i_page IS NULL OR i_page < 1) OR (i_size IS NULL OR i_size < 1) THEN 
    RAISE EXCEPTION -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null or less than 1";
END IF

LET calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;

LET total = (SELECT COUNT(1)
             FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
             WHERE (i_rpt_ripl_age_id IS NULL OR t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id)
               AND (i_p_dt_req IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_req = i_p_dt_req)
               AND (i_p_imp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_imp_status = i_p_imp_status)
               AND (i_p_exp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_exp_status = i_p_exp_status)
               AND (i_p_ent_ty IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
               AND (i_p_ent_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_nm LIKE '%' || i_p_ent_nm ||'%')
               AND (i_p_dt_due_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_fr >= i_p_dt_due_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_due_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_to <= i_p_dt_due_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr >= i_p_dt_rcpt_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_to <= i_p_dt_rcpt_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_imp_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_fr >= i_p_dt_imp_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_imp_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_to <= i_p_dt_imp_to)
               AND (i_p_dt_wo_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_fr >= i_p_dt_wo_fr)
               AND (i_p_dt_wo_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_to <= i_p_dt_wo_to)
               AND (i_created_by IS NULL OR t1.created_by = i_created_by)
               AND (i_modified_by IS NULL OR t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
               AND (i_status IS NULL OR t1.status = i_status)
               AND (i_p_email IS NULL OR t1.p_email = i_p_email)
               AND (i_p_file_size IS NULL OR t1.p_file_size = i_p_file_size)
               AND (i_p_file_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_file_nm LIKE '%' || i_p_file_nm ||'%')
               AND (i_p_file_type IS NULL OR t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type));

FOREACH c_getriplaging FOR
    SELECT SKIP calculatedpage LIMIT i_size
           t1.rpt_ripl_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_imp_status, t1.p_exp_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm,
           t1.p_dt_due_fr, t1.p_dt_due_to, t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr, t1.p_dt_rcpt_to, t1.p_dt_imp_fr, t1.p_dt_imp_to,
           t1.p_dt_wo_fr, t1.p_dt_wo_to, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by,
           t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm 
    INTO o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
         o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
         o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
         o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm
    FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
    WHERE (i_rpt_ripl_age_id IS NULL OR t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id)
      AND (i_p_dt_req IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_req = i_p_dt_req)
      AND (i_p_imp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_imp_status = i_p_imp_status)
      AND (i_p_exp_status IS NULL OR t1.p_exp_status = i_p_exp_status)
      AND (i_p_ent_ty IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_ty = i_p_ent_ty)
      AND (i_p_ent_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_ent_nm LIKE '%' || i_p_ent_nm ||'%')
      AND (i_p_dt_due_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_fr >= i_p_dt_due_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_due_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_due_to <= i_p_dt_due_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr >= i_p_dt_rcpt_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_rcpt_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_rcpt_to <= i_p_dt_rcpt_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_fr >= i_p_dt_imp_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_imp_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_imp_to <= i_p_dt_imp_to)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_fr IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_fr >= i_p_dt_wo_fr)
      AND (i_p_dt_wo_to IS NULL OR t1.p_dt_wo_to <= i_p_dt_wo_to)
      AND (i_created_by IS NULL OR t1.created_by = i_created_by)
      AND (i_modified_by IS NULL OR t1.modified_by = i_modified_by)
      AND (i_status IS NULL OR t1.status = i_status)
      AND (i_p_email IS NULL OR t1.p_email = i_p_email)
      AND (i_p_file_size IS NULL OR t1.p_file_size = i_p_file_size)
      AND (i_p_file_nm IS NULL OR t1.p_file_nm LIKE '%' || i_p_file_nm ||'%')
      AND (i_p_file_type IS NULL OR t1.p_file_type = i_p_file_type)
    ORDER BY t1.dt_modified DESC

    RETURN o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
           o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
           o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
           o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 'RG'||LPAD(o_rpt_ripl_age_id, 6, '0'), total WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH

END PROCEDURE
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getriplagingrpt (
	i_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8
)
RETURNING
    INT8 AS rpt_ripl_age_id,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_req,
    INT AS p_imp_status,
    INT AS p_exp_status,
    NVARCHAR(1) AS p_ent_ty,
    NVARCHAR(100) AS p_ent_nm,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_due_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_rcpt_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_imp_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_fr,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS p_dt_wo_to,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_created,
    DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_modified,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS status,
    nvarchar(50) as p_email,
	nvarchar(50) as p_file_type,
	int as p_file_size,
	nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,
	nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no,
	nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no,
	nvarchar(10) as task_id;

DEFINE o_rpt_ripl_age_id INT8;
DEFINE o_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_imp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_exp_status INT;
DEFINE o_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1);
DEFINE o_p_ent_nm NVARCHAR(100);
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_due_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_imp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_status NVARCHAR(10);
define o_p_email			nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_type		nvarchar(50);
define o_p_file_size		int;
define o_p_file_nm		    nvarchar(255);
define o_p_batch_no		    nvarchar(30);
define o_p_fms_ref_no		nvarchar(25);



FOREACH c_getriplaging FOR
    select t1.rpt_ripl_age_id, t1.p_dt_req, t1.p_imp_status, t1.p_exp_status, t1.p_ent_ty, t1.p_ent_nm,
           t1.p_dt_due_fr, t1.p_dt_due_to, t1.p_dt_rcpt_fr, t1.p_dt_rcpt_to, t1.p_dt_imp_fr, t1.p_dt_imp_to,
           t1.p_dt_wo_fr, t1.p_dt_wo_to, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified, t1.created_by, t1.modified_by,
           t1.status, t1.p_email, t1.p_file_type, t1.p_file_size, t1.p_file_nm, 
	    t1.p_batch_no, t1.p_fms_ref_no
    INTO o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
         o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
         o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
         o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm,
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no
    FROM rms_rpt_ripl_age t1
    
    where t1.rpt_ripl_age_id = i_rpt_ripl_age_id	
      

    RETURN o_rpt_ripl_age_id, o_p_dt_req, o_p_imp_status, o_p_exp_status, o_p_ent_ty, o_p_ent_nm,
           o_p_dt_due_fr, o_p_dt_due_to, o_p_dt_rcpt_fr, o_p_dt_rcpt_to, o_p_dt_imp_fr, o_p_dt_imp_to,
           o_p_dt_wo_fr, o_p_dt_wo_to, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by,
           o_status, o_p_email, o_p_file_type, o_p_file_size, o_p_file_nm, 
	    o_p_batch_no, o_p_fms_ref_no, 'RG'||lpad(o_rpt_ripl_age_id,6,'0') WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH


	
END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getRIPLID()
returning int8 as result;

define o_ricp_id int8;
define o_exist int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Existing checking
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_ripl
where status in ('CA','IP');

if o_exist > 0 then

    foreach c_getripl for

    select ripl_id
    into o_ricp_id
	from rms_ripl
    where status in ('CA','IP') -- Check collectable and impair only;

    return o_ricp_id with resume;
	end foreach

end if;

commit work;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getrmsdetaillisting(i_page integer, i_size integer, 
                                        i_dt_pymt date, i_cust_nm nvarchar(50), i_fnd_in_pg nvarchar(3),
                                        i_txn_id nvarchar(30), i_orn_no nvarchar(25), i_sub_cri nvarchar(25),
                                        i_order_status nvarchar(18))
returning nvarchar(100) as dt_pymt,
          nvarchar(30) as txn_id,
          nvarchar(50) as cust_nm,
          nvarchar(25) as orn_no,
          nvarchar(3) as fnd_in_pg,
          nvarchar(50) as sub_criteria,
          decimal(15,2) as txn_amt,
          nvarchar(18) as order_status,
          int as total;

define o_dt_pymt nvarchar(100);
define o_txn_id nvarchar(30);
define o_cust_nm nvarchar(50);
define o_orn_no nvarchar(25);
define o_fnd_in_pg nvarchar(3);
define c_fnd_in_pg int;
define o_sub_cri nvarchar(50);
define o_txn_amt decimal(15,2);
define o_order_status nvarchar(18);

define calculatedpage		int;
define total	 			int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if;

begin work;
-- create a temporary table
create temp table temprms (
    dt_payment DateTime year to second,
    pg_txn_id nvarchar(30),
    cust_nm nvarchar(50),
    orn_no nvarchar(25),
    fnd_in_pg nvarchar(3),
    sub_criteria nvarchar(25),
    txn_amt decimal(15,2),
    order_status nvarchar(18)
);

-- select related fields



















insert into temprms (dt_payment, pg_txn_id, cust_nm, orn_no, fnd_in_pg, sub_criteria, txn_amt, order_status)
select
    case 
        when t1.order_status = 'P' then t2.rcpt_dt
        when t1.order_status = 'F' then (SELECT MAX(pymt_submit_dt) FROM rms_mtt_pg WHERE mtt_id = t1.mtt_id)
    end dt_payment,
        t3.pg_txn_id, t1.cust_nm, t1.orn_no, 
    t4.found_in_pg,
        t4.sub_criteria, t3.pg_pymt_amt, t1.order_status
from rms_mtt t1
left join rms_mtt_rcpt t2 on t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
left join rms_mtt_pg t3 on t1.mtt_id = t3.mtt_id
left join rms_rc_pgmtt t4 on t3.mtt_pg_id = t4.mtt_pg_id
where t1.order_status in ('P', 'F')
and t4.status='A';

let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
let total = (select count(1)
             from temprms
             where (i_dt_pymt is null or date(dt_payment) = i_dt_pymt)
             and (i_cust_nm is null or cust_nm like '%' || i_cust_nm || '%')
             and (i_fnd_in_pg is null or fnd_in_pg = i_fnd_in_pg)
             and (i_txn_id is null or pg_txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
             and (i_orn_no is null or orn_no like '%' || i_orn_no || '%')
             and (i_sub_cri is null or sub_criteria = i_sub_cri)
             and (i_order_status is null or order_status = i_order_status )
             );

foreach c_getrmsdetaillisting for

    select skip calculatedpage limit i_size dt_payment, pg_txn_id, cust_nm, orn_no,
                                    case
                                        when fnd_in_pg = 1 then 'Yes'
                                        when fnd_in_pg = 0 then 'No'
                                    end fnd_in_pg
                                    , t4.nm_en, txn_amt, t5.nm_en
    into o_dt_pymt, o_txn_id, o_cust_nm, o_orn_no, 
            o_fnd_in_pg, o_sub_cri, o_txn_amt, o_order_status
    from temprms
    left join rms_param t4 on sub_criteria = t4.param_cd and t4.param_grp_nm = 'PGRecon-RMSSubCri'
    left join rms_param t5 on order_status = t5.param_cd and t5.param_grp_nm = 'OrderStatus'
    where (i_dt_pymt is null or date(dt_payment) = i_dt_pymt)
             and (i_cust_nm is null or cust_nm like '%' || i_cust_nm || '%')
             and (i_fnd_in_pg is null or fnd_in_pg = i_fnd_in_pg )
             and (i_txn_id is null or pg_txn_id like '%' || i_txn_id || '%')
             and (i_orn_no is null or orn_no like '%' || i_orn_no || '%')
             and (i_sub_cri is null or sub_criteria =i_sub_cri)
             and (i_order_status is null or order_status = i_order_status )

    return o_dt_pymt, o_txn_id, o_cust_nm, o_orn_no, o_fnd_in_pg,
             o_sub_cri, o_txn_amt, o_order_status, total with resume;
end foreach;

drop table temprms;

commit work;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getroleperm(i_role_id integer)
	returning integer as perm_id, integer as is_allow, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;
    


    DEFINE o_perm_id integer;
    DEFINE o_is_allow integer;



	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE total integer;

	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_role_perm
        WHERE status = 'A');

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        SELECT perm_id, is_allow, status
        INTO o_perm_id, o_is_allow, o_status
        FROM rms_role_perm WHERE role_id = i_role_id

		RETURN o_perm_id, o_is_allow, o_status, total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getroles (i_page integer,i_size integer, i_r_id int8, i_r_role_nm_en nvarchar(50), i_r_role_nm_bm nvarchar(50),
										i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_status nvarchar(10))

returning 		int8 as r_id,
				nvarchar(50) as r_role_nm_en,
				nvarchar(50) as r_role_nm_bm,
				datetime year to second as dt_modified, 
				nvarchar(25) as modified_by, 
				nvarchar(10) as status,
				integer as total;

	define o_r_id int8;
	define o_r_role_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_r_role_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_role t1
					left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
        			left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
					where (i_r_role_nm_en is null or i_r_role_nm_en = '' or t1.role_nm_en = i_r_role_nm_en)
        					and (i_r_id is null or t1.role_id = i_r_id)
       						and (i_r_role_nm_bm is null or t1.role_nm_bm like '%' || i_r_role_nm_bm || '%')
       						and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        					and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        					and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        					and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                            and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
							);

	foreach c_getroles for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.role_id, t1.role_nm_en , t1.role_nm_bm, t1.dt_modified, t1.modified_by, t1.status
		into o_r_id, o_r_role_nm_en, o_r_role_nm_bm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status
	    from rms_role t1
	    left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
	    left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
	    where (i_r_role_nm_en is null or i_r_role_nm_en = '' or t1.role_nm_en = i_r_role_nm_en)
	    		and (i_r_id is null or t1.role_id = i_r_id)
	       		and (i_r_role_nm_bm is null or t1.role_nm_bm like '%' || i_r_role_nm_bm || '%')
	       		and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
	        	and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
	        	and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
	        	and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
         order by t1.role_nm_en
			return o_r_id, o_r_role_nm_en, o_r_role_nm_bm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, total with resume;
	end foreach
	
end procedure
GO

returning integer;
define o_count integer;
select count(*) into o_count from rms_rpt_ricp_age;
return o_count with resume;
END PROCEDURE;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptricpagelisting(i_page integer, i_size integer) returning 
integer as rpt_ricp_age_id, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req, integer as p_exp_status, integer as p_can_v_status, nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty, 
nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_fr, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, nvarchar(255) as p_email, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_to, nvarchar(5) as file_type, integer as p_file_size,
nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no, nvarchar(8) as task_id;

	DEFINE o_rpt_ricp_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_exp_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_can_v_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_ent_ty nvarchar(1);
	DEFINE o_p_ent_nm nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
	define o_task_id nvarchar(8);
	define calculatedpage int;

	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;
	
	if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
	    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
	end if;
	
	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;


	FOREACH c_getrptricpagelisting FOR
        select skip calculatedpage limit i_size rpt_ricp_age_id,p_dt_req,p_exp_status,p_can_v_status,p_ent_ty,p_ent_nm,p_dt_iss_fr,p_dt_iss_to,
				p_dt_exp_fr,p_dt_exp_to,p_dt_wo_fr,p_dt_wo_to,p_dt_can_fr,p_dt_can_to,p_dt_void_fr,
				p_dt_void_to,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,p_email,p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				p_dt_rcpt_to,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,p_batch_no,p_fms_ref_no,'RG' || lpad(rpt_ricp_age_id,6,'0')
        INTO o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id
        FROM rms_rpt_ricp_age order by dt_created asc
		
		RETURN o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptricpagequeue()
returning integer;
define o_count integer;
select count(*) into o_count from rms_rpt_ricp_age where status = "P" or status = "I";
return o_count with resume;
END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptricpagerq(i_rpt_ricp_age_id integer) returning  
integer as rpt_ricp_age_id, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req, integer as p_exp_status, integer as p_can_v_status, nvarchar(1) as p_ent_ty, 
nvarchar(100) as p_ent_nm, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_iss_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_exp_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_fr, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_wo_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_can_to, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_void_to, datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, nvarchar(255) as p_email, 
datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_fr, datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_rcpt_to, nvarchar(5) as file_type, integer as p_file_size,
nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no, nvarchar(8) as task_id;

	DEFINE o_rpt_ricp_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_exp_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_can_v_status integer;
	DEFINE o_p_ent_ty nvarchar(1);
	DEFINE o_p_ent_nm nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_wo_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_can_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_void_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
	define o_task_id nvarchar(8);

	FOREACH c_getrptumagerq FOR
        select rpt_ricp_age_id,p_dt_req,p_exp_status,p_can_v_status,p_ent_ty,p_ent_nm,p_dt_iss_fr,p_dt_iss_to,
				p_dt_exp_fr,p_dt_exp_to,p_dt_wo_fr,p_dt_wo_to,p_dt_can_fr,p_dt_can_to,p_dt_void_fr,
				p_dt_void_to,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,p_email,p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				p_dt_rcpt_to,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,p_batch_no,p_fms_ref_no,'RG' || lpad(rpt_ricp_age_id,6,'0')
        INTO o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id
        FROM rms_rpt_ricp_age where rpt_ricp_age_id = i_rpt_ricp_age_id
		
		RETURN o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptumage(i_rpt_um_age_id integer) returning 
integer as rpt_um_age_id,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req,nvarchar(30) as p_txn_id
,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified
,nvarchar(25) as created_by,nvarchar(25) as modified_by,nvarchar(10) as status
,nvarchar(50) as p_rcpt_no,nvarchar(50) as p_stmt_no,nvarchar(10) as p_recon_status
,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_fr,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_to
,integer as p_dup,nvarchar(255) as p_email,nvarchar(5) as p_file_type,integer as p_file_size
,nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm, nvarchar(8) as task_id, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no;

	DEFINE o_rpt_um_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_txn_id nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_rcpt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_stmt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_recon_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dup integer;
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_task_id nvarchar(8);
	define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);

	FOREACH c_getrptumage FOR
        SELECT rpt_um_age_id,p_dt_req,p_txn_id,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,
				p_rcpt_no,p_stmt_no,p_recon_status,p_dt_stmt_fr,p_dt_stmt_to,p_dup,p_email,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,
				'RG' || lpad(rpt_um_age_id,6,'0'),p_batch_no,p_fms_ref_no
        INTO o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,
			o_p_file_nm,o_task_id,o_batch_no,o_fms_ref_no
        FROM rms_rpt_um_age where rpt_um_age_id = i_rpt_um_age_id
		
		RETURN o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,
			o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_task_id,o_batch_no,o_fms_ref_no WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptumagecount()
returning integer;
define o_count integer;
select count(*) into o_count from rms_rpt_um_age;
return o_count with resume;
END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptumagelisting(i_page integer, i_size integer) returning 
integer as rpt_um_age_id,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_req,nvarchar(30) as p_txn_id
,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_created,datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified
,nvarchar(25) as created_by,nvarchar(25) as modified_by,nvarchar(10) as status
,nvarchar(50) as p_rcpt_no,nvarchar(50) as p_stmt_no,nvarchar(10) as p_recon_status
,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_fr,datetime year to fraction(5) as p_dt_stmt_to
,integer as p_dup,nvarchar(255) as p_email,nvarchar(5) as p_file_type,integer as p_file_size
,nvarchar(255) as p_file_nm,nvarchar(8) as task_id, nvarchar(30) as p_batch_no, nvarchar(25) as p_fms_ref_no;

	DEFINE o_rpt_um_age_id integer;
	DEFINE o_p_dt_req datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_txn_id nvarchar(30);
	DEFINE o_dt_created datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_rcpt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_stmt_no nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_p_recon_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_stmt_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dup integer;
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_file_type nvarchar(5);
	DEFINE o_p_file_size integer;
	DEFINE o_p_file_nm nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_task_id nvarchar(8);
	define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
	define calculatedpage int;

	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;
	
	if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
	    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
	end if;
	
	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;

	FOREACH c_getrptumagelisting FOR
        select skip calculatedpage limit i_size rpt_um_age_id,p_dt_req,p_txn_id,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,
				p_rcpt_no,p_stmt_no,p_recon_status,p_dt_stmt_fr,p_dt_stmt_to,p_dup,p_email,p_file_type,p_file_size,p_file_nm,
				'RG' || lpad(rpt_um_age_id,6,'0'), p_batch_no, p_fms_ref_no
        INTO o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,
			o_p_file_nm,o_task_id,o_batch_no,o_fms_ref_no
        FROM rms_rpt_um_age order by dt_created asc
		
		RETURN o_rpt_um_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_txn_id,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,
			o_p_rcpt_no,o_p_stmt_no,o_p_recon_status,o_p_dt_stmt_fr,o_p_dt_stmt_to,o_p_dup,o_p_email,o_p_file_type,
			o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_task_id,o_batch_no,o_fms_ref_no WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptumagequeue()
returning integer;
define o_count integer;
select count(*) into o_count from rms_rpt_um_age where status = "P" or status = "I";
return o_count with resume;
END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getrptumagerq(i_rpt_ricp_age_id integer) returning 
integer, datetime year to fraction(5), integer, integer, nvarchar(1), nvarchar(100), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), nvarchar(25), nvarchar(25), nvarchar(10), nvarchar(255), datetime year to fraction(5), datetime year to fraction(5), nvarchar(5), nvarchar(10), nvarchar(255), nvarchar(30), nvarchar(25), nvarchar(8);

	DEFINE o_rpt_ricp_age_id integer;

	DEFINE o_p_ent_nm nvarchar(100);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_iss_to datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_exp_to datetime year to fraction(5);

	DEFINE o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_status nvarchar(10);
	DEFINE o_p_email nvarchar(255);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_fr datetime year to fraction(5);
	DEFINE o_p_dt_rcpt_to datetime year to fraction(5);

        select rpt_ricp_age_id,p_dt_req,p_exp_status,p_can_v_status,p_ent_ty,p_ent_nm,p_dt_iss_fr,p_dt_iss_to,

        INTO o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id
        FROM rms_rpt_ricp_age where rpt_ricp_age_id = i_rpt_ricp_age_id
		
		RETURN o_rpt_ricp_age_id,o_p_dt_req,o_p_exp_status,o_p_can_v_status,o_p_ent_ty,o_p_ent_nm,o_p_dt_iss_fr,o_p_dt_iss_to,
				o_p_dt_exp_fr,o_p_dt_exp_to,o_p_dt_wo_fr,o_p_dt_wo_to,o_p_dt_can_fr,o_p_dt_can_to,o_p_dt_void_fr,
				o_p_dt_void_to,o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,o_p_email,o_p_dt_rcpt_fr,
				o_p_dt_rcpt_to,o_p_file_type,o_p_file_size,o_p_file_nm,o_p_batch_no,o_p_fms_ref_no,o_task_id WITH RESUME;
	END FOREACH
end procedure

/*
Remarks:
chk - check
run - running
i - input
o - output
cd - code
*/

/*Only for checking and refreshing the running number only*/
CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_getrunno(i_runno_cd NVARCHAR(50))
RETURNING INT AS result;

DEFINE o_dt_last_runno DATE;
DEFINE o_result INT;

/* Reset running no */
SELECT FIRST 1 dt_last_runno
INTO o_dt_last_runno
FROM rms_runno
WHERE runno_cd = i_runno_cd;

IF DAY(TODAY) <> DAY(o_dt_last_runno)
	THEN 	
			UPDATE 	rms_runno
			SET		last_runno = 0,
					dt_last_runno = current
			WHERE 	runno_cd = i_runno_cd;
END IF;

LET o_result = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

RETURN o_result;

END PROCEDURE
GO
/*
remarks on shortcut:
fr - from
en - english
bm - bahasa malaysia
i - input
o - output 
c - cursor
ss - source system
*/

create or replace procedure sp_getsourcesystem (i_page integer,i_size integer, i_ss_id int8, i_ss_cd nvarchar(10), i_ss_nm nvarchar(50),
										i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_status nvarchar(10))

returning 		int8 as ss_id,
				nvarchar(10) as ss_cd,
				nvarchar(50) as ss_nm,
				datetime year to second as dt_modified, 
				nvarchar(25) as modified_by, 
				nvarchar(10) as status,
				nvarchar(50) as status_en,
				nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
				integer as total;

	define o_ss_id int8;
	define o_ss_cd nvarchar(10);
	define o_ss_nm nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to second;
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define o_status_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_status_bm nvarchar(50);
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_ss t1
					left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
        			left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
					where (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = '' or t1.ss_cd = i_ss_cd)
        					and (i_ss_id is null or t1.ss_id = i_ss_id)
       						and (i_ss_nm is null or t1.ss_nm like '%' || i_ss_nm || '%')
       						and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        					and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        					and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        					and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                            and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
							);

	foreach c_getsourcesystem for
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.ss_id, t1.ss_cd , t1.ss_nm, t1.dt_modified, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t3.nm_en, t3.nm_bm
		into o_ss_id, o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm
	    from rms_ss t1
	    left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
	    left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
	    where (i_ss_cd is null or i_ss_cd = '' or t1.ss_cd = i_ss_cd)
	    		and (i_ss_id is null or t1.ss_id = i_ss_id)
	       		and (i_ss_nm is null or t1.ss_nm like '%' || i_ss_nm || '%')
	       		and (i_modified_by is null or i_modified_by == '' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
	        	and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
	        	and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
	        	and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
			return o_ss_id, o_ss_cd, o_ss_nm, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm,total with resume;
	end foreach
	
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_gettaxcode_v2(i_page integer,i_size integer, i_tax_cd_id int8,i_tax_cd nvarchar(10), i_tax_cd_nm_en nvarchar(50),
								 i_tax_cd_nm_bm nvarchar(50), i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_dt_modified_fr datetime year to second, i_dt_modified_to datetime year to second, i_status nvarchar(10))
	returning 	nvarchar(50) as tax_cd,
				int8 as tax_cd_id,
				nvarchar(50) as tax_cd_nm_en,
				nvarchar(50) as tax_cd_nm_bm,
				decimal(16,2) as tax_pct,
				datetime year to fraction(5) as dt_modified, 
				nvarchar(25) as modified_by, 
				nvarchar(10) as status,
				nvarchar(50) as status_en,
				nvarchar(50) as status_bm,
				integer as total;

	define o_tax_cd_id int8;
	define o_tax_cd nvarchar(10);
	define o_tax_cd_nm_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_tax_cd_nm_bm nvarchar(50);
	define o_tax_pct decimal(16,2);
	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define o_status_en nvarchar(50);
	define o_status_bm nvarchar(50);
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;

if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1) 
					from rms_tax_code t1
					left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
        			left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
					where (i_tax_cd is null or t1.tax_cd like '%' || i_tax_cd || '%')
        					and (i_tax_cd_id is null or t1.tax_cd_id = i_tax_cd_id)
       						and (i_tax_cd_nm_en is null or t1.tax_cd_nm_en like '%' || i_tax_cd_nm_en || '%')
        					and (i_tax_cd_nm_bm is null or t1.tax_cd_nm_bm like '%' || i_tax_cd_nm_bm || '%')
       						and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        					and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        					and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        					and (i_status is null or  t1.status = i_status)
                            and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
							);

	foreach c_gettaxcode for
        select skip calculatedpage limit i_size t1.tax_cd, t1.tax_cd_id , t1.tax_cd_nm_en, t1.tax_cd_nm_bm, t1.tax_pct, t1.dt_modified, t1.modified_by, t1.status, t3.nm_en, t3.nm_bm
		into o_tax_cd, o_tax_cd_id, o_tax_cd_nm_en, o_tax_cd_nm_bm, o_tax_pct, o_dt_modified, o_modified_by, o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm
        from rms_tax_code t1
        left outer join rms_user t2 on t1.modified_by = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
        left outer join rms_param t3 on t1.status = t3.param_cd
        where (i_tax_cd is null or t1.tax_cd like '%' || i_tax_cd || '%')
        and (i_tax_cd_id is null or t1.tax_cd_id = i_tax_cd_id)
        and (i_tax_cd_nm_en is null or t1.tax_cd_nm_en like '%' || i_tax_cd_nm_en || '%')
        and (i_tax_cd_nm_bm is null or t1.tax_cd_nm_bm like '%' || i_tax_cd_nm_bm || '%')
        and (i_modified_by is null or t1.modified_by like '%' || i_modified_by || '%' or t2.ssm4uuserrefno = i_modified_by)
        and (i_dt_modified_fr is null or t1.dt_modified >= i_dt_modified_fr)
        and (i_dt_modified_to is null or t1.dt_modified <= i_dt_modified_to)
        and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
        and t3.param_grp_nm = 'Status'
        order by t1.tax_cd_nm_en

		return o_tax_cd,o_tax_cd_id,o_tax_cd_nm_en,o_tax_cd_nm_bm,o_tax_pct,o_dt_modified,o_modified_by,o_status, o_status_en, o_status_bm,total with resume;
	end foreach
	
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getUpperUser(i_username nvarchar(50))
	returning nvarchar(50) as ssm4uuserrefno,nvarchar(50) as nm,nvarchar(50) as email,
	DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_created, DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_ssm4uuserrefno nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_nm nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_email nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define total integer;
	define current_user_role nvarchar(50);
	define upper_user_role nvarchar(50);


	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_user
    WHERE status = 'A');
       
    select t3.role_nm_en into current_user_role from rms_user as t1 inner join rms_user_role as t2 on t1.user_id=t2.user_id
	inner join rms_role as t3 on t2.role_id=t3.role_id where t1.status='A' and t2.status='A' and t3.status='A' 
    and t1.nm=i_username;
    
    if current_user_role='REQUESTER' then
       let upper_user_role = 'REQUESTERHOD';
    
    elif current_user_role='REQUESTERHOD' then
      let upper_user_role = 'FINANCEADMIN';
       
    elif current_user_role='FINANCEADMIN' then
      let upper_user_role = 'FINANCEHOD';
      
    else
      let upper_user_role = '';
      
    end if;

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        select t1.ssm4uuserrefno, t1.nm, t1.email, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status   
        INTO o_ssm4uuserrefno, o_nm, o_email, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status
        from rms_user as t1 inner join rms_user_role as t2 on t1.user_id=t2.user_id
		inner join rms_role as t3 on t2.role_id=t3.role_id where t1.status='A' and t2.status='A' and t3.status='A' 
        and t3.role_nm_en=upper_user_role

		
		RETURN o_ssm4uuserrefno,o_nm,o_email, o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace PROCEDURE sp_getUpperUser(i_username nvarchar(50), i_email nvarchar(50))
	returning nvarchar(50) as ssm4uuserrefno,nvarchar(50) as nm,nvarchar(50) as email,
	DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_created, DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_ssm4uuserrefno nvarchar(25);
	DEFINE o_nm nvarchar(50);
	DEFINE o_email nvarchar(50);
	define o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);
	define total integer;
	define current_user_role nvarchar(50);
	define upper_user_role nvarchar(50);


	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_user
    WHERE status = 'A');
       
    select t3.role_nm_en 
    into current_user_role 
    from rms_user as t1 
    inner join rms_user_role as t2 on t1.ssm4uuserrefno=t2.ssm4uuserrefno
	inner join rms_role as t3 on t2.role_id=t3.role_id 
    where t1.status='A' and t2.status='A' and t3.status='A' 
    and t1.nm=i_username and t1.email=i_email;
    
    if current_user_role='REQUESTER' then
       let upper_user_role = 'REQUESTERHOD';
    
    elif current_user_role='REQUESTERHOD' then
      let upper_user_role = 'FINANCEADMIN';
       
    elif current_user_role='FINANCEADMIN' then
      let upper_user_role = 'FINANCEHOD';
      
    else
      let upper_user_role = '';
      
    end if;

	FOREACH cursor1 FOR
        select t1.ssm4uuserrefno, t1.nm, t1.email, t1.dt_created, t1.dt_modified,t1.created_by, t1.modified_by, t1.status   
        INTO o_ssm4uuserrefno, o_nm, o_email, o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status
        from rms_user as t1 inner join rms_user_role as t2 on t1.ssm4uuserrefno=t2.ssm4uuserrefno
		inner join rms_role as t3 on t2.role_id=t3.role_id where t1.status='A' and t2.status='A' and t3.status='A' 
        and t3.role_nm_en=upper_user_role

		
		RETURN o_ssm4uuserrefno,o_nm,o_email, o_dt_created,o_dt_modified,o_created_by,o_modified_by,o_status,total WITH RESUME;
	END foreach

END procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_getuseranduserroles(
    i_page INTEGER,
    i_size INTEGER,
    i_user NVARCHAR(50),
    i_user_role NVARCHAR(50))
RETURNING 
    NVARCHAR(50) AS ssm4uuserrefno,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS name,
    NVARCHAR(50) AS email,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
    NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by,
    NVARCHAR(10) AS status,
    LVARCHAR(MAX) AS roles,
    INTEGER AS total_roles;

DEFINE o_user NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_name NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_email NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_status NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_roles LVARCHAR(MAX);
DEFINE total_roles INTEGER;
DEFINE calculatedpage INTEGER;

IF (i_page IS NULL OR i_page < 1) THEN 
    RAISE EXCEPTION -746, 0, "i_page is null or invalid";
END IF;

LET calculatedpage = (i_page - 1) * i_size;

LET total_roles = (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT u.ssm4uuserrefno)
                   FROM rms_user u
                   LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user_role ur ON u.ssm4uuserrefno = ur.ssm4uuserrefno
                   LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_role r ON ur.role_id = r.role_id
                   WHERE (i_user IS NULL OR u.nm LIKE '%' || i_user || '%')
                     AND (i_user_role IS NULL OR r.role_nm_en = i_user_role));

FOREACH c_getuserroles FOR
    SELECT SKIP calculatedpage LIMIT i_size
        u.ssm4uuserrefno,
        u.nm,
        u.email,
        u.created_by,
        u.modified_by,
        u.status,
        sp_GROUP_CONCAT(r.role_nm_en) AS roles
    INTO 
        o_user,
        o_name,
        o_email,
        o_created_by,
        o_modified_by,
        o_status,
        o_roles
    FROM rms_user u
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user_role ur ON u.ssm4uuserrefno = ur.ssm4uuserrefno
    LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_role r ON ur.role_id = r.role_id
    WHERE (i_user IS NULL OR u.nm LIKE '%' || i_user || '%')
    AND (i_user_role IS NULL OR r.role_nm_en = i_user_role OR u.ssm4uuserrefno IN (
        SELECT ur_inner.ssm4uuserrefno
        FROM rms_user_role ur_inner
        JOIN rms_role r_inner ON ur_inner.role_id = r_inner.role_id
        WHERE r_inner.role_nm_en = i_user_role
    ))
    GROUP BY u.ssm4uuserrefno, u.nm, u.email, u.created_by, u.modified_by, u.status
    order by u.nm
    RETURN o_user, o_name, o_email, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status, o_roles, total_roles WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
/*
remarks on shortcut:
fr - from
en - english
bm - bahasa malaysia
i = input
o = output 
c = cursor
*/

create or replace procedure sp_getuserbyrole (i_page integer,i_size integer, i_role_nm_en nvarchar(255), i_role_nm_bm nvarchar(255), i_status nvarchar(10))

returning 	nvarchar(25) as ssm4uuserrefno,
			nvarchar(255) as nm,
			nvarchar(255) as email,
			integer as total;
			
	define o_ssm4uuserrefno nvarchar(25);
	define o_nm nvarchar(255);
	define o_email nvarchar(255);
	define calculatedpage integer;
	define total integer;
	
if (i_page is null or i_page < 1) or (i_size is null or i_page < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_page or i_size is null integer";
end if

	let calculatedpage = (i_page-1)*i_size;
	let total = (select count(1)
				from rms_user t1
				join rms_user_role t2 on t1.ssm4uuserrefno = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
				join rms_role t3 on t2.role_id = t3.role_id
				where (i_role_nm_en is null or ',' || i_role_nm_en || ',' like '%' || ',' || t3.role_nm_en || ','  || '%')
       					and (i_role_nm_bm is null or ',' || i_role_nm_bm || ',' like '%' || ',' || t3.role_nm_bm || ','  || '%')
						and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
				);
	foreach c_getuserbyrole for		
		select skip calculatedpage limit i_size  t1.ssm4uuserrefno, t1.nm, t1.email
		into o_ssm4uuserrefno, o_nm, o_email
	    from rms_user t1
		join rms_user_role t2 on t1.ssm4uuserrefno = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
		join rms_role t3 on t2.role_id = t3.role_id
		where (i_role_nm_en is null or ',' || i_role_nm_en || ',' like '%' || ',' || t3.role_nm_en || ','  || '%')
       			and (i_role_nm_bm is null or ',' || i_role_nm_bm || ',' like '%' || ',' || t3.role_nm_bm || ','  || '%')
				and (i_status is null or t1.status = i_status)
					
		return  o_ssm4uuserrefno, o_nm, o_email,total with resume;
	end foreach
	
end procedure
GO

	--END foreach

END procedure

create or replace procedure sp_getUserRole(i_username nvarchar(50), i_email nvarchar(50))
	returning nvarchar(50) as role_nm_en, nvarchar(50) as role_nm_bm,nvarchar(50) as role_desc, integer as role_special, nvarchar(50) as role_owner,
	DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_created, DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) as dt_modified, nvarchar(25) as created_by, nvarchar(25) as modified_by, nvarchar(10) as status, integer as total;

	DEFINE o_role_nm_bm nvarchar(50);

	define o_dt_modified datetime year to fraction(5);
	define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);
	define o_status nvarchar(10);

	let total = (select count(1) FROM rms_user
    WHERE status = 'A' and nm=i_username and email=i_email);
  

	--FOREACH cursor1 for
	
	
	    select t3.role_nm_en, t3.role_nm_bm, t3.role_desc, t3.role_special, t3.role_owner, t3.dt_created,
	    t3.dt_modified, t3.created_by, t3.modified_by, t3.status  
	    into o_role_nm_en, o_role_nm_bm, o_role_desc, o_role_special, o_role_owner,o_dt_created,
	    o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status

	    inner join rms_role as t3 on t2.role_id=t3.role_id where t1.status='A' and t2.status='A' and t3.status='A' 
        and t1.nm=i_username and t1.email=i_email limit 1;
	
		--RETURN o_role_nm_en, o_role_nm_bm, o_role_desc, o_role_special, o_role_owner,o_dt_created,
	   -- o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status,total WITH RESUME;
	   
	   RETURN o_role_nm_en, o_role_nm_bm, o_role_desc, o_role_special, o_role_owner,o_dt_created,
	    o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by, o_status,total ;
	   
	--END foreach

END procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getutldays(i_period_key DATE)
RETURNING 
    nvarchar(20) AS period,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS in,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS out,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS variance,
    nvarchar(10) AS periodbalance,
    DATE AS dummydate;

DEFINE o_period nvarchar(20);
DEFINE o_in DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_out DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_variance DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_period_balance nvarchar(10);
DEFINE o_dummydate DATE;
DEFINE total_in DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE total_out DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE total_variance DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE total_period_balance DECIMAL(15,5);

-- Initialize totals
LET total_in = 0;
LET total_out = 0;
LET total_variance = 0;
LET total_period_balance = 0;

-- Cursor to fetch data
FOREACH cursor1 FOR

    WITH days_of_month(day_key) AS (
    SELECT MDY(MONTH(i_period_key), 1, YEAR(i_period_key)) -- First day of the input month
    UNION ALL
    SELECT day_key + 1
    FROM days_of_month
    WHERE day_key < LAST_DAY(i_period_key)
    )
    SELECT 
        CASE 
            WHEN d.day_key > TODAY THEN '' 
            ELSE TO_CHAR(d.day_key, '%d %b %Y')
        END AS period,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.day_key > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE NVL(SUM(NVL(r.debit_amt, 0)), 0) 
        END AS in,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.day_key > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE NVL(SUM(NVL(r.credit_amt, 0)), 0) 
        END AS out,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.day_key > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE NVL(SUM(NVL(r.variance, 0)), 0) 
        END AS variance,
        CASE 
            WHEN d.day_key > TODAY THEN '' 
            ELSE TO_CHAR(ROUND(NVL(SUM(NVL(r.accumulate_amt, 0)), 0), 2))
        END AS periodbalance,
        d.day_key AS dummydate
    INTO
        o_period,
        o_in,
        o_out,
        o_variance,
        o_period_balance,
        o_dummydate
    FROM
        days_of_month d
    LEFT JOIN
        rms_unmatch_txn r ON d.day_key = r.period_key
    GROUP BY
        d.day_key
    ORDER BY
        d.day_key
	
    -- Accumulate totals only if the date is not in the future
    IF o_dummydate <= today THEN
        LET total_in = total_in + NVL(o_in, 0);
        LET total_out = total_out + NVL(o_out, 0);
        LET total_variance = total_variance + NVL(o_variance, 0);
        LET total_period_balance = total_period_balance + NVL(CAST(o_period_balance AS DECIMAL(15,5)), 0);
    END IF;

    RETURN o_period, o_in, o_out, o_variance, o_period_balance, o_dummydate WITH RESUME;
END FOREACH;

-- Add totals as the last row
RETURN 'Total', total_in, total_out, total_variance, 'N/A', NULL;
END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_getutlmonths(i_period_key DATE)
RETURNING 
    nvarchar(20) AS period,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS in,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS out,
    DECIMAL(15,5) AS variance,
    nvarchar(10) AS periodbalance,
    DATE AS dummydate;

DEFINE o_period nvarchar(20);
DEFINE o_in DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_out DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_variance DECIMAL(15,5);
DEFINE o_period_balance nvarchar(10);
DEFINE o_dummydate DATE;
DEFINE o_month_key INTEGER;
DEFINE total_previous_year_balance DECIMAL(15,5);

-- Calculate the total amount for the period balance of the previous year
SELECT COALESCE(SUM(accumulate_amt), 0) 
INTO total_previous_year_balance 
FROM rms_unmatch_txn 
WHERE YEAR(period_key) = YEAR(i_period_key) - 1;

-- Add "Beginning Balance" row at the top
RETURN 'Beginning Balance', 0.00, 0.00, 0.00, TO_CHAR(ROUND(total_previous_year_balance, 2)), NULL::DATE WITH RESUME;

FOREACH cursor1 FOR
    SELECT 
        CASE 
            WHEN DummyDate > TODAY THEN '' 
            ELSE Period 
        END AS Period,
        CASE 
            WHEN DummyDate > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE COALESCE(SUM(In), 0) 
        END AS In,
        CASE 
            WHEN DummyDate > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE COALESCE(SUM(Out), 0) 
        END AS Out,
        CASE 
            WHEN DummyDate > TODAY THEN NULL 
            ELSE COALESCE(SUM(Variance), 0) 
        END AS Variance,
        CASE 
            WHEN MonthKey = 13 THEN 'N/A' 
            WHEN DummyDate > TODAY THEN '' 
            ELSE TO_CHAR(ROUND(COALESCE(SUM(PeriodBalance), 0), 2))
        END AS PeriodBalance,
        DummyDate,
        MonthKey
    INTO
        o_period,
        o_in,
        o_out,
        o_variance,
        o_period_balance,
        o_dummydate,
        o_month_key
    FROM (
        SELECT
            CASE MONTH(period_key)
                WHEN 1 THEN 'January'
                WHEN 2 THEN 'February'
                WHEN 3 THEN 'March'
                WHEN 4 THEN 'April'
                WHEN 5 THEN 'May'
                WHEN 6 THEN 'June'
                WHEN 7 THEN 'July'
                WHEN 8 THEN 'August'
                WHEN 9 THEN 'September'
                WHEN 10 THEN 'October'
                WHEN 11 THEN 'November'
                WHEN 12 THEN 'December'
            END AS Period,
            debit_amt AS In, 
            credit_amt AS Out, 
            variance AS Variance, 
            accumulate_amt AS PeriodBalance,
            MDY(MONTH(period_key), 1, YEAR(i_period_key)) AS DummyDate,
            MONTH(period_key) AS MonthKey
        FROM 
            rms_unmatch_txn
        WHERE 
            YEAR(period_key) = YEAR(i_period_key)
        UNION ALL
        SELECT
            CASE n
                WHEN 1 THEN 'January'
                WHEN 2 THEN 'February'
                WHEN 3 THEN 'March'
                WHEN 4 THEN 'April'
                WHEN 5 THEN 'May'
                WHEN 6 THEN 'June'
                WHEN 7 THEN 'July'
                WHEN 8 THEN 'August'
                WHEN 9 THEN 'September'
                WHEN 10 THEN 'October'
                WHEN 11 THEN 'November'
                WHEN 12 THEN 'December'
            END AS Period,
            0 AS In, 
            0 AS Out, 
            0 AS Variance, 
            0 AS PeriodBalance,
            MDY(n, 1, YEAR(i_period_key)) AS DummyDate,
            n AS MonthKey
        FROM (SELECT 1 AS n UNION ALL SELECT 2 UNION ALL SELECT 3 UNION ALL SELECT 4 UNION ALL SELECT 5 UNION ALL SELECT 6 UNION ALL SELECT 7 UNION ALL SELECT 8 UNION ALL SELECT 9 UNION ALL SELECT 10 UNION ALL SELECT 11 UNION ALL SELECT 12) AS Months
    ) AS Subquery
    GROUP BY 
        Period,
        DummyDate,
        MonthKey

    UNION ALL

    SELECT
        'Total' AS Period,
        COALESCE(SUM(In), 0) AS In,
        COALESCE(SUM(Out), 0) AS Out,
        COALESCE(SUM(Variance), 0) AS Variance,
        'N/A' AS PeriodBalance,
        NULL::DATE AS DummyDate,
        13 AS MonthKey
    FROM (
        SELECT
            debit_amt AS In, 
            credit_amt AS Out, 
            variance AS Variance, 
            accumulate_amt AS PeriodBalance,
            0 AS MonthKey
        FROM 
            rms_unmatch_txn
        WHERE 
            YEAR(period_key) = YEAR(i_period_key)
    ) AS TotalSubquery

    ORDER BY 
        MonthKey ASC

										  
						  
    RETURN o_period, o_in, o_out, o_variance, o_period_balance, o_dummydate WITH RESUME;
		   

END FOREACH;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
/*
Remarks:
wfth - workflow history
ast - assign to by task id 
i - input
o - output
sp - store procedure
*/


create or replace procedure sp_getwfh_ast(i_task_id NVARCHAR(50), i_status NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNING NVARCHAR(20) AS assign_to,
          NVARCHAR(50) AS assign_to_nm;

DEFINE o_assign_to 		NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_assign_to_nm 	NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_wf_id 			INT8;
define pairStatus       NVARCHAR(20);

LET o_wf_id = TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(i_task_id, 3));

IF i_status = 'P-RHOD' THEN
    LET pairStatus = 'Q-RHOD';
elif i_status = 'P-FA' THEN
    LET pairStatus = 'Q-FA';
elif i_status = 'Q-FA' THEN
    LET pairStatus = 'P-FA';
elif i_status = 'Q-RHOD' THEN
    LET pairStatus = 'P-RHOD';
ELSE
    LET pairStatus = '';
END IF;

BEGIN WORK;

    --SELECT DISTINCT t1.assign_to, t2.nm
    --INTO o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm
    --FROM rms_mft_wfhist t1
    --LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user t2 ON t1.assign_to = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
    --WHERE t1.wf_id = o_wf_id
    --AND t1.status = i_status;
IF i_status IN ('Q-R','P-FHOD') THEN
 	  SELECT assign_to, nm 
 	  INTO o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm
 	  FROM (
      SELECT ROW_NUMBER () OVER (PARTITION BY t1.wf_id ORDER BY t1.wf_id, t1.dt_activity DESC) AS rn, t1.assign_to, t2.nm FROM rms_mft_wfhist t1
	  LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user t2 ON t1.assign_to = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
      WHERE t1.wf_id = o_wf_id
      AND t1.status = i_status 
      ) T1 where rn = 1;
ELSE
	  SELECT assign_to, nm 
 	  INTO o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm
 	  FROM (
      SELECT ROW_NUMBER () OVER (PARTITION BY t1.wf_id ORDER BY t1.wf_id, t1.dt_activity DESC) AS rn, t1.assign_to, t2.nm FROM rms_mft_wfhist t1
	  LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user t2 ON t1.assign_to = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
      WHERE t1.wf_id = o_wf_id
      AND (t1.status = i_status or t1.status = pairStatus) 
      ) T1 where rn = 1;
END IF;

COMMIT WORK;

RETURN o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm;
                        
END PROCEDURE;
GO
/*
Remarks:
wfth - workflow history
ast - assign to by task id 
i - input
o - output
sp - store procedure
*/


create or replace procedure sp_getwfh_status(i_task_id NVARCHAR(50), i_status NVARCHAR(20))
RETURNING NVARCHAR(20) AS assign_to,
          NVARCHAR(50) AS assign_to_nm,
          NVARCHAR(10) AS status;

DEFINE o_assign_to 		NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_assign_to_nm 	NVARCHAR(50);
DEFINE o_status 		NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_wf_id 			INT8;

LET o_wf_id = TO_NUMBER(SUBSTR(i_task_id, 3));

BEGIN WORK;


 	  SELECT assign_to, nm, status
 	  INTO o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm, o_status 
 	  FROM (
      SELECT ROW_NUMBER () OVER (PARTITION BY t1.wf_id ORDER BY t1.wf_id, t1.dt_activity DESC) AS rn, t1.assign_to, t2.nm, t1.status
      FROM rms_mft_wfhist t1
	  LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_user t2 ON t1.assign_to = t2.ssm4uuserrefno
      WHERE t1.wf_id = o_wf_id
      AND t1.status != i_status
      ) T1 where rn = 1;

COMMIT WORK;

RETURN o_assign_to, o_assign_to_nm, o_status;
                        
END PROCEDURE;
GO

                                                                            i_remark NVARCHAR(255), i_source NVARCHAR(255), i_response_msg LVARCHAR(5000), i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10))

	(actor, request_url, module, request_msg, action, page_url, remark, source, response_msg, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status)
VALUES 
	(i_actor,i_request_url, i_module, i_request_msg,  i_action, i_page_url, i_remark, i_source, i_response_msg,current, current, i_created_by, i_created_by, i_status);

LET row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

RETURN row_count;

END PROCEDURE
