CREATE or REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_insbank(i_file_nm nvarchar(255), i_file_content BLOB, i_file_type nvarchar(5), i_file_size_kb INT,
							i_dt_settlement nvarchar(100), i_created_by nvarchar(25))
                            
returning int as result;											

define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
define o_task_no nvarchar(25);
define o_rc_bank_id nvarchar(20);
define o_rc_pg_id nvarchar(20);
define o_exist2 int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

-- Set a default value for o_result
let o_result = 0;

-- check exist settlement's status
select count(1), rc_pg_id
into o_exist, o_rc_pg_id
from rms_rc_pg
where dt_settlement = to_date(i_dt_settlement,'%d/%m/%Y')
and task_status = 'CS'
group by rc_pg_id;

if o_exist > 0 then

select count(1)
into o_exist2
from rms_rc_bank
where rc_pg_id = o_rc_pg_id
and task_status = 'O';

    if o_exist2 = 0 then

        BEGIN WORK;
        set lock mode to wait 30;

        -- check latest running no
        execute procedure sp_getrunno('RC') into o_result;

        /* UPDATE last running no */
        UPDATE rms_runno
        SET last_runno = last_runno +1
        WHERE runno_cd = 'RC';

        /* Select running no */
        SELECT FIRST 1 ('RC' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
        INTO o_task_no
        FROM rms_runno
        WHERE runno_cd = 'RC';

        -- insert rms_rc_bank
        INSERT INTO rms_rc_bank(task_no, rc_pg_id, task_status, recon_status, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, dt_upload) 
                         VALUES(o_task_no, o_rc_pg_id, "O", "PE", current, current, i_created_by, i_created_by, current);

        -- get inserted id
        let o_rc_bank_id = DBINFO('Serial8');

        -- insert rms_rc_pgdoc
        INSERT INTO rms_rc_bankdoc( rc_bank_id, file_nm, file_content, file_type, file_size_kb, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
                            VALUES( o_rc_bank_id, i_file_nm, i_file_content, i_file_type, i_file_size_kb, current, current, i_created_by, i_created_by, 'A');

        -- get inserted id
        let o_result = DBINFO('Serial8');

        COMMIT WORK;    

    end if;
end if;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insdi(i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_txn_type nvarchar(10), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), 
                            i_dt_effective date, i_dt_expiry date, i_item_ref_no nvarchar(30),
                            i_approval_status nvarchar(10), i_dt_approval date)
returning int8 as result;

define o_exist int;
define o_exist_a int;
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_qty int;
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_dt_effective date;
define o_result int;
define o_total_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_bal_amt decimal(16,2);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

let o_result = 0;

-- Record exists checking
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_mtt_item
where fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
and entity_type = i_entity_type
and entity_no = i_entity_no
and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no
and status = 'A';

if o_exist > 0 then

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    -- Select from rms_mtt_item
    select first 1 fee_detail_pk, qty, unit_fee
    into o_fee_detail_pk, o_qty, o_unit_fee
    from rms_mtt_item
    where fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no;

    select count(1)
    into o_exist_a
    from rms_di
    where fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    --and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no
    and status not in ('C','T');
    
    let o_total_fee = o_qty * o_unit_fee;

    if o_exist_a > 0 then

        -- Insert into rms_di
        insert into rms_di(fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, entity_type, entity_no, dt_effective, dt_expiry,
                            dt_termination, item_ref_no, approval_status, dt_approval, no_of_yr, unit_fee, total_fee,
                                bal_di_amt, next_calc_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, txn_type) 
        values(o_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, i_entity_type, i_entity_no, i_dt_effective, i_dt_expiry,
             '', i_item_ref_no, i_approval_status, i_dt_approval, o_qty, o_unit_fee, o_total_fee,
                o_total_fee, i_dt_effective, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'R', i_txn_type);

    -- Set rows effected in variable
    let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

    -- Insert into rms_di audit
    insert into rms_di_a(di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, dt_txn, action_type, 
                            entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt_b4, bal_di_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, in_fms_posting) 
    values(o_result, o_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, current, 'PCR',
                i_entity_type, i_entity_no, 0.00, o_total_fee, '', 'R',
                    current, current, 'system', 'system', 'R', 0);

    else
        -- Amount Calculation
        let o_bal_amt = o_total_fee - o_unit_fee;
        let o_dt_effective = EXTEND(EXTEND(i_dt_effective, YEAR TO DAY) + 1 UNITS YEAR, YEAR TO DAY);

        -- Insert into rms_di
        insert into rms_di(fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, entity_type, entity_no, dt_effective, dt_expiry,
                            dt_termination, item_ref_no, approval_status, dt_approval, no_of_yr, unit_fee, total_fee,
                                bal_di_amt, next_calc_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, txn_type) 
        values(o_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, i_entity_type, i_entity_no, i_dt_effective, i_dt_expiry,
             '', i_item_ref_no, i_approval_status, i_dt_approval, o_qty, o_unit_fee, o_total_fee,
                o_bal_amt, o_dt_effective, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', i_txn_type);

        -- Set rows effected in variable
        let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

        -- Insert into rms_di audit
        insert into rms_di_a(di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, dt_txn, action_type, 
                                entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt_b4, bal_di_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, 
                                    dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, in_fms_posting) 
        values(o_result, o_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, current, 'PCR',
                    i_entity_type, i_entity_no, 0.00, o_total_fee, '', 'R',
                        current, current, 'system', 'system', 'R', 0);

        -- Insert into rms_di audit
        insert into rms_di_a(di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, dt_txn, action_type, 
                                entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt_b4, bal_di_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, 
                                    dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, in_fms_posting) 
        values(o_result, o_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, current, 'PCA',
                    i_entity_type, i_entity_no, o_total_fee, o_bal_amt, 'R', 'A',
                        current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0);
    end if

    commit work;

end if;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    let o_result = 0;
    return o_result;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insdi_tmn_log(i_txn_type nvarchar(10), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_entity_type nvarchar(1),
                                    i_dt_termination date, i_dt_approval date)
returning int8 as result;

define o_exists int;
define o_di_id int8;
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10);
define o_entity_type nvarchar(1);
define o_entity_no nvarchar(20);
define o_total_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_bal_di_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_status nvarchar(10);
define o_modified_by nvarchar(25);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 10;

select count(1)
into o_exists
from rms_di
where entity_type = i_entity_type
and entity_no = i_entity_no
and i_dt_termination between dt_effective and dt_expiry
and status not in ('C','T');

if o_exists > 0 then

    -- Select di_id from rms_di
    select first 1 di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, entity_type, entity_no, total_fee, bal_di_amt, status, modified_by
    into o_di_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, o_entity_type, o_entity_no, o_total_fee, o_bal_di_amt, o_status, o_modified_by
    from rms_di
    where entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and i_dt_termination between dt_effective and dt_expiry
    and status not in ('C','T');

    -- Insert statement into rms_di_tmn_log
    insert into rms_di_tmn_log(di_id, entity_type, entity_no, dt_termination, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, txn_type) 
    values(o_di_id, i_entity_type, i_entity_no, i_dt_termination,
               current, current, 'system', 'system', o_status, i_txn_type);
    
    -- Update statement in rms_di
    update rms_di
    set dt_termination = i_dt_termination,
        status = 'T',
        dt_modified = current
    where entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and i_dt_termination between dt_effective and dt_expiry
    and status not in ('C','T');

    -- Insert statement into rms_di audit 
    insert into rms_di_a(di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, dt_txn, action_type, 
                            entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt_b4, bal_di_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
    values(o_di_id, o_fee_detail_pk, o_fee_detail_id, current, 'PCT',
                o_entity_type, o_entity_no, o_total_fee, o_bal_di_amt, o_status, 'T',
                    current, current, o_modified_by, o_modified_by, o_status);

    -- Insert statement into rms_di journal debit

    -- Insert statement into rms_di journal credit

else

    let o_di_id = -1;

end if;

commit work;

return o_di_id;

end procedure
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_insdiagingrpt (i_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_tmn_status INT, i_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1), i_p_ent_nm LVARCHAR(2000),
								i_p_txn_ty NVARCHAR(10), i_p_status nvarchar(10), i_p_dt_exp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_dt_exp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
								i_p_dt_eff_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_dt_eff_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_dt_app_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_dt_app_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
								i_p_dt_tmn_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_p_dt_tmn_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND, i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),
								i_status NVARCHAR(10), i_p_email nvarchar(255), i_p_file_type nvarchar(5), i_p_file_size INT, i_p_file_nm nvarchar(255), 
								i_p_batch_no nvarchar(30), i_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25))

RETURNING INT8 as wf_id;


	DEFINE o_wf_id INT8;
	DEFINE o_current_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
    define o_insresult int8;

BEGIN WORK;	
	
	/*Set current date time*/
	let o_current_dt = current;
	
	
	/*Insert data into MFT WF table*/
	INSERT INTO rms_rpt_di_age
		(p_dt_req, p_tmn_status, p_ent_ty, p_ent_nm, p_txn_ty, p_status, p_dt_exp_fr, p_dt_exp_to, p_dt_eff_fr, p_dt_eff_to,

		(i_p_dt_req, i_p_tmn_status, i_p_ent_ty, i_p_ent_nm, i_p_txn_ty, i_p_status, i_p_dt_exp_fr, i_p_dt_exp_to, i_p_dt_eff_fr, i_p_dt_eff_to,
		 i_p_dt_app_fr, i_p_dt_app_to, i_p_dt_tmn_fr, i_p_dt_tmn_to, o_current_dt, o_current_dt, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status, i_p_email, 
		 i_p_file_type, i_p_file_size, i_p_file_nm, i_p_batch_no, i_p_fms_ref_no);
		
	/*Get latest Serial8 ID number from last inserted records*/
	LET o_wf_id = DBINFO('Serial8');
    
COMMIT WORK;
	
RETURN o_wf_id;

END PROCEDURE

create or replace procedure sp_insfmsarr()
returning int as result;
define o_rc_bank_id int8;
define o_rc_pg_id int8;
define o_rc_banktxn_id int8;
define o_pgtxn_id int8;
define o_credit decimal(15,5);
define o_dt_txn datetime year to second;
define o_mdr_amt decimal(15,5);
define o_txn_amt decimal(15,5);
define o_dt_txn_pgtxn datetime year to second;
define arr_amt decimal(15,5);
define charge_amt decimal(15,5);
define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
define o_hid int8;
define o_arr_cid int8;
define o_result int;
on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
execute procedure sp_getrunno('arrc') into o_batch_no;
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;
--foreach c_data for
----    execute procedure sp_getfmsarr()
--	select
--        t1.rc_bank_id,
--        t1.rc_pg_id,
--        t2.credit,
--        t2.dt_txn,
--        t3.mdr_amt
--    from
--        rms_rc_bank t1
--        left join rms_rc_banktxn t2 on t1.rc_bank_id = t2.rc_bank_id
--        left join rms_rc_pgtxn t3 on t1.rc_pg_id = t3.rc_pg_id
foreach execute procedure sp_getfmsarr() into o_rc_bank_id, o_rc_pg_id, o_credit, o_dt_txn, o_mdr_amt
    -- insert into rms_fms_arr_h (header)
    insert into rms_fms_arr_h (
        type, branch, dt_sent, cash_acct, pymt_method,
        cust, rms_batch_no, pymt_amt, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys,
        resp_ref_no, resp_co, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt,
        dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry
    ) values (
        'payment', '000', current, 'ca0010', 'pg',
        'rms pg mid account id', o_batch_no, o_credit, 'rms', null,
        null, null, null, null, null,
        current, current, 'system', 'system', 'a', 0
    );
    let o_hid = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd1');
    let charge_amt = 0.00;
    -- loop through rms_rc_banktxn for the current bank record
    foreach c_banktxn for
        select t2.rc_banktxn_id, t2.credit, t2.dt_txn
        into   o_rc_banktxn_id,  o_credit,  o_dt_txn
        from rms_rc_banktxn t2
        where t2.rc_bank_id = o_rc_bank_id
        -- loop through rms_rc_pgtxn for the current rc_pg_id
        foreach c_pgtxn for
            select t3.rc_pgtxn_id, t3.txn_amt, t3.dt_txn,t3.mdr_amt
            into o_pgtxn_id, o_txn_amt, o_dt_txn_pgtxn, o_mdr_amt
            from rms_rc_pgtxn t3
            where t3.rc_pg_id = o_rc_pg_id
 
            -- sum up mdr_amt for charge
            let charge_amt = charge_amt + o_mdr_amt;
        end foreach;
        -- insert into rms_fms_arr_b (details)
        insert into rms_fms_arr_b (
            arr_hid, fms_ref_no, doc_type, dt_created, dt_modified,
            created_by, modified_by, status, mtt_pg_id
        ) values (
            o_hid, 'arrc2024071900001', 'pmt', current, current,
            'system', 'system', 'a',
            (select rms_mtt_pg.mtt_pg_id from rms_mtt_pg where rms_mtt_pg.pg_txn_id = o_rc_pg_id)
        );
    end foreach;
    -- insert into rms_fms_arr_c (charge)
    insert into rms_fms_arr_c (
        arr_hid, amt, doc_type, entity_type, offset_subacct,
        dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status
    ) values (
        o_hid, charge_amt, 'pmt', 'pgcharges', '000-000-00000-000000000',
        current, current, 'system', 'system', 'a'
    );
    let o_arr_cid = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd1');
    update rms_rc_bank
    set in_fms_posting = 1
    where rc_bank_id = o_rc_bank_id;
end foreach;
let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');
if (o_result > 0) then
    commit work;
    return o_result;
else
    rollback work;
    return -1;
end if;
end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsarr(i_rc_bank_id int8, i_rc_pg_id int8, i_credit decimal(15,5), i_mdr_amt decimal(15,5),
                                    i_mtt_pg_id int8, i_acct_cd nvarchar(10), i_cust nvarchar(10))
returning int as result;
 
define o_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25);
define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
define o_hid int8;
define o_result int;
 
on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
 
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

/*Get latest running no*/
execute procedure sp_getrunno('arrc') into o_result;

/* update last running no */
update rms_runno
set last_runno = last_runno + 1
where runno_cd = 'arrc';

/* select running no */
select first 1 ('ARRC' || to_char(today, '%y%m%d') || lpad(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
into o_batch_no
from rms_runno
where runno_cd = 'arrc';

-- insert into rms_fms_arr_h (header)
insert into rms_fms_arr_h (
    type, branch, dt_sent, cash_acct, pymt_method,
    cust, rms_batch_no, pymt_amt, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys,
    fms_ref_no, resp_co, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt,
    dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry
) values (
    'Payment', '000', current, i_acct_cd, 'PG',
    i_cust, o_batch_no, i_credit, 'RMS', null,
    null, null, null, null, null,
    current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0
);
 
let o_hid = dbinfo('serial8');
 
-- insert into rms_fms_arr_c (charge)
insert into rms_fms_arr_c (
    arr_hid, amt, doc_type, entity_type, offset_subacct,
    dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status
) values (
    o_hid, i_mdr_amt, 'PMT', 'PGCHARGES', '000-000-00000-000000000',
    current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A'
);
 
-- insert into rms_fms_arr_b (details)
insert into rms_fms_arr_b (
    arr_hid, fms_ref_no, doc_type, dt_created, dt_modified,
    created_by, modified_by, status, mtt_pg_id
)	
select distinct o_hid, t3.fms_ref_no, 'Invoice', current, current,
            'system', 'system', 'A', i_mtt_pg_id
from rms_rc_pgmtt t1
left join rms_fms_ari_b t2 on t1.mtt_pg_id = t2.mtt_pg_id
left join rms_fms_ari_h t3 on t2.ari_hid = t3.ari_hid
where t1.rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id;

 
update rms_rc_bank
set in_fms_posting = 1, 
	dt_modified = current
where rc_bank_id = i_rc_bank_id;
 
let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');
 
if (o_result > 0) then
    commit work;
    return o_result;
else
    rollback work;
    return -1;
end if;
 
end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsdia(i_audit_id int8, i_di_id int8, i_dt_txn date, i_bal_di_amt_af decimal(16,2), i_unit_fee decimal(16,2), i_action_type nvarchar(10))
returning int8 as result;

define o_hid            int8;
define o_batch_no       nvarchar(30);
define o_result         int8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    execute procedure sp_getrunno('JNDI') into o_result;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'jndi';

    /* Select running no */
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('JNDI' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_batch_no
    FROM rms_runno
    WHERE runno_cd = 'jndi';

    insert into rms_fms_jn_h(batch_no, branch_id, desc, ledger_id, module, dt_txn, attr_ext_ref_no, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys, fms_ref_no, resp_ext_ref_no, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry) 
    values(o_batch_no, '000000', 'GL RMS', 'ACTUAL', 'GL', DATE(i_dt_txn), 'DI-' || i_di_id || '-' || i_audit_id, 'RMS', null, null, null, null, null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0);

    let o_hid = dbinfo('serial8');

    if (i_action_type like '%A') then 
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Prepayment/DI'), '000000000000000', i_unit_fee, 0, 'DI PC Amortize', current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');

        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Revenue'), '000000000000000', 0, i_unit_fee, 'DI PC Amortize', current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
elif (i_action_type like '%T') then
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Prepayment/DI'), '000000000000000', i_bal_di_amt_af, 0, 'DI PC Terminate', current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');

        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Revenue'), '000000000000000', 0, i_bal_di_amt_af, 'DI PC Terminate', current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    end if;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    if (o_result > 0) then
        update rms_di_a
        set in_fms_posting = 1,
        dt_modified = current
        where audit_id = i_audit_id;
    end if;

    commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure informix.sp_insfmsledgerdoc (i_fms_id INT8, i_file_nm NVARCHAR(255), i_file_content BLOB, i_file_type NVARCHAR(5), i_file_size INT,
											i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10), i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10),
                                            i_fee_detail_nm_en NVARCHAR(100), i_fms_ledger_cd NVARCHAR(50))
RETURNING INT AS result,
            INT AS file_index;									

    DEFINE o_result INT;
    DEFINE temp_count INT;
    DEFINE t_file_index INT;
    DEFINE temp_count_2 INT;
    DEFINE i_file_size_kb INT;

    
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO temp_count
    FROM rms_fms_doc
    WHERE fms_id = i_fms_id
    AND file_nm = i_file_nm;

    LET i_file_size_kb = i_file_size / 1024;

    -- Insert into rms_fms_doc


    IF temp_count > 0 THEN
        -- File with the same name already exists, update the existing record
        UPDATE rms_fms_doc 
        SET file_content = i_file_content,
            file_type = i_file_type,
            file_size_kb = i_file_size_kb,
            dt_modified = CURRENT,
            modified_by = i_modified_by,
            status = i_status
        WHERE fms_id = i_fms_id
          AND file_nm = i_file_nm;
    ELSE
        INSERT INTO rms_fms_doc
            (fms_id, file_nm, file_content, file_type, file_size_kb, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status)
        VALUES 
            (i_fms_id, i_file_nm, i_file_content, i_file_type, i_file_size_kb, current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);
    END IF;

    SELECT file_index INTO t_file_index FROM rms_fms_doc WHERE file_nm=i_file_nm and file_content = i_file_content and i_fms_id = fms_id;


    -- Check if the record with i_fee_detail_id and i_fms_ledger_cd already exists
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO o_result
    FROM rms_fms_ledger
    WHERE fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
    AND fms_id = i_fms_id
    AND file_index <> t_file_index
    AND status = 'A';

    IF o_result > 0 THEN

        UPDATE rms_fms_ledger
        SET
            status = 'D'
        WHERE fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
        AND fms_id = i_fms_id
        AND file_index <> t_file_index  
        AND status = 'A';
    END IF;

        -- If the record doesn't exist, insert it
        INSERT INTO rms_fms_ledger
            (fms_id, fee_detail_id, fee_detail_nm_en, fms_ledger_cd, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, file_index, status)
        VALUES 
            (i_fms_id, i_fee_detail_id, i_fee_detail_nm_en, i_fms_ledger_cd, current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, t_file_index, 'A');



        UPDATE rms_fms_ledger t1
SET found = 
    CASE 
        WHEN EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 
            FROM rms_fms_ledger t2 
            WHERE t2.fee_detail_id = t1.fee_detail_id
            AND t2.file_index = t1.file_index
            AND t2.fms_id = t1.fms_id -- Exclude the current record
            AND t2.fms_ledger_id <> t1.fms_ledger_id
            AND t2.status = 'A'
        ) THEN 'DU'  -- Duplicate
        WHEN EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 
            FROM rms_mft t3 
            WHERE t3.fee_detail_id = t1.fee_detail_id
            AND t1.status = 'A'
        ) THEN 'F'  -- Not Found
        ELSE 'NF'     -- Found
    END;
    
        -- If the record exists, update it
        

    LET o_result = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    RETURN o_result, t_file_index;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsmttb(i_mtt_pg_id int8,i_pg_pymt_amt decimal(16,2),i_qty int,i_item_desc nvarchar(100)
                ,i_unit_fee decimal(16,2),i_rcpt_no nvarchar(100),i_cust_nm nvarchar(100), i_entity_nm nvarchar(100), i_entity_no nvarchar(100)
                ,i_entity_type nvarchar(100), i_gross_amt decimal(16,2),i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(100), i_pg_pymt_method nvarchar(100)
                ,i_tax_amt decimal(16,2),i_customer nvarchar(100),i_hid int8,i_item_ref_no nvarchar(100),i_cp_no nvarchar(100))

returning int8 as result;

define o_result         int;
define di_exist         int;
define cp_exist         int;
define coa1             nvarchar(100);
define coa1_d           nvarchar(100);
define o_accr_amt         decimal(16,2);
define temp_amt              decimal(16,2);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    -- default coa1 to mft.ledger_cd
    select ledger_cd
    into coa1_d
    from rms_mft
    where fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id;

    -- check if is RICP arrcual    
    select count(1),accr_amt
    into cp_exist,o_accr_amt
    from rms_ricp
    where cp_no = i_cp_no
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and cp_tier != '3' -- tony say if tier 3 means direct sales
    group by accr_amt;
    
    if cp_exist > 0 then -- if count>0 means this is not direct sale
        -- compare amt
        if o_accr_amt=i_gross_amt then
            -- find account from fms_acct
            select acct_cd
            into coa1
            from rms_fms_acct
            where acct_nm = 'RI/CMP';

            -- insert rms_fms_ari_b  
            INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                        txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                        ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                        item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                        status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
                VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                        i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                        i_entity_no, i_entity_type, i_gross_amt, coa1, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                        i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                        'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
        end if;

        if o_accr_amt<i_gross_amt then -- need insert 2 rows to body table
            let temp_amt = i_gross_amt-o_accr_amt;
            -- find account from fms_acct
            select acct_cd
            into coa1
            from rms_fms_acct
            where acct_nm = 'RI/CMP';
            
            -- 1st row
            INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                        txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                        ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                        item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                        status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
                VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                        i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                        i_entity_no, i_entity_type, o_accr_amt, coa1, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                        i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                        'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
            -- 2nd row
            INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                        txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                        ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                        item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                        status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
                VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                        i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                        i_entity_no, i_entity_type, temp_amt, coa1_d, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                        i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                        'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
        end if;

            if o_accr_amt>i_gross_amt then -- need insert 2 rows to body table
                let temp_amt = o_accr_amt-i_gross_amt;

                -- find account from fms_acct
                select acct_cd
                into coa1
                from rms_fms_acct
                where acct_nm = 'RI/CMP';

                -- 1st row
                INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                            txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                            ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                            item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                            status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
                    VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                            i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                            i_entity_no, i_entity_type, o_accr_amt, coa1, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                            i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                            'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);

                -- find account from fms_acct
                select acct_cd
                into coa1
                from rms_fms_acct
                where acct_nm = 'Compound Discount';
                -- 2nd row
                INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                            txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                            ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                            item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                            status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
                    VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                            i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                            i_entity_no, i_entity_type, temp_amt, coa1, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                            i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                            'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
        end if;
            
    end if;

    -- check if is DI arrcual
    select count(1)
    into di_exist
    from rms_di
    where item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id
    and (status = 'R' or status = 'A');
    
    if di_exist > 0 then -- if count>0 means this is not direct sale
        -- find account from fms_acct
        select acct_cd
        into coa1
        from rms_fms_acct
        where acct_nm = 'Prepayment/DI';

        -- insert rms_fms_ari_b  
        INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                    txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                    ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                    item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                    status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
            VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                    i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                    i_entity_no, i_entity_type, i_gross_amt, coa1, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                    i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                    'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
    else

         INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_b(ari_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, 
                txn_desc, unit_price, rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, 
                ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, coa1, pymt_mode, 
                item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                status, coa2, mtt_pg_id) 
        VALUES(i_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', 
                i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, 
                i_entity_no, i_entity_type, i_gross_amt, coa1_d, i_pg_pymt_method, 
                i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
                'A', i_fee_detail_id, i_mtt_pg_id);
    end if;

    let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

    -- update rms_fms_ari_h
    update rms_fms_ari_h
    set amt=amt+i_gross_amt
    where ari_hid = i_hid;

    -- update rms_mtt_pg
    update rms_mtt_pg
    set in_fms_posting = 1,
        dt_modified = current
    where mtt_pg_id=i_mtt_pg_id;

    commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsmtth(i_customer nvarchar(100))

returning int8 as hid;

define o_batch_no       nvarchar(30);
define o_hid            int8;
define o_result         int;
define runno            nvarchar(30);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

    -- check got overnight anot
    execute procedure sp_getrunno('ARIV') into o_result;

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'ARIV';

    -- get running number
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('ARIV' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_batch_no
    FROM rms_runno
    WHERE runno_cd = 'ARIV';

    -- insert rms_fms_ari_h
    -- geo: dt_sent = current
    INSERT INTO rms_fms_ari_h(type, link_branch, amt, cust, rms_batch_no, 
                                dt_sent, desc, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys, fms_ref_no, 
                                resp_co, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry) 
        VALUES('Invoice', '000', 0, i_customer, o_batch_no 
                , current, 'Collection with Receipt', 'RMS', null, null
                , null, null, null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0);

    let o_hid = dbinfo('serial8');

    commit work;

return o_hid;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsrcpgmtt(i_rc_pg_id INT8,
											i_pg_pymt_method NVARCHAR(3),
											i_mtt_pg_id INT8,
											i_qty INT,
											i_item_desc NVARCHAR(150),
											i_unit_fee DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_entity_nm NVARCHAR(100),
											i_entity_no NVARCHAR(20),
											i_entity_type NVARCHAR(1),
											i_gross_amt DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10),
											i_tax_amt DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_rcpt_no NVARCHAR(20),
											i_cust_nm NVARCHAR(255),
											i_pg_pymt_amt DECIMAL(16,2))
returning int as result;

	define o_fms_acct_cd NVARCHAR(10);
	define o_fms_ref_no NVARCHAR(25); 
	
	define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	define o_hid int8;
	define o_result int;
	 

	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;
	 
	begin work;
	set lock mode to wait 30;
	
						 
						   
   

			
	execute procedure sp_getrunno('DN');
	
	update rms_runno
	set last_runno = last_runno + 1
	where runno_cd = 'DN';
	
	select first 1 ('DN' || to_char(today, '%y%m%d') || lpad(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
	into o_batch_no
	from rms_runno;
					   
	
				
					
				   
	select acct_cd into o_fms_acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'AR Invoice''s RMS PG MID Account ID';
	
	-- insert into rms_fms_drmemo_h
	insert into rms_fms_drmemo_h (
		type, link_branch, amt, cust, rms_batch_no, dt_sent, desc, 
		attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys, fms_ref_no, resp_co, resp_status, 
		resp_msg, resp_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
		status, retry
	) values (
		'Debit Memo', '000', i_pg_pymt_amt, o_fms_acct_cd, o_batch_no, current, 'Debit Note Batch', 
		'RMS', null, null, null, null, 
		null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
		'A', 0
	);
	 
	let o_hid = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd1');

								
							   
																 
														 
																		
							   
		   
																		 
																			  
																	 
												  
   
	
	foreach c_arr for
				   
								  
		select distinct t3.fms_ref_no
		into o_fms_ref_no
		from rms_rc_pgmtt t1
		left join rms_fms_ari_b t2 on t1.mtt_pg_id = t2.mtt_pg_id
									
 
								 
					 
						 
		left join rms_fms_ari_h t3 on t2.ari_hid = t3.ari_hid
		where t1.rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id

		
		-- insert into rms_fms_drmemo_f
		insert into rms_fms_drmemo_f (
			drmemo_hid, fms_ref_no, doc_ty, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, 
			modified_by, status
		) values (
			o_hid, o_fms_ref_no, 'Invoice', current, current, 'system', 
			'system', 'A'
			 
  
			
																 
				  
		);
	 
		-- insert into rms_fms_drmemo_b
		insert into rms_fms_drmemo_b (
			drmemo_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, txn_desc, unit_price, 
			rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, 
			pymt, item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
			status, mtt_pg_id, coa1, coa2
		) values (
			o_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, 
			i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, i_entity_no, i_entity_type, i_gross_amt, 
			i_pg_pymt_method, i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
			'A', i_mtt_pg_id, o_fms_acct_cd, i_fee_detail_id
		);
	end foreach;
	 
	update rms_mtt_pg
	set in_fms_posting = 1, 
		dt_modified = current
	where mtt_id = i_mtt_id;
	 
	let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

				  
	 
	if (o_result > 0) then
	    commit work;
	    return o_result;
	else
	    rollback work;
	    return -1;
	end if;
 
end procedure;
GO
		
																  
										 
							 
					  
									  
									 
									  
									 
									  
									  
										 
									
								   
									
						

								   
					 

			 
				
			   
  
			
						  
 
				
					
				   
											  
 

								
							   
																 
														 
																		
							   
		   
																				
																			  
																	 
												  
   
  
										 
  
					   
				 
					 
	 
				   
			   
		
 
			  
  
																  
								
						

						
					   
									  

				
				
			   
  
			
						  

						
							
								 
	  

						  
									
								 
						 
														  
									 
						   
   
					 
   
															  
			
						 
					   
			   
	 
									 
						
					
							 
									   
									   

											  
						   
										  
																					
								   
					  
																				   
							 
			  
										
			   
				

											  

					  
					 

						  
					
						
		
					  
				  
		   

			  
  
		
																		   

							  

								   
								
				   
					 
					  

			 
				
			   
  
			
						  

			
													

				 
								
					   
 
																					 
				
			   
					   
 
				
					
				   
											  
 
								
							   
															 
																	 
																	   
			   
		   
																								
								 
													
		
   
  
							   
  
										 
  
					   
				 
				  
	 
				   
			   
		
 
			  
  
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsrcpgtxn(i_rc_pg_id INT8,
											i_pg_pymt_method NVARCHAR(3),
											i_mtt_pg_id INT8,
											i_qty INT,
											i_item_desc NVARCHAR(150),
											i_unit_fee DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_entity_nm NVARCHAR(100),
											i_entity_no NVARCHAR(20),
											i_entity_type NVARCHAR(1),
											i_gross_amt DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10),
											i_tax_amt DECIMAL(16,2),
											i_rcpt_no NVARCHAR(20),
											i_cust_nm NVARCHAR(255),
											i_pg_pymt_amt DECIMAL(16,2))
returning int as result;

	define o_fms_acct_cd NVARCHAR(10);
	define o_fms_ref_no NVARCHAR(25); 
	
	define o_batch_no nvarchar(30);
	define o_hid int8;
	define o_result int;
	 
	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;

	set lock mode to wait 30;
	
	execute procedure sp_getrunno('CN');

	set last_runno = last_runno + 1
	where runno_cd = 'CN';

	into o_batch_no
	from rms_runno;

	-- insert into rms_fms_crmemo_h

		type, link_branch, amt, cust, rms_batch_no, dt_sent, desc,

		resp_msg, resp_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by,

	) values (
		'Credit Memo', '000', i_pg_pymt_amt, o_fms_acct_cd, o_batch_no, current, 'Credit Note Batch', 
		'RMS', null, null, null, null, 
		null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
		'A', 0
	);
	 
	let o_hid = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd1');
	
	foreach c_arr for
		select distinct t3.fms_ref_no
		into o_fms_ref_no
		from rms_rc_pgmtt t1
		left join rms_fms_ari_b t2 on t1.mtt_pg_id = t2.mtt_pg_id
		left join rms_fms_ari_h t3 on t2.ari_hid = t3.ari_hid
		where t1.rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id
		
		-- insert into rms_fms_crmemo_f
		insert into rms_fms_crmemo_f (
			crmemo_hid, fms_ref_no, doc_ty, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by,

		) values (
			o_hid, o_fms_ref_no, 'Invoice', current, current, 'system', 
			'system', 'A'
		);
	 
		-- insert into rms_fms_crmemo_b
		insert into rms_fms_crmemo_b (
			crmemo_hid, acct, branch, qty, sub_acct, txn_desc, unit_price, 
			rcpt_no, payee_info, ent_nm, ent_no, ent_ty, item_amt, 
			pymt, item_tax_amt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
			status, mtt_pg_id, coa1, coa2
		) values (
			o_hid, null, '000', i_qty, '000000000000000', i_item_desc, i_unit_fee, 
			i_rcpt_no, i_cust_nm, i_entity_nm, i_entity_no, i_entity_type, i_gross_amt, 
			i_pg_pymt_method, i_tax_amt, current, current, 'system', 'system', 
			'A', i_mtt_pg_id, o_fms_acct_cd, i_fee_detail_id
		);
	end foreach;
	 
	update rms_mtt_pg
	set in_fms_posting = 1, 
		dt_modified = current
	where mtt_id = i_mtt_id;
	 
	let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

create or replace procedure sp_insfmsricpa(i_audit_id int8, i_ricp_id int8, i_dt_txn date, i_accr_amt_af decimal(16,2), i_action_type nvarchar(10))
returning int8 as result;

define o_hid            int8;
define o_batch_no       nvarchar(30);
define o_result         int8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    execute procedure sp_getrunno('JNCP') into o_result;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'JNCP';

    /* Select running no */
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('JNCP' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_batch_no
    FROM rms_runno
    WHERE runno_cd = 'JNCP';

    insert into rms_fms_jn_h(batch_no, branch_id, desc, ledger_id, module, dt_txn, attr_ext_ref_no, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys, fms_ref_no, resp_ext_ref_no, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry) 
    values(o_batch_no, '000', 'GL RMS', 'ACTUAL', 'GL', DATE(i_dt_txn), 'CP-' || i_ricp_id || '-' || i_audit_id, 'RMS', null, null, null, null, null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0);

    let o_hid = dbinfo('serial8');

    if i_action_type like '%I' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'RI/CMP'), '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', 'RC', '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type like '%WO' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000','CP Write Off Debit Account', '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', 'CP Write Off Credit Account', '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type like '%C' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000','CP Cancel Debit Account', '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000','CP Cancel Credit Account', '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type like '%V' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', 'CP Void Debit Account', '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', 'CP Void Credit Account', '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');              
    end if;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    if (o_result > 0) then
        update rms_ricp_a
        set in_fms_posting = 1,
        dt_modified = current
        where audit_id = i_audit_id;
    end if;

    commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insfmsripla(i_audit_id int8, i_ripl_id int8, i_dt_txn date, i_accr_amt_af decimal(16,2), i_action_type nvarchar(10))
returning int8 as result;

define o_hid            int8;
define o_batch_no       nvarchar(30);
define o_result         int8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

    begin work;
    set lock mode to wait 30;

    execute procedure sp_getrunno('JNPL') into o_result;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'JNPL';

    /* Select running no */
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('JNPL' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_batch_no
    FROM rms_runno
    WHERE runno_cd = 'JNPL';

    insert into rms_fms_jn_h(batch_no, branch_id, desc, ledger_id, module, dt_txn, attr_ext_ref_no, attr_ext_sys, resp_attr_ext_sys, fms_ref_no, resp_ext_ref_no, resp_status, resp_msg, resp_dt, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, retry) 
    values(o_batch_no, '000', 'GL RMS', 'ACTUAL', 'GL', DATE(i_dt_txn), 'PL-' || i_ripl_id || '-' || i_audit_id, 'RMS', null, null, null, null, null, null, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A', 0);

    let o_hid = dbinfo('serial8');

    if i_action_type  like '%R' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Receivable ' || SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2)), '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Revenue ' || SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2)), '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type  = '%RP' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Revenue ' || SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2)), '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = 'Receivable ' || SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2)), '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type  = '%I' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2) || ' Impair Income Statement'), '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2) || ' Impair Balance Sheet'), '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    elif i_action_type  = '%WO' then
        --  debit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2) || ' Write Off Debit Account'), '000000000000000', i_accr_amt_af, 0, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
        --	credit
        insert into rms_fms_jn_b(jn_hid, branch, acct, sub_acct, debit, credit, txn_desc, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values(o_hid, '000', (select acct_cd from rms_fms_acct where acct_nm = SUBSTRING(i_action_type from 1 for 2) || ' Write Off Credit Account'), '000000000000000', 0, i_accr_amt_af, 'RI '||i_action_type, current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A');
    end if;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    if (o_result > 0) then
        update rms_ripl_a
        set in_fms_posting = 1,
        dt_modified = current
        where audit_id = i_audit_id;
    end if;

    commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insmasterfeetable (i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10),i_fee_grp_id integer, i_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100),
i_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100), i_unit_fee decimal, i_promo_startdt date, i_promo_enddt date, i_promo_fee decimal, i_tax_cd_id integer,
i_allow_otc integer, i_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10), i_ll_start_day integer, i_ll_start_mth integer, i_ll_end_day integer, i_ll_end_mth integer,
i_ledger_cd nvarchar(50), i_ss_cd nvarchar(100), i_created_by nvarchar(25),i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_status nvarchar(10)
)
	returning int as row_count;

	define row_count int;

	insert into rms_mft
	(fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_e, fee_detail_nm_b, unit_fee, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
     tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd, dt_created, dt_modified,
     created_by, modified_by, status)
	 values
    (i_fee_detail_id, i_fee_grp_id, i_fee_detail_nm_en, i_fee_detail_nm_bm, i_unit_fee, i_promo_startdt, i_promo_enddt, i_promo_fee,
     i_tax_cd_id, i_allow_otc, i_ll_parent_id, i_ll_start_day, i_ll_start_mth, i_ll_end_day, i_ll_end_mth, i_ledger_cd, i_ss_cd, current, current,
     i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);

	let row_count = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	return row_count;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insmasterfeetablewf (i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10), i_fee_grp_id integer, i_fee_detail_nm_en nvarchar(100),
i_fee_detail_nm_bm nvarchar(100), i_fee_amt decimal, i_promo_startdt date, i_promo_enddt date, i_promo_fee decimal, i_tax_cd_id integer,
i_allow_otc integer, i_ll_parent_id nvarchar(10), i_ll_start_day integer, i_ll_start_mth integer, i_ll_end_day integer, i_ll_end_mth integer,
i_ledger_cd nvarchar(50), i_ss_cd nvarchar(100), i_effective_date date, i_created_by nvarchar(25),i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_status nvarchar(10)
)
	RETURNING int AS row_count;

	DEFINE row_count INT;

	INSERT INTO rms_mft_wf
	(fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_en, fee_detail_nm_bm, fee_amt, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
     tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd, effective_date, dt_created, dt_modified,
     created_by, modified_by, status)
	 VALUES
    (i_fee_detail_id, i_fee_grp_id, i_fee_detail_nm_en, i_fee_detail_nm_bm, i_fee_amt, i_promo_startdt, i_promo_enddt, i_promo_fee,
     i_tax_cd_id, i_allow_otc, i_ll_parent_id, i_ll_start_day, i_ll_start_mth, i_ll_end_day, i_ll_end_mth, i_ledger_cd, i_ss_cd, i_effective_date, current, current,
     i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);

	LET row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	RETURN row_count;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insmasterfeetablewfhis (i_action NVARCHAR(50),i_act_by NVARCHAR(25), 
i_assign_to NVARCHAR(25),i_remark NVARCHAR(200),  i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),i_status NVARCHAR(10) )

RETURNING INT AS row_count;

	DEFINE row_count INT;
	DEFINE current_mtfwf_id INT;

    SELECT MAX(wf_id) 
    INTO current_mtfwf_id 
    FROM rms_mft_wf;


	INSERT INTO ssm_rms:rms_mft_wfhist
	(wf_id, action, dt_activity, act_by, assign_to, remark, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by,status)
	VALUES
	(current_mtfwf_id, i_action,current, i_act_by, i_assign_to, i_remark, current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);

	SELECT COUNT(1) 
	INTO row_count
	FROM rms_mft_wfhist
	WHERE wf_id=current_mtfwf_id and status='A';

	RETURN row_count;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insmftwf (i_fee_detail_pk int, i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10), i_fee_grp_id INT, i_fee_detail_nm_e NVARCHAR(100), i_fee_detail_nm_b NVARCHAR(100),
						i_fee_amt DECIMAL, i_promo_startdt DATE, i_promo_enddt DATE, i_promo_fee DECIMAL, i_tax_cd_id INT, i_allow_otc INT,
						i_ll_parent_id NVARCHAR(10), i_ll_start_day INT, i_ll_start_mth INT, i_ll_end_day INT, i_ll_end_mth INT,
						i_ledger_cd NVARCHAR(50), i_ss_cd NVARCHAR(100), i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10),
						i_effective_date DATE, i_remark LVARCHAR(500), i_assign_to NVARCHAR(25), i_action NVARCHAR(50), i_r_fee_det_nm NVARCHAR(100),
						i_r_fee_amt DECIMAL, i_r_ss_cd NVARCHAR(100), i_r_promo_startdt DATE, i_r_promo_enddt DATE, i_r_ll_required INT, i_r_add_notes LVARCHAR(500),
						i_mft_status NVARCHAR(10), i_r_promo_fee DECIMAL)

RETURNING INT8 as wf_id;


	DEFINE o_wf_id INT8;
	DEFINE o_current_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
    define o_insresult int8;

BEGIN WORK;	
	
	/*Set current date time*/
	let o_current_dt = current;
	
	
	/*Insert data into MFT WF table*/
	INSERT INTO rms_mft_wf
		(fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_e, fee_detail_nm_b, fee_amt, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
		 tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth,ll_end_day, ll_end_mth,
		  ledger_cd, ss_cd, effective_date, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, assign_to, action,
		  r_fee_det_nm, r_fee_amt, r_ss_cd, r_promo_startdt, r_promo_enddt, r_ll_required, r_add_notes, mft_status, r_promo_fee)
	VALUES 
		(i_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, i_fee_grp_id, i_fee_detail_nm_e, i_fee_detail_nm_b, i_fee_amt, i_promo_startdt, i_promo_enddt, i_promo_fee,
		i_tax_cd_id, i_allow_otc, i_ll_parent_id, i_ll_start_day, i_ll_start_mth, i_ll_end_day, i_ll_end_mth,
		i_ledger_cd, i_ss_cd, i_effective_date, o_current_dt, o_current_dt, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status, i_assign_to,i_action,
		i_r_fee_det_nm, i_r_fee_amt, i_r_ss_cd, i_r_promo_startdt, i_r_promo_enddt, i_r_ll_required, i_r_add_notes, i_mft_status, i_r_promo_fee);
		
	/*Get latest Serial8 ID number from last inserted records*/
	LET o_wf_id = DBINFO('Serial8');
	
	
	/*Exec insertMFTWFHist stored procedure*/
    /*CALL sp_insmftwfhis(o_wf_id, i_action, o_current_dt,i_created_by, i_assign_to, i_remark, i_created_by, i_modified_by,i_status);*/
	execute procedure sp_insmftwfhis(o_wf_id, i_action, o_current_dt,i_created_by, i_assign_to, i_remark, i_created_by, i_modified_by,i_status) into o_insresult;

    
COMMIT WORK;
	
RETURN o_wf_id;

END PROCEDURE
GO

let o_result = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

create or replace procedure sp_insmftwfhis (i_wf_id INT8, i_action NVARCHAR(50), i_dt_activity DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
						i_act_by NVARCHAR(25), i_assign_to NVARCHAR(25), i_remarks LVARCHAR(500), 
						i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10))
returning int8 as result;

define o_result int8;

	/*Insert data into MFT WF History table*/
	INSERT INTO rms_mft_wfhist
		(wf_id, action, dt_activity, act_by, assign_to, remark, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status)
	VALUES 
		(i_wf_id, i_action , i_dt_activity, i_modified_by, i_assign_to, i_remarks, i_dt_activity, i_dt_activity, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);

        let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

return o_result;

END PROCEDURE

create or replace procedure sp_insmftwfhiswithhid(i_wf_id INT, i_action NVARCHAR(50),i_act_by NVARCHAR(25), 
i_assign_to NVARCHAR(25),i_remark NVARCHAR(200),  i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),i_status NVARCHAR(10) )

returning INT as row_count;

	Define row_count INT;

	INSERT INTO ssm_rms:rms_mft_wfhist
	(wf_id, action, dt_activity, act_by, assign_to, remark, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by,status)
	VALUES
	(i_wf_id, i_action,current, i_act_by, i_assign_to, i_remark, current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status);

	SELECT COUNT(1)
	INTO row_count
	FROM rms_mft_wfhist
	WHERE wf_id = i_wf_id AND status = 'A';

	RETURN row_count;

END PROCEDURE;

CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_insmttrcpt(i_pg_pymt_id NVARCHAR(20),i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25))
returning INT8 AS mtt_rcpt_id,
                     INT8 AS mtt_id,
                     INT8 AS mtt_pg_id,
                     NVARCHAR(20) AS rcpt_no,
                     DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS rcpt_dt,
                     NVARCHAR(10) AS rcpt_status,
                     INT AS rcpt_reprint,
                     INT AS is_uploaded,
                     DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND AS dt_created,
                     DATETIME YEAr TO SECOND AS dt_modified,
                     NVARCHAR(25) AS created_by,
                     NVARCHAR(25) AS modified_by;

DEFINE o_mtt_rcpt_id INT8;
DEFINE o_mtt_id INT8;
DEFINE o_mtt_pg_id INT8;
DEFINE o_rcpt_no NVARCHAR(20);
DEFINE o_rcpt_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_rcpt_status NVARCHAR(10);
DEFINE o_rcpt_reprint INT;
DEFINE o_is_uploaded INT;
DEFINE o_dt_created DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_dt_modified DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_created_by NVARCHAR(25);
DEFINE o_modified_by NVARCHAR(25);

DEFINE i_mtt_id INT8;
DEFINE i_mtt_pg_id INT8;
DEFINE o_result int;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

EXECUTE PROCEDURE sp_getrunno('OR') into o_result;

/* UPDATE last running no */
UPDATE rms_runno
SET last_runno = last_runno +1
WHERE runno_cd = 'OR';

/* Select running no */
SELECT FIRST 1 ('OR' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
INTO o_rcpt_no
FROM rms_runno;

SELECT mtt_pg_id, mtt_id 
INTO i_mtt_pg_id,i_mtt_id
FROM rms_mtt_pg
WHERE pg_pymt_id = i_pg_pymt_id;

INSERT INTO rms_mtt_rcpt(mtt_id, mtt_pg_id, rcpt_no, rcpt_dt, rcpt_status, rcpt_reprint, is_uploaded, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by) 
	VALUES(i_mtt_id, i_mtt_pg_id, o_rcpt_no, current, 'A', 0, 0, current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by);

LET o_mtt_rcpt_id = DBINFO('serial8') ;

commit work;

SELECT first 1 mtt_rcpt_id, mtt_id, mtt_pg_id, rcpt_no, rcpt_dt, rcpt_status, rcpt_reprint, is_uploaded, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by 
INTO o_mtt_rcpt_id, o_mtt_id, o_mtt_pg_id, o_rcpt_no, o_rcpt_dt, o_rcpt_status, o_rcpt_reprint, o_is_uploaded,  o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by
FROM rms_mtt_rcpt
WHERE mtt_rcpt_id = o_mtt_rcpt_id;

--let o_rcpt_no = 'PG' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(o_mtt_rcpt_id, 6, '0');

RETURN  o_mtt_rcpt_id, o_mtt_id, o_mtt_pg_id, o_rcpt_no, o_rcpt_dt, o_rcpt_status, o_rcpt_reprint, o_is_uploaded,  o_dt_created, o_dt_modified, o_created_by, o_modified_by;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
/*
Remarks:
o - output
f - formatted
i - input
*/
CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_inspayment(
	i_mtt_id INT,
	i_pg_pymt_method NVARCHAR(3),
	i_pg_service_id NVARCHAR(3),
	i_pg_pymt_amt DECIMAL,
	i_pg_lang_cd NVARCHAR(2),
	i_username_c NVARCHAR(25),
	i_username_m NVARCHAR(25)
	)
 
	RETURNING 	NVARCHAR(20) AS pymt_id,
				NVARCHAR(7) AS transaction_type,
				NVARCHAR(3) AS pymt_method,
				NVARCHAR(3) AS service_id,
				NVARCHAR(20) AS ord_no,
				NVARCHAR(100) AS pymt_desc,
				NVARCHAR(1) AS return_url,
				DECIMAL(16,2) AS amt,
				NVARCHAR(3) AS curr_cd,
				NVARCHAR(45) AS cust_ip,
				NVARCHAR(255) AS cust_nm,
				NVARCHAR(15) AS cust_ph,
				NVARCHAR(1) AS hash_value,
				NVARCHAR(255) AS page_timeout,
                NVARCHAR(150) AS cust_email;
 
	DEFINE o_pymt_id NVARCHAR(20);
	DEFINE o_pg_txn_type NVARCHAR(7);
	DEFINE o_pg_pymt_method NVARCHAR(3);
	DEFINE o_pg_service_id NVARCHAR(3);
	DEFINE o_orn_no NVARCHAR(20);
	DEFINE o_pg_pymt_desc NVARCHAR(100);
	DEFINE o_pg_pymt_amt DECIMAL(16,2);
	DEFINE o_pg_curr_cd NVARCHAR(3);
	DEFINE o_cust_ip NVARCHAR(45);
	DEFINE o_cust_nm NVARCHAR(255);
	DEFINE o_cust_ph NVARCHAR(15);
	DEFINE o_page_timeout NVARCHAR(255);
	DEFINE o_return_url NVARCHAR(1);
	DEFINE o_hash_value NVARCHAR(1);
	DEFINE o_f_pymt_id NVARCHAR(20);
    DEFINE o_result int;
    DEFINE o_cust_email NVARCHAR(150);

-- vicky change the pg to mgo due to ssm using pg to submit payment, and eghl cannot accept duplicate pg number
BEGIN WORK; 
 
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE sp_getrunno('MPG') into o_result;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'MPG';

    /* Select running no */
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('MPG' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_f_pymt_id
    FROM rms_runno
    WHERE runno_cd = 'MPG';

 	LET o_return_url = '';
 	LET o_hash_value = '';
 
	INSERT INTO rms_mtt_pg (
    	mtt_id, pymt_submit_dt, pg_txn_type, pg_pymt_method, pg_service_id, pg_pymt_desc, pg_pymt_amt,
    	pg_curr_cd, pg_lang_cd, pg_txn_status,dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by,pg_pymt_id
	)
	VALUES (
	    i_mtt_id, current, 'SALE', i_pg_pymt_method, i_pg_service_id, 'Payment to Suruhanjaya Syarikat Malaysia',
	    i_pg_pymt_amt, 'MYR', i_pg_lang_cd, 2,CURRENT, CURRENT, i_username_c, i_username_m,o_f_pymt_id
	); -- default pg_txn_status = 2
 
	SELECT FIRST 1 config_value
	INTO o_page_timeout
	FROM rms_config
	WHERE config_cd = 'PIP_BlockPayOnline_In_Minute';
	
	/*Return last inserted record row data*/
	SELECT FIRST 1 t1.pg_txn_type, t1.pg_pymt_method ,t1.pg_service_id, t2.orn_no, t1.pg_pymt_desc, t1.pg_pymt_amt, t1.pg_curr_cd, t2.cust_ip, t2.cust_nm, t2.cust_phone,t2.cust_email
	INTO o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_orn_no, o_pg_pymt_desc, o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_cust_ip, o_cust_nm, o_cust_ph,o_cust_email
	FROM rms_mtt_pg t1
	LEFT OUTER JOIN rms_mtt t2 ON t1.mtt_id = t2.mtt_id
	WHERE t1.pg_pymt_id = o_f_pymt_id;

COMMIT WORK;
	
RETURN o_f_pymt_id,o_pg_txn_type, o_pg_pymt_method, o_pg_service_id, o_orn_no, o_pg_pymt_desc, o_return_url,
	o_pg_pymt_amt, o_pg_curr_cd, o_cust_ip, o_cust_nm, o_cust_ph, o_hash_value,o_page_timeout,o_cust_email;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE sp_inspaymentmtt(i_rms_type nvarchar(10),i_ss_cd nvarchar(10),i_orn_no nvarchar(20),i_orn_dt DATETIME YEAR TO FRACTION(5) DEFAULT CURRENT YEAR TO FRACTION(5),
	i_cust_ip nvarchar(45),i_cust_nm nvarchar(255),i_cust_addr_1 nvarchar(155),i_cust_addr_2 nvarchar(155),i_cust_addr_3 nvarchar(155),
	i_cust_postcode nvarchar(15),i_cust_city nvarchar(50),i_cust_state  nvarchar(50),i_cust_email nvarchar(155),i_cust_phone nvarchar(15),
	i_total_amt decimal,i_ss_return_url lvarchar(2000),i_username_c nvarchar(25), i_username_m nvarchar(25))
	RETURNING INT AS mtt_id;
 
	DEFINE o_mtt_id INT;
    DEFINE o_orn_no_exists INT;
    DEFINE o_chckpnt INT;
 
    BEGIN WORK;
    set lock mode to wait 30;
 
    SELECT COUNT(1)
    INTO o_orn_no_exists
    FROM rms_mtt
    WHERE orn_no = UPPER(i_orn_no);
    IF o_orn_no_exists = 0 THEN
        INSERT INTO rms_mtt (
            rms_type, ss_cd, orn_no, orn_dt, cust_ip, cust_nm, cust_addr_1, cust_addr_2, cust_addr_3, cust_postcode, 
            cust_city, cust_state, cust_email, cust_phone, total_amt, ss_return_url,order_status , dt_created, dt_modified, 
            created_by, modified_by
        )
        VALUES (
            i_rms_type, i_ss_cd, UPPER(i_orn_no), i_orn_dt, i_cust_ip, i_cust_nm, i_cust_addr_1, i_cust_addr_2, i_cust_addr_3, i_cust_postcode, 
            i_cust_city, i_cust_state, i_cust_email, i_cust_phone, i_total_amt, i_ss_return_url,'PIP', current, current, i_username_c, i_username_m
        );
        LET o_mtt_id = DBINFO('serial8');
        LET o_chckpnt = 1;
	    --RETURN o_mtt_id;
    ELSE --Means this orn no is exist
        LET o_chckpnt = 2;
        UPDATE rms_mtt
        SET order_status = 'PIP',
        rms_type = i_rms_type,
        ss_cd = i_ss_cd,
        orn_dt=i_orn_dt,
        cust_ip= i_cust_ip,
        cust_nm = i_cust_nm,
        cust_addr_1 = i_cust_addr_1,
        cust_addr_2 = i_cust_addr_2,
        cust_addr_3 = i_cust_addr_3,
        cust_postcode = i_cust_postcode,
        cust_city = i_cust_city,
        cust_state = i_cust_state,
        cust_email = i_cust_email,
        cust_phone = i_cust_phone,
        total_amt = i_total_amt,
        ss_return_url = i_ss_return_url,
        dt_modified = current,
        modified_by=i_username_m
        WHERE orn_no = UPPER(i_orn_no);
        select mtt_id 
        into o_mtt_id
        from rms_mtt 
        WHERE orn_no = UPPER(i_orn_no);
        --RETURN -1;
        -- delete existing item
        DELETE rms_mtt_item
        where mtt_id = o_mtt_id;
    END IF;
COMMIT WORK;
IF o_chckpnt = 1 or o_chckpnt = 2  THEN
    RETURN o_mtt_id;
ELSE
    RETURN 0;
END IF;
END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_inspaymentmttitem(
	i_mtt_id int,
	i_fee_detail_id nvarchar(10),
	i_item_ref_no nvarchar(30),
	i_item_desc nvarchar(30),
	i_line_no int,
	i_qty int,
	i_unit_fee decimal,
	i_gross_amt decimal,
	i_grant_cd nvarchar(50),
	i_disc_amt decimal,
	i_tax_pct decimal,
	i_tax_amt decimal,
	i_net_amt decimal,
	i_entity_type nvarchar(1),
	i_entity_no nvarchar(20),
	i_entity_nm nvarchar(100),
	i_cp_no nvarchar(20),
	i_cp_tier int,
	i_cp_tier_amt decimal,
	i_cp_tier_disc_pct decimal,
	i_username_c varchar(25),
	i_username_m varchar(25)
	)

	returning int as mtt_item_id;

	DEFINE o_mtt_item_id int;
	define i_fee_detail_pk int;
    DEFINE o_exist INT;

    
    SELECT COUNT(1)
    INTO o_exist
    FROM rms_mtt_item
    WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no;

    IF o_exist = 0 THEN 

        SELECT first 1 fee_detail_pk
        INTO i_fee_detail_pk
        FROM informix.rms_mft 
        WHERE fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id;

        INSERT INTO rms_mtt_item(
            mtt_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, item_ref_no, item_desc, line_no, qty, unit_fee, gross_amt, grant_cd, 
            disc_amt, tax_pct, tax_amt, net_amt, entity_type, entity_no, entity_nm, cp_no, cp_tier, cp_tier_amt, cp_tier_discpct, 
            dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by)
        VALUES(
            i_mtt_id, i_fee_detail_pk, i_fee_detail_id, i_item_ref_no, i_item_desc, i_line_no, i_qty, i_unit_fee, i_gross_amt, 
            i_grant_cd,i_disc_amt, i_tax_pct, i_tax_amt, i_net_amt, i_entity_type, i_entity_no, i_entity_nm, i_cp_no, i_cp_tier, 
            i_cp_tier_amt, i_cp_tier_disc_pct,current, current, i_username_c, i_username_m
        );

        SELECT first 1 mtt_item_id
        INTO o_mtt_item_id
        FROM rms_mtt_item
        WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no;

        IF (o_mtt_item_id IS NULL OR o_mtt_item_id < 1) THEN
          -- Set 'a' to -1
          LET o_mtt_item_id = -1;
        END IF;

    ELSE 

        UPDATE rms_mtt_item 
        SET  dt_modified=current, 
                modified_by=i_username_m
        WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no; 

        SELECT first 1 mtt_item_id
        INTO o_mtt_item_id
        FROM rms_mtt_item
        WHERE mtt_id = i_mtt_id and item_ref_no = i_item_ref_no;

        IF (o_mtt_item_id IS NULL OR o_mtt_item_id < 1) THEN
          -- Set 'a' to -1
          LET o_mtt_item_id = -1;
        END IF;
        
    END IF;
	
	RETURN o_mtt_item_id;

END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insperm()
returning int as row_count;
define o_row_count int;


DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'TCD001';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'TCD002';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'TCD003';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'FG001';

DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'FG003';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT001';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT002';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT003';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT004';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT005';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT006';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT007';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT008';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT009';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT010';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT011';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT012';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT013';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT014';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT015';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT016';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'MFT017';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'FMS001';
DELETE FROM rms_perm where perm_cd = 'FMS002';
