CREATE or replace PROCEDURE informix.sp_inspg(i_dt_settlement NVARCHAR(100),i_merchant_id NVARCHAR(25),i_stmt_no NVARCHAR(25),i_dt_statement NVARCHAR(100),
                                        i_total_txn decimal(16,2),i_total_refund decimal(16,2),i_total_adj decimal(16,2),
                                        i_total_others decimal(16,2),i_total_paid decimal(16,2),i_bal_bfwd decimal(16,2),
                                        i_bal_cfwd decimal(16,2),i_file_nm NVARCHAR(255), i_file_content BLOB, i_file_type NVARCHAR(5), 
                                        i_file_size_kb INT,i_created_by NVARCHAR(25), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25))
returning int as result;											

define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
define o_runno nvarchar(25);
define o_rc_pg_id NVARCHAR(20);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

-- Set a default value for o_result
LET o_result = 0;


set lock mode to wait 30;

-- check exist settlement's status
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pg
where dt_settlement = to_date(i_dt_settlement,'%d/%m/%Y')
and task_status = 'O';

if o_exist < 1 then

--	let o_runno = 'RC2024061100010';

   BEGIN WORK; 

    -- get latest running no
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE sp_getrunno('RC') into o_result;

    /* UPDATE last running no */
    UPDATE rms_runno
    SET last_runno = last_runno +1
    WHERE runno_cd = 'RC';

    /* Select running no */
    SELECT FIRST 1 ('RC' || TO_CHAR(TODAY, '%Y%m%d') || LPAD(last_runno, 6,0)) as run_no
    INTO o_runno
    FROM rms_runno
    where runno_cd = 'RC';

    -- insert rms_rc_pg
    INSERT INTO rms_rc_pg(task_no, dt_settlement, dt_upload, merchant_id, task_status, 
                    recon_status, dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                    stmt_no, dt_statement, total_txn, total_refund, total_adj, 
                    total_others, total_paid, bal_bfwd, remarks, bal_cfwd) 
        VALUES(o_runno, to_date(i_dt_settlement,'%d/%m/%Y'), current, i_merchant_id, 'O', 
                'PE', current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, 
                i_stmt_no, to_date(i_dt_statement,'%m/%d/%Y'), i_total_txn, i_total_refund, i_total_adj, 
                i_total_others, i_total_paid, i_bal_bfwd, '', i_bal_cfwd);

    -- get inserted id



    let o_rc_pg_id = dbinfo('serial8');

    -- insert rms_rc_pgdoc
    INSERT INTO rms_rc_pgdoc( rc_pg_id, file_nm, file_content, file_type, file_size_kb, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        VALUES( o_rc_pg_id, i_file_nm, i_file_content, i_file_type, i_file_size_kb, 
                current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, 'A');

    -- get inserted id



    let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

   COMMIT WORK; 
else
    let o_result = -2;
end if;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_inspgmtttxn(i_rc_pg_id int8) -- to get settlement date
returning int8 as result;
 
define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
define o_compare_range int;
define o_dt_settlement date;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
 
-- Set a default value
LET o_result = '0';
 
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- create a temporary table
create temp table temppgmtt (
    rc_pg_id int8,
    mtt_pg_id int8,
    found_in_pg int,
    sub_criteria nvarchar(10)
);
 
-- check exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pg
where rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id;
 
if o_exist > 0 then

    -- get settlement date
    select dt_settlement
    into o_dt_settlement
    from rms_rc_pg
    where rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id;

    -- get compare range
    select config_value
    into o_compare_range
    from rms_config
    where config_cd='PGRecon_Period_In_Days';

    --select statement
    insert into temppgmtt (mtt_pg_id,rc_pg_id, sub_criteria,found_in_pg)
    SELECT 
        rms_mtt_pg.mtt_pg_id, 
        rms_rc_pgtxn.rc_pg_id,
        CASE 
            WHEN rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_id IS NULL THEN 'NF' 
            WHEN rms_mtt_pg.pg_txn_status = 1 THEN 'TXF' 
            WHEN rms_mtt_pg.pg_pymt_amt = rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_amt THEN 'SAM' 
            ELSE 'SNM' 
        END AS status,
        CASE 
            WHEN rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_id IS NULL THEN 0 
            ELSE 1 
        END AS found_in
    FROM 
        rms_mtt_pg 
    LEFT JOIN 
        rms_rc_pgtxn 
    ON 
        rms_mtt_pg.pg_txn_id = rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_id 
    WHERE rms_mtt_pg.pg_txn_id is not null and rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_cd='Settlement'
    and DATE(rms_mtt_pg.pymt_submit_dt) = o_dt_settlement;
								 

    --and DATE(rms_mtt_pg.pymt_submit_dt) <= o_dt_settlement and DATE(rms_mtt_pg.pymt_submit_dt) >= (o_dt_settlement -o_compare_range UNITS DAY);

    -- insert rms_rc_pgmtt
    INSERT INTO informix.rms_rc_pgmtt( rc_pg_id, mtt_pg_id, found_in_pg, sub_criteria, 
                                        dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
    select rc_pg_id, mtt_pg_id, found_in_pg, sub_criteria,current, current, 'system', 'system', 'A'
    from temppgmtt;
 
    -- get inserted id
    let o_result = DBINFO('Serial8');

    -- update rms_rc_pg'recon_status
    update rms_rc_pg
    set recon_status ='PSSCR'
    where rc_pg_id =i_rc_pg_id;

drop table temppgmtt;
 
end if;
 
commit work;
 
if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;
 
end procedure
GO
CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_inspgtxn(i_rc_pg_id int8,i_dt_txn NVARCHAR(100),i_txn_id NVARCHAR(50),i_txn_type NVARCHAR(25),i_txn_cd NVARCHAR(25),
                            i_txn_amt decimal(16,2),i_mdr_amt decimal(16,2),i_sst_amt decimal(16,2),i_net_amt decimal(16,2),
                            i_created_by NVARCHAR(25),i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25))
returning int8 as result;
 
define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
define o_exist_in_rms int;
define o_mtt_pg_status nvarchar(25);
define o_mtt_pg_amt decimal(16,2);
define o_amt_match int;
define o_sub_cri NVARCHAR(10);
define o_mtt_pg_id int8;
 
on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
 
-- Set a default value
LET o_result = '0';
LET o_mtt_pg_status = '';
LET o_mtt_pg_amt=0;
LET o_exist_in_rms=0;
LET o_sub_cri='NFR';
LET o_mtt_pg_id = null;
 
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;
 
-- check exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pg
where rc_pg_id = i_rc_pg_id;
 
if o_exist > 0 then
 
    -- check the txnID exist in rms
    select count(1)
    into o_exist_in_rms
    from rms_mtt_pg
    where pg_txn_id=SUBSTR(i_txn_id, 9)
    and i_txn_cd=='Settlement';
 
    if o_exist_in_rms >0 then
 
        -- check the txnID exist in rms
        select pg_txn_status,pg_pymt_amt,mtt_pg_id
        into o_mtt_pg_status,o_mtt_pg_amt,o_mtt_pg_id
        from rms_mtt_pg
        where pg_txn_id=SUBSTR(i_txn_id, 9);
 
    end if;
 
    -- if the payment status = Failed
    if o_mtt_pg_status=='1' then
        let o_sub_cri='TXF';
    end if;
 
    -- if the payment status = Paid
    if o_mtt_pg_status=='0' then
 
        -- if the payment amount is same
        if o_mtt_pg_amt == i_txn_amt then
            let o_sub_cri='SAM';
        end if;
 
        -- if the payment amoount is not same
        if o_mtt_pg_amt <> i_txn_amt then
            let o_sub_cri='SNM';
        end if;
 
    end if;

    -- if the payment status = Paid
    if o_mtt_pg_status=='-1' then
 
        let o_sub_cri='NFR';
 
    end if;
 
    -- insert rms_rc_pg_txn
    INSERT INTO rms_rc_pgtxn(rc_pg_id, dt_txn, txn_id, txn_type, txn_cd, 
                            txn_amt, mdr_amt, sst_amt, net_amt, dt_created, 
                            dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, found_in_rms, 
                            sub_criteria,mtt_pg_id) 
	VALUES(i_rc_pg_id, TO_DATE(i_dt_txn, '%m/%d/%Y %I:%M:%S %p'), SUBSTR(i_txn_id, 9),i_txn_type, i_txn_cd,
            i_txn_amt, i_mdr_amt, i_sst_amt, i_net_amt, current, 
            current, i_created_by,i_modified_by,'A', o_exist_in_rms,  
            o_sub_cri,o_mtt_pg_id);
 
    -- get inserted id
    let o_result = DBINFO('Serial8');
 
end if;
 
commit work;
 
if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;
 
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insrcbanktxn(i_rc_bank_id int8, i_rc_bankdoc_id int8, i_acct_no nvarchar(50), i_acct_type nvarchar(50), i_acct_nm nvarchar(50),
                            i_dt_fr date, i_dt_to date, i_total_debit int, i_total_credit int, i_begin_bal nvarchar(20), i_end_bal nvarchar(20),
                        i_dt_txn nvarchar(30), i_dt_posting nvarchar(30), i_txn_desc nvarchar(50), i_txn_ref nvarchar(50),
                     i_debit nvarchar(20), i_credit nvarchar(20), i_source_cd nvarchar(50), i_teller_id nvarchar(50), i_brn_chn nvarchar(50), 
                  i_txn_cd nvarchar(50), i_end_bal2 nvarchar(20), i_virtual_acct nvarchar(50), i_txn_desc2 nvarchar(50),
                i_txn_desc3 nvarchar(50), i_txn_desc4 nvarchar(50), i_dt_expiry date)
returning int8 as result;

define o_begin_bal decimal(15,2);
define o_end_bal decimal(15,2);
define o_debit decimal(15,2);
define o_credit decimal(15,2);
define o_end_bal2 decimal(15,2);
define o_dt_txn datetime year to second;
define o_dt_posting datetime year to second;
define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

if (i_rc_bank_id is null or i_rc_bank_id < 1) 
    or (i_rc_bankdoc_id is null or i_rc_bankdoc_id < 1) 
    or (i_credit is null or i_credit < 1)
    or (i_txn_ref is null or i_txn_ref = "")
then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "Detected parameter is null";
end if;

begin work;

let o_begin_bal = cast(i_begin_bal as decimal(15,2));
let o_end_bal = cast(i_end_bal as decimal(15,2));
let o_debit = cast(i_debit as decimal(15,2));
let o_credit = cast(i_credit as decimal(15,2));
let o_end_bal2 = cast(i_end_bal2 as decimal(15,2));

if i_dt_txn is not null then
    let o_dt_txn = to_date(i_dt_txn, '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S');
else
    let o_dt_txn = null;
end if;

if i_dt_posting is not null then
    let o_dt_posting = to_date(i_dt_posting, '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S');
else 
    let o_dt_posting = null;
end if;

let o_result = 0;

INSERT INTO rms_rc_banktxn(rc_bank_id, rc_bankdoc_id, acct_no, acct_type, acct_nm, 
                    dt_fr, dt_to, total_debit, total_credit, begin_bal, end_bal, dt_txn, dt_posting, 
                txn_desc, txn_ref, debit, credit, source_cd, teller_id, brn_chn, txn_cd, end_bal2, 
            virtual_acct, txn_desc2, txn_desc3, txn_desc4, dt_expiry, 
        dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
	VALUES(i_rc_bank_id, i_rc_bankdoc_id, i_acct_no, i_acct_type, i_acct_nm, 
        i_dt_fr, i_dt_to, i_total_debit, i_total_credit, o_begin_bal, o_end_bal, o_dt_txn, o_dt_posting, 
    i_txn_desc, i_txn_ref, o_debit, o_credit, i_source_cd, i_teller_id, i_brn_chn, i_txn_cd, o_end_bal2, 
  i_virtual_acct, i_txn_desc2, i_txn_desc3, i_txn_desc4, i_dt_expiry,
current, current, 'system', 'system', 'PBSR');

let o_result = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_insricp(i_txn_type nvarchar(20), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_calendar_yr nvarchar(5), 
i_cp_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_act_id nvarchar(20), i_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20), i_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20), i_dt_issuance date,

i_created_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_status nvarchar(10), i_cp_tier integer, i_cp_tier_amt decimal)

	returning int as row_count;

	define row_count int;

	insert into rms_ricp
	(txn_type,entity_type,entity_no,calendar_yr,cp_no,cp_act_id,cp_sect_id,cp_sub_sect_id,dt_issuance,dt_expiry,
	dt_void,dt_cancel,dt_writeoff,cp_amt,accr_amt,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,cp_tier,cp_tier_amt)
	 values
    (i_txn_type,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,i_calendar_yr,i_cp_no,i_cp_act_id,i_cp_sect_id,i_cp_sub_sect_id,
   	i_dt_issuance,i_dt_expiry,i_dt_void,i_dt_cancel,i_dt_writeoff,i_cp_amt,i_accr_amt,current,
  	current,i_created_by,i_modified_by,i_status,i_cp_tier,i_cp_tier_amt);

	let row_count = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	return row_count;

end procedure;

	returning int as row_count;

	insert into rms_ricp_a
	(ricp_id,dt_txn,action_type,cp_no,entity_type,entity_no,accr_amt_b4,accr_amt_af,status_b4,status_af,
	dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status)
	 values
    (i_ricp_id,i_dt_txn,i_action_type,i_cp_no,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,i_accr_amt_b4,i_accr_amt_af,i_status_b4,i_status_af,
    current,current,i_created_by,i_modified_by,i_status);

	let row_count = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	return row_count;

end procedure;

create or replace procedure sp_insricpandaudit(i_txn_type nvarchar(20), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_calendar_yr nvarchar(5), 
i_cp_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_act_id nvarchar(20), i_cp_sect_id nvarchar(20), i_cp_sub_sect_id nvarchar(20), i_dt_issuance date, 
i_dt_expiry date, i_dt_void date, i_dt_cancel date, i_cp_amt decimal, i_accr_amt decimal, 
i_created_by nvarchar(25), i_modified_by nvarchar(25), i_status nvarchar(10), i_cp_tier integer, i_cp_tier_amt decimal)

	returning int8 as result;

	define o_exist int;
	define o_result int;
	define o_writeoff_month int;
	define o_dt_writeoff date;

	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;
	
	begin work;
	set lock mode to wait 30;

	-- Duplication checking
	select count(1)
	into o_exist
	from rms_ricp
	where entity_type = i_entity_type
	and entity_no = i_entity_no
	and cp_no = i_cp_no;

	let o_result = 0;

	if o_exist < 1 then
	    -- Get write off month
        select config_value
        into o_writeoff_month
        from rms_config
        where config_cd ='RICP_WriteOff_In_Month'
        and status='A';
        
        -- Calculation for write off
        let o_dt_writeoff = ADD_MONTHS(i_dt_expiry, o_writeoff_month);

		insert into rms_ricp
		(txn_type,entity_type,entity_no,calendar_yr,cp_no,cp_act_id,cp_sect_id,cp_sub_sect_id,dt_issuance,dt_expiry,
		dt_void,dt_cancel,dt_writeoff,cp_amt,accr_amt,dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status,cp_tier,cp_tier_amt)
		 values
	    (i_txn_type,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,i_calendar_yr,i_cp_no,i_cp_act_id,i_cp_sect_id,i_cp_sub_sect_id,
	   	i_dt_issuance,i_dt_expiry,i_dt_void,i_dt_cancel,o_dt_writeoff,i_cp_amt,i_accr_amt,current,
	  	current,i_created_by,i_modified_by,i_status,i_cp_tier,i_cp_tier_amt);
	
	    -- Set rows effected in variable
	    let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

	   	insert into rms_ricp_a
		(ricp_id,dt_txn,action_type,cp_no,entity_type,entity_no,accr_amt_b4,accr_amt_af,status_b4,status_af,
		dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status)
		 values
	    (o_result,TODAY,'CPI',i_cp_no,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,0.00,i_accr_amt,'',i_status,
	    current,current,i_created_by,i_modified_by,'A');
		   
	end if;
	
	commit work;
	
	if o_result > 0 then
	    return o_result;
	else
	    return -1;
	end if;

end procedure
GO

create or replace procedure sp_insRIPL(i_txn_type nvarchar(5), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(40),
                            i_calendar_yr nvarchar(5), i_dt_due nvarchar(100), i_ripl_ctype nvarchar(10),i_created_by nvarchar(25),i_modified_by nvarchar(25))
returning int8 as result;

define o_exist int;
define o_impair_month int;
define o_writeoff_month int;
define o_dt_impair date;
define o_dt_writeoff date;
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_result int;


define o_qty int;
define o_dt_effective date;
define o_total_fee decimal(16,2);

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Check Exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_mft
where fee_detail_id = i_ripl_ctype
and status = 'A';

if o_exist > 0 then

    -- Duplication checking
    select count(1)
    into o_exist
    from rms_ripl
    where txn_type = i_txn_type
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and calendar_yr = i_calendar_yr
    and ripl_ctype = i_ripl_ctype;

    if o_exist < 1 then

        -- Get impair month
        select config_value
        into o_impair_month
        from rms_config
        where config_cd ='RIPL_Impair_In_Month'
        and status='A';

        -- Get write off month
        select config_value
        into o_writeoff_month
        from rms_config
        where config_cd ='RIPL_WriteOff_In_Month'
        and status='A';

        -- Calculation for impair
        let o_dt_impair= ADD_MONTHS( to_date(i_dt_due,'%d/%m/%Y'), o_impair_month);
        let o_dt_impair = MDY(12, 31, YEAR(o_dt_impair));

        -- Calculation for write off
        let o_dt_writeoff=ADD_MONTHS( to_date(i_dt_due,'%d/%m/%Y'), o_writeoff_month);

        -- Get fee detail and amount
        select fee_detail_pk,unit_fee
        into o_fee_detail_pk, o_unit_fee
        from rms_mft
        where fee_detail_id = i_ripl_ctype;

        -- Insert into rms_ripl
        insert into rms_ripl(txn_type, entity_type, entity_no, calendar_yr, dt_due, 
                            dt_impair, dt_writeoff, ripl_ctype, accr_amt, rcpt_no, 
                            dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, 
                            status, fee_detail_pk) 
        values(i_txn_type, i_entity_type, i_entity_no, i_calendar_yr, to_date(i_dt_due,'%d/%m/%Y'), 
                o_dt_impair,o_dt_writeoff,i_ripl_ctype,o_unit_fee,'', 
                current, current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, 
                'CA', o_fee_detail_pk);

        -- Set rows effected in variable
        let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

        -- Insert into rms_ripl_a
        insert into rms_ripl_a(ripl_id, dt_txn, action_type, entity_type, entity_no,
                                accr_amt_b4, accr_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, dt_created, 
                                dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values( o_result, current, i_txn_type||'R', i_entity_type, i_entity_no, 
                0, o_unit_fee, '', 'CA', current, 
                current, i_created_by, i_modified_by, 'A');

        -- Insert into rms_ripl journal credit
    end if;
end if;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
CREATE or replace PROCEDURE sp_insriplagingrpt (
    i_p_dt_req DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_imp_status INT,
    i_p_exp_status INT,
    i_p_ent_ty NVARCHAR(1),
    i_p_ent_nm LVARCHAR(2000),
    i_p_dt_due_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_due_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_rcpt_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_imp_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_imp_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_wo_fr DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_p_dt_wo_to DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND,
    i_created_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),
    i_status NVARCHAR(10),
    i_p_email NVARCHAR(255),
    i_p_file_type NVARCHAR(5),
    i_p_file_size INT, 
    i_p_file_nm nvarchar(255), 							
    i_p_batch_no nvarchar(30), 
    i_p_fms_ref_no nvarchar(25)
)
RETURNING INT8 AS wf_id;

DEFINE o_wf_id INT8;
DEFINE o_current_dt DATETIME YEAR TO SECOND;
DEFINE o_insresult INT8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Set current date time
LET o_current_dt = CURRENT;

-- Insert data into rms_rpt_ripl_age table
INSERT INTO rms_rpt_ripl_age
    (p_dt_req, p_imp_status, p_exp_status, p_ent_ty, p_ent_nm, p_dt_due_fr, p_dt_due_to,
     p_dt_rcpt_fr, p_dt_rcpt_to, p_dt_imp_fr, p_dt_imp_to, p_dt_wo_fr, p_dt_wo_to,
     dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status, p_email, p_file_type, p_file_size, p_file_nm, p_batch_no, p_fms_ref_no)
VALUES
    (i_p_dt_req, i_p_imp_status, i_p_exp_status, i_p_ent_ty, i_p_ent_nm, i_p_dt_due_fr, i_p_dt_due_to,
     i_p_dt_rcpt_fr, i_p_dt_rcpt_to, i_p_dt_imp_fr, i_p_dt_imp_to, i_p_dt_wo_fr, i_p_dt_wo_to,
     o_current_dt, o_current_dt, i_created_by, i_modified_by, i_status, i_p_email, i_p_file_type, i_p_file_size, i_p_file_nm, i_p_batch_no, i_p_fms_ref_no);

-- Get latest Serial8 ID number from last inserted records
LET o_wf_id = DBINFO('Serial8');

commit work;

RETURN o_wf_id;

END PROCEDURE;

create or replace procedure sp_insuserrole(userId nvarchar(255), roleId integer)
	returning int as row_count;
 
	Define row_count int;
 
	INSERT INTO rms_user_role(ssm4uuserrefno, role_id)
		VALUES
		(userId, roleId);

	SELECT COUNT(1)
	INTO row_count
	FROM rms_user_role
	WHERE ssm4uuserrefno = userId and role_id = roleId and status = 'A';

	RETURN row_count;

END PROCEDURE;

create or replace procedure sp_mftwf_effective()
returning int as result;

define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 180;

let o_result = 0;

/* Request Add - Start*/
/* Insert into rms_mft from rms_mft_wf */
INSERT INTO rms_mft
	( fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_e, fee_detail_nm_b, unit_fee, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee, 
	    tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd,
	     dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status)
SELECT fee_detail_id, fee_grp_id, fee_detail_nm_e, fee_detail_nm_b, fee_amt, promo_startdt, promo_enddt, promo_fee,
	    tax_cd_id, allow_otc, ll_parent_id, ll_start_day, ll_start_mth, ll_end_day, ll_end_mth, ledger_cd, ss_cd,
        current, current, created_by, modified_by, status
FROM rms_mft_wf
WHERE rms_mft_wf.effective_date >= current
AND rms_mft_wf.status = 'APV'
AND rms_mft_wf.action = 'requestadd';

/* Update rms_mft_wf */
UPDATE rms_mft_wf
SET status = 'EFF'
WHERE rms_mft_wf.effective_date >= current
AND rms_mft_wf.action = 'requestadd';
/* Request Add - End*/

/*  Request Update - Start */
/* Update rms_mft */
UPDATE rms_mft
SET 	fee_grp_id = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.fee_grp_id IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.fee_grp_id
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.fee_grp_id
	    			END,
	    fee_detail_nm_e = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.fee_detail_nm_e IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.fee_detail_nm_e
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.fee_detail_nm_e
	    			END,
	    fee_detail_nm_b = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.fee_detail_nm_b IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.fee_detail_nm_b
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.fee_detail_nm_b
	    			END,
	    unit_fee = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.fee_amt IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.unit_fee
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.fee_amt
	    			END,
	    promo_startdt = CASE 
	      					WHEN rms_mft_wf.promo_startdt IS NULL 
	       						THEN rms_mft.promo_startdt
	       					ELSE rms_mft_wf.promo_startdt
	       				END,
	    promo_enddt = CASE
	      				WHEN rms_mft_wf.promo_enddt IS NULL
	       						THEN rms_mft.promo_enddt
	       					ELSE rms_mft_wf.promo_enddt
	       				END,
	    promo_fee = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.promo_startdt IS NULL 
	    					THEN rms_mft.promo_fee
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.promo_fee
	    			END,
	    tax_cd_id = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.tax_cd_id IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.tax_cd_id
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.tax_cd_id
	    			END,
	    allow_otc = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.allow_otc IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.allow_otc
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.allow_otc
	    			END,
	    ll_parent_id = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ll_parent_id IS NULL 
	    					THEN rms_mft.ll_parent_id
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ll_parent_id
	    			END,
	    ll_start_day = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ll_start_day IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.ll_start_day
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ll_start_day
	    			END,
	    ll_start_mth = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ll_start_mth IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.ll_start_mth
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ll_start_mth
	    			END,
	    ll_end_day = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ll_start_mth IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.ll_start_mth
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ll_start_mth
	    			END,
	    ll_end_mth = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ll_end_mth IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.ll_end_mth
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ll_end_mth
	    			END,
	    ledger_cd = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ledger_cd IS NULL 
	    					THEN rms_mft.ledger_cd
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ledger_cd
	    			END,
	    ss_cd = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.ss_cd IS NULL 
	    					THEN rms_mft.ss_cd
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.ss_cd
	    			END,
	    dt_modified = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.dt_modified IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.dt_modified
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.dt_modified
	    			END,
        created_by = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.created_by IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.created_by
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.created_by
	    			END,
	    modified_by = CASE
	    				WHEN rms_mft_wf.modified_by IS NULL
	    					THEN rms_mft.modified_by
	    				ELSE rms_mft_wf.modified_by
	    			END
FROM rms_mft_wf
WHERE rms_mft_wf.effective_date >= current
AND rms_mft_wf.status = 'APV'
AND rms_mft_wf.action = 'requestupd'
AND rms_mft.fee_detail_id = rms_mft_wf.fee_detail_id;

/* Update rms_mft_wf */
UPDATE rms_mft_wf
SET status = 'EFF'
WHERE rms_mft_wf.effective_date >= current
AND rms_mft_wf.action = 'requestupd';
/*  Request Update - End */

/* Request Delete - Start */
/* Update rms_mft */
UPDATE rms_mft
SET status = rms_mft_wf.status,
    dt_modified = rms_mft_wf.dt_modified,
    modified_by = rms_mft_wf.modified_by
FROM rms_mft_wf 
WHERE rms_mft_wf.status = 'D'
AND rms_mft_wf.action = 'requestdel';

/* Request Delete - End */
let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

commit work;

return o_result;

END PROCEDURE
GO
create or replace procedure sp_upddi()
returning int as result;

define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
--set lock mode to wait 10;

select count(1)
into o_result
from rms_di
where status not in ('C','T')
and next_calc_dt <= today;

if o_result > 0 then

    -- create a temporary table
    create temp table tempdi (
        di_id int8,
        fee_detail_pk int,
        fee_detail_id nvarchar(10),
        entity_type nvarchar(1),
        entity_no nvarchar(20),
        unit_fee decimal(16,2),
        bal_di_amt decimal(16,2),
        next_calc_dt date,
        status nvarchar(10)
    );

    -- complete terminated exclude
    insert into tempdi (di_id, unit_fee, bal_di_amt, next_calc_dt, status)
    select di_id, unit_fee, bal_di_amt, next_calc_dt, status
    from rms_di
    where status not in ('C','T')
    and next_calc_dt <= today;

    -- insert statement rms_di audit
    insert into rms_di_a(di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, dt_txn, action_type, 
                            entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt_b4, bal_di_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, 
                                dt_created, dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
    select di_id, fee_detail_pk, fee_detail_id, current, upper('pca'),
            entity_type, entity_no, bal_di_amt, bal_di_amt - unit_fee, status, 
            case 
                when bal_di_amt - unit_fee > 0 
                    then upper('a')
                else upper('c')
            end,
                current, current, 'system', 'system', upper('a')
			 
    from rms_di 
    where status not in ('C','T')
    and next_calc_dt <= today;

    -- update statement rms_di
    update rms_di
    set t1.bal_di_amt = t2.bal_di_amt - t2.unit_fee,
        t1.next_calc_dt = extend(extend(t2.next_calc_dt, year to day) + 1 units year, year to day),
        t1.dt_modified = current,
        t1.status = case 
                    when t2.bal_di_amt - t2.unit_fee > 0 
                        then upper('a')
                    else upper('c')
                 end
    from rms_di t1
    inner join tempdi t2 on t1.di_id = t2.di_id;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    -- insert statement rms_di journal debit

    -- insert statement rms_di journal credit

    drop table tempdi;

else

    let o_result = 0;

end if;

commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure
GO

create or replace procedure sp_updfms(
    i_fms_id INT, 
    i_fms_cd NVARCHAR(50), 
    i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25),  
    i_is_active INT
)
RETURNING INT AS row_count;

DEFINE o_row_count INT;
DEFINE is_other_active INT;

IF i_is_active = 0 THEN
    -- Check if there is an FMS currently active
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO is_other_active
    FROM rms_fms
    WHERE is_active = 1 and fms_id <> i_fms_id;

    -- If the FMS is currently active, deactivate it
    IF is_other_active > 0 THEN
        UPDATE rms_fms
        SET is_active = 0
        WHERE fms_id = i_fms_id;
    END IF;
END IF;


-- Check if i_is_active is 1
IF i_is_active = 1 THEN
    -- Check if other FMS records are active
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    INTO is_other_active
    FROM rms_fms
    WHERE is_active = 1 AND fms_id <> i_fms_id;

    -- If other FMS records are active, set them to not active
    IF is_other_active > 0 THEN
        UPDATE rms_fms
        SET is_active = 0
        WHERE is_active = 1 AND fms_id <> i_fms_id;
    END IF;

     UPDATE rms_fms
        SET is_active = 1
        WHERE is_active = 0 AND fms_id = i_fms_id;
END IF;

-- Update the specified FMS record
UPDATE rms_fms
SET
    fms_cd = CASE WHEN i_fms_cd IS NULL THEN fms_cd ELSE i_fms_cd END,
    dt_modified = CURRENT,
    modified_by = i_modified_by
WHERE fms_id = i_fms_id;

-- Get the row count affected by the update
LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updfms_activation(i_fms_id NVARCHAR(50), i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25))
RETURNING INT AS row_count;

DEFINE o_row_count INT;


/*Update Active FMS code in MFT*/
UPDATE rms_mft
SET ledger_cd = t2.fms_ledger_cd,
        dt_modified = current,
        modified_by = i_modified_by,
        status = 'A'
FROM rms_mft t1
INNER JOIN rms_fms_ledger t2 ON t1.fee_detail_id = t2.fee_detail_id 
WHERE t2.fms_id = i_fms_id and t2.found = 'F' and t2.status = 'A';

LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE
GO

create or replace procedure sp_updmftwf(i_wf_id INT8, i_fee_detail_pk INT, i_fee_detail_id NVARCHAR(10), i_fee_grp_id INT, i_fee_detail_nm_e NVARCHAR(100), i_fee_detail_nm_b NVARCHAR(100), i_fee_amt DECIMAL,
                              i_promo_startdt DATE, i_promo_enddt DATE, i_promo_fee DECIMAL, i_tax_cd_id INT, i_allow_otc INT, 
                              i_ll_parent_id NVARCHAR(10), i_ll_start_day INT, i_ll_end_day INT, i_ll_start_mth INT, i_ll_end_mth INT, 
                              i_ledger_cd NVARCHAR(50), i_ss_cd NVARCHAR(100), i_effective_date DATE, i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), 
                              i_status NVARCHAR(10), i_assign_to NVARCHAR(25), i_remark LVARCHAR(500), i_action NVARCHAR(50),
                              i_r_fee_det_nm NVARCHAR(100), i_r_fee_amt DECIMAL, i_r_ss_cd NVARCHAR(100), i_r_promo_startdt DATE,
                              i_r_promo_enddt DATE, i_r_ll_required INT, i_r_add_notes LVARCHAR(500), i_mft_status NVARCHAR(10), i_r_promo_fee DECIMAL)
RETURNING INT as row_count;

DEFINE o_row_count INT;
DEFINE o_status_nm NVARCHAR(50);
define o_insresult int8;

BEGIN WORK;

SELECT FIRST 1 nm_en
INTO o_status_nm
FROM rms_param
WHERE param_cd = i_status 
AND param_grp_nm = 'Status-MFT';

UPDATE rms_mft_wf
SET
	fee_detail_pk = i_fee_detail_pk,
	fee_detail_id = i_fee_detail_id,
	fee_grp_id = i_fee_grp_id,
	fee_detail_nm_e = i_fee_detail_nm_e,
	fee_detail_nm_b = i_fee_detail_nm_b,
	fee_amt = i_fee_amt,
	promo_startdt = i_promo_startdt,
	promo_enddt = i_promo_enddt,
	promo_fee = i_promo_fee,
	tax_cd_id = i_tax_cd_id,
	allow_otc = i_allow_otc,
	ll_parent_id = i_ll_parent_id,
	ll_start_day = i_ll_start_day,
	ll_start_mth = i_ll_start_mth,
	ll_end_day = i_ll_end_day,
	ll_end_mth = i_ll_end_mth,
	ledger_cd = i_ledger_cd,
	ss_cd = i_ss_cd,
	effective_date = i_effective_date,
	dt_modified = current,
	modified_by = i_modified_by,
	status = i_status,
	assign_to = i_assign_to,
	action  = i_action,
	r_fee_det_nm = i_r_fee_det_nm,
	r_fee_amt = i_r_fee_amt,
	r_ss_cd = i_r_ss_cd,
	r_promo_startdt = i_r_promo_startdt,
	r_promo_enddt = i_r_promo_enddt,
	r_ll_required = i_r_ll_required,
	r_add_notes = i_r_add_notes,
	mft_status = i_mft_status,
	r_promo_fee = i_r_promo_fee
	
WHERE wf_id = i_wf_id;
	
LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

/*CALL sp_insmftwfhis(i_wf_id,o_status_nm, current, i_modified_by,i_assign_to,i_remark,i_modified_by,i_modified_by,i_status);*/
execute procedure sp_insmftwfhis(i_wf_id,o_status_nm, current, i_modified_by,i_assign_to,i_remark,i_modified_by,i_modified_by,i_status) into o_insresult;

COMMIT WORK;

RETURN o_row_count;

END PROCEDURE

create or replace procedure sp_updmtt(
	i_orn_no nvarchar(20),
	i_cust_nm nvarchar(255),
	i_cust_addr_1 nvarchar(150),
	i_cust_addr_2 nvarchar(150),
	i_cust_addr_3 nvarchar(150),
	i_cust_postcode nvarchar(15),
	i_cust_city nvarchar(50),
	i_cust_state nvarchar(50)
	)
RETURNING INT as mtt_id;

DEFINE o_mtt_id int;

	update informix.rms_mtt 
	set cust_nm = i_cust_nm,
		cust_addr_1= i_cust_addr_1,
		cust_addr_2= i_cust_addr_2,
		cust_addr_3= i_cust_addr_3,
		cust_postcode= i_cust_postcode,
		cust_city= i_cust_city,
		cust_state=i_cust_state
	where orn_no = i_orn_no;
	
	select first 1 mtt_id
	into o_mtt_id
	from informix.rms_mtt 
	where orn_no = i_orn_no;
	
	
	return o_mtt_id;

END PROCEDURE;

create or replace procedure sp_updmttrcpt( i_mtt_rcpt_id int8,i_ver_id nvarchar(100),i_ssdocref_id nvarchar(100))
returning int as result;

define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
--set lock mode to wait 10;

select count(1)
into o_result
from rms_mtt_rcpt
where mtt_rcpt_id = i_mtt_rcpt_id;

if o_result > 0 then

    -- update rcpt
    update rms_mtt_rcpt
    set ver_id=i_ver_id,
        ssdocref_id=i_ssdocref_id,
        is_uploaded = is_uploaded+1,
        dt_modified = current
    where mtt_rcpt_id = i_mtt_rcpt_id;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

else

    let o_result = 0;

end if;

commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updpgmtttxn()
returning int8 as result;
 
define o_result int;
define o_exist int;
define o_compare_range int;
define o_dt_settlement date;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;
 
-- Set a default value
LET o_result = '0';
 
begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- create a temporary table
create temp table temppgmtt (
    rc_pgmtt_id int8,
    rc_pg_id int8,
    sub_criteria nvarchar(10)
);
 
-- check exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pgmtt
where sub_criteria = 'NF';

if o_exist > 0 then

    -- select statement
    insert into temppgmtt (rc_pgmtt_id,rc_pg_id,sub_criteria)
    SELECT 
        rms_rc_pgmtt.rc_pgmtt_id, 
        rms_rc_pgmtt.rc_pg_id,
        CASE 
            WHEN rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_id IS NULL THEN 'NFP'
            WHEN rms_rc_pg.task_status = 'CL' THEN 'CIP'
            ELSE 'NCP'
        END as Status
    FROM 
        rms_rc_pgmtt
    LEFT JOIN 
        rms_mtt_pg ON rms_rc_pgmtt.mtt_pg_id = rms_mtt_pg.mtt_pg_id
    LEFT JOIN 
        rms_rc_pgtxn ON rms_mtt_pg.pg_txn_id = rms_rc_pgtxn.txn_id
    LEFT JOIN 
        rms_rc_pg ON rms_rc_pgtxn.rc_pg_id = rms_rc_pg.rc_pg_id
    WHERE 
        rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = 'NF';

    -- update
    UPDATE 
        rms_rc_pgmtt
    SET 
        rms_rc_pgmtt.sub_criteria = temppgmtt.sub_criteria
    FROM 
        temppgmtt
    WHERE 
        rms_rc_pgmtt.rc_pgmtt_id = temppgmtt.rc_pgmtt_id;
 
    -- get update count
    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    -- update rms_rc_pg' recon status
    update rms_rc_pg
    set recon_status = 'PSSCR'
    where rc_pg_id in (select distinct rc_pg_id from temppgmtt);

drop table temppgmtt;
 
end if;
 
commit work;
 
if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;
 
end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updPGReconDetail(i_task_id nvarchar(30), i_remarks nvarchar(255), i_task_status nvarchar(10),i_modified_by nvarchar(25))
returning int8 as result;

define o_exist int;
define o_result int;
define o_task_status nvarchar(10);
define o_rc_pg_id int;
define o_dt_settlement date;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Check Task No Exist
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_rc_pg
where task_no = i_task_id;

if o_exist > 0 then

    -- Check Task No Exist
    select rc_pg_id,dt_settlement
    into o_rc_pg_id,o_dt_settlement
    from rms_rc_pg
    where task_no = i_task_id;

    -- get task_status code
    select param_cd
    into o_task_status
    from rms_param
    where param_grp_nm='Status-Task' and nm_en = i_task_status;

    if o_task_status= 'CL' then

        -- update rms_rc_pgtxn
        update rms_rc_pgtxn
        set status = 'D'
        where rc_pg_id=o_rc_pg_id;

        -- update rms_rc_pgmtt

        update rms_rc_pgmtt
        set status ='D'
        from rms_rc_pgmtt t1
        inner join rms_mtt_pg t2 on t1.mtt_pg_id=t2.mtt_pg_id
        where date(t2.pg_resp_time)=o_dt_settlement;

    end if;

    -- update rms_rc_pg
    update rms_rc_pg
    set remarks = i_remarks,
        task_status=o_task_status,
        dt_modified = current,
        modified_by = i_modified_by,
        recon_status = (CASE 
                            WHEN o_task_status= 'CS' THEN 'SSSCR' 
                            WHEN o_task_status= 'CL' THEN 'FSSCR'
                            ELSE recon_status END)
    where task_no=i_task_id;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

end if;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updrcbank(i_rc_bank_id int8)
returning int8 as result;

define o_result int8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

if (i_rc_bank_id is null or i_rc_bank_id < 1) then 
    raise exception -746, 0, "i_rc_bank_id is null integer";
end if

begin work;

let o_result = 0;

update rms_rc_bank
set recon_status = 'PBSR',
    dt_modified = current
where rc_bank_id = i_rc_bank_id;

commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updrcbankstatus(i_task_no nvarchar(25), i_task_status nvarchar(25), i_remarks nvarchar(255))
returning int8 as result;

define o_status nvarchar(25);
define o_result int8;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;

    select param_cd
    into o_status
    from rms_param
    where (nm_en = i_task_status or nm_bm = i_task_status)
    and param_grp_nm = 'Status-Task';

    update rms_rc_bank
    set task_status = o_status,
        remarks = i_remarks,
        recon_status = case 
                            when o_status = 'O' then 'PBSR'
                            when o_status = 'CS' then 'SBSR'
                            when o_status = 'CL' then 'FBSR'
                        end,
        dt_modified = current
    where task_no = i_task_no;

    let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd1');

commit work;

return o_result;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updrcbanktxn()
returning int as result;

define o_txn_ref nvarchar(50);
define o_rc_bank_id int8;
define o_total_credit decimal(15, 2);
define o_stmt_no nvarchar(25);
define o_total_paid decimal(15, 2);
define o_total_count int;
define o_status int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;

let o_status = 1;

select count(txn_ref)
into o_total_count
from rms_rc_banktxn
where status = 'PBSR';

while o_total_count > 0

    -- Select txn_ref
    select first 1 txn_ref
    into o_txn_ref
    from rms_rc_banktxn
    where status = 'PBSR';

    -- Select from rms_rc_banktxn table
    select rc_bank_id, sum(credit)
    into o_rc_bank_id, o_total_credit
    from rms_rc_banktxn
    where status = 'PBSR'
    and txn_ref like substring(o_txn_ref from 0 for 15) || '%'
    group by rc_bank_id;

    -- Select from pg table
    select total_paid
    into o_total_paid
    from rms_rc_pg
    where o_txn_ref like '%' || stmt_no || '%';

    if(o_total_paid <> o_total_credit) then
            -- Update status in bank txn 
            update rms_rc_banktxn
            set status = 'FBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where txn_ref like substring(o_txn_ref from 0 for 15) || '%';

            -- Update status in rc pg
            update rms_rc_pg
            set recon_status = 'FBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where o_txn_ref like '%' || stmt_no || '%'; 

            -- Update status in rc bank
            update rms_rc_bank
            set recon_status = 'FBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where rc_bank_id = o_rc_bank_id;

            -- Set status = failed
            let o_status = 0;
        else
            -- Update status in bank txn 
            update rms_rc_banktxn
            set status = 'SBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where txn_ref like substring(o_txn_ref from 0 for 15) || '%';

            -- Update status in rc pg
            update rms_rc_pg
            set recon_status = 'SBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where o_txn_ref like '%' || stmt_no || '%'; 

            -- Update status in rc pg
            update rms_rc_bank
            set recon_status = 'SBSR',
                dt_modified = current
            where rc_bank_id = o_rc_bank_id;

            -- Set status = success
            let o_status = 1;
        end if;

let o_total_count = o_total_count - 1;

end while;

commit work;

return o_status;

end procedure;
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updricp(i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(20), i_cp_no nvarchar(20),
i_status nvarchar(10), i_audit_action nvarchar(10), i_old_status nvarchar(10))

	returning int8 as result;

	define o_exist int;
	define o_result int;
	define o_accr_amt decimal;

	on exception
		rollback work;
	end exception;
	
	begin work;
	set lock mode to wait 30;

	-- Exist checking
	select ricp_id, accr_amt
	into o_exist, o_accr_amt
	from rms_ricp
	where entity_type = i_entity_type
	and entity_no = i_entity_no
	and cp_no = i_cp_no
	and status = i_old_status;

	let o_result = 0;

	if o_exist > 0 then
	
		update rms_ricp
		set status=i_status,
		dt_modified = current
	    where ricp_id = o_exist;
	   
	   	insert into rms_ricp_a
		(ricp_id,dt_txn,action_type,cp_no,entity_type,entity_no,accr_amt_b4,accr_amt_af,status_b4,status_af,
		dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status)
		 values
	    (o_exist,TODAY,i_audit_action,i_cp_no,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,o_accr_amt,0.00,i_old_status,i_status,
	    current,current,'system','system','A');
	   
	   if i_audit_action == 'CPV' then 
	   			insert into rms_ricp_cv_log
				(ricp_id,entity_type,entity_no,cp_no,dt_void,dt_cancel,
				dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status)
				 values
			    (o_exist,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,i_cp_no,TODAY,NULL,
			    current,current,'system','system','A');
			   	update rms_ricp set dt_void=TODAY
			    where ricp_id = o_exist;
	   end if;
		   
	  if i_audit_action == 'CPC' then
	   			insert into rms_ricp_cv_log
				(ricp_id,entity_type,entity_no,cp_no,dt_void,dt_cancel,
				dt_created,dt_modified,created_by,modified_by,status)
				 values
			    (o_exist,i_entity_type,i_entity_no,i_cp_no,NULL,TODAY,
			    current,current,'system','system','A');	  	
			   	update rms_ricp set dt_cancel=TODAY
			    where ricp_id = o_exist;
	  end if;
	 
	  let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');
	 
	end if;
	
	commit work;
	
	if o_result > 0 then
	    return o_result;
	else
	    return -1;
	end if;

end procedure
GO

create or replace procedure sp_updRIPL(i_txn_type nvarchar(5), i_entity_type nvarchar(1), i_entity_no nvarchar(40),
                            i_calendar_yr nvarchar(5), i_rcpt_no nvarchar(100),i_modified_by nvarchar(25))
returning int8 as result;

define o_exist int;
define o_exist2 int;
define o_status_check int;
define o_previous_status nvarchar(10);
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Existing checking
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_ripl
where txn_type = i_txn_type
and entity_type = i_entity_type
and entity_no = i_entity_no
and calendar_yr = i_calendar_yr;

-- check receipt
-- remove this checking due to most of the payment is perform outside of rms







if o_exist > 0 then

    -- check status
    select count(1)
    into o_status_check
    from rms_ripl
    where status in ('CA','IP') -- want collectable and impair only
    and txn_type = i_txn_type
    and entity_type = i_entity_type
    and entity_no = i_entity_no
    and calendar_yr = i_calendar_yr;

    if o_status_check > 0 then

        -- get status and create by
        select ripl_id,status,created_by,accr_amt
        into o_result,o_previous_status,o_created_by,o_unit_fee
        from rms_ripl
        where status in ('CA','IP') -- want collectable and impair only
        and txn_type = i_txn_type
        and entity_type = i_entity_type
        and entity_no = i_entity_no
        and calendar_yr = i_calendar_yr;

        -- Update to rms_ripl
        update rms_ripl
        set rcpt_no = i_rcpt_no,
            status = 'CE', -- update to collected
            modified_by = i_modified_by,
            dt_modified = current
        where txn_type = i_txn_type
        and entity_type = i_entity_type
        and entity_no = i_entity_no
        and calendar_yr = i_calendar_yr;

        -- Set rows effected in variable
       --let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

        -- Insert into rms_ripl_a
        insert into rms_ripl_a(ripl_id, dt_txn, action_type, entity_type, entity_no,
                                accr_amt_b4, accr_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, dt_created, 
                                dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
        values( o_result, current, i_txn_type||'RP', i_entity_type, i_entity_no, 
                o_unit_fee, o_unit_fee, o_previous_status, 'CE', current, 
                current, i_modified_by, i_modified_by, 'A');

        -- Insert into rms_ripl journal credit
        end if;

end if;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO

create or replace procedure sp_updRIPLImpairStatus()
returning int8 as result;

define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- create a temporary table
create temp table tempripl (
    ripl_id int8,
    txn_type nvarchar(5),
    entity_type nvarchar(1),
    entity_no nvarchar(20),
    unit_fee decimal(16,2),
    status nvarchar(10)
);

-- select related fields
insert into tempripl (ripl_id, txn_type, entity_type, entity_no, unit_fee, status)
select ripl_id, txn_type, entity_type, entity_no, accr_amt, status
from rms_ripl
where status = 'CA'
and dt_impair <= current;

-- Update to rms_ripl status to IP
update rms_ripl
set status = 'IP', -- update to impair
    modified_by = 'system',
    dt_modified = current
where ripl_id IN ( select ripl_id from tempripl);

let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

-- Insert into rms_ripl_a
insert into rms_ripl_a(ripl_id, dt_txn, action_type, entity_type, entity_no,
                        accr_amt_b4, accr_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, dt_created, 
                        dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
select ripl_id, current, txn_type||'I',entity_type,entity_no,
    unit_fee,unit_fee,status,'IP',current,
    current,'system','system','A'
from tempripl;

drop table tempripl;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updRIPLStatus(i_ripl_id nvarchar(5), i_status nvarchar(10),i_modified_by nvarchar(25))
returning int8 as result;

define o_exist int;
define o_status_check int;
define o_previous_status nvarchar(10);
define o_created_by nvarchar(25);
define o_fee_detail_pk int;
define o_unit_fee decimal(16,2);
define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- Existing checking
select count(1)
into o_exist
from rms_ripl
where ripl_id=i_ripl_id;

if o_exist > 0 then

    -- Update to rms_ripl
    update rms_ripl
    set status = 'CE', -- update to collected
        modified_by = i_modified_by,
        dt_modified = current
    where ripl_id=i_ripl_id;

    -- Get fee detail and amount
    select fee_detail_pk,unit_fee
    into o_fee_detail_pk, o_unit_fee
    from rms_mft
    where fee_detail_id = i_ripl_ctype;

    -- Set rows effected in variable
    let o_result = dbinfo('serial8');

    -- Insert into rms_ripl_a
    insert into rms_ripl_a(ripl_id, dt_txn, action_type, entity_type, entity_no,
                            accr_amt_b4, accr_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, dt_created, 
                            dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
    values( o_result, current, 'RP', '', '', 
            1, 1, 'CA', 'IP', current, 
            current, i_modified_by, i_modified_by, 'A');

end if;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure
GO
create or replace procedure sp_updRIPLWriteOffStatus()
returning int8 as result;

define o_result int;

on exception
	rollback work;
end exception;

begin work;
set lock mode to wait 30;

-- create a temporary table
create temp table tempripl (
    ripl_id int8,
    txn_type nvarchar(5),
    entity_type nvarchar(1),
    entity_no nvarchar(20),
    unit_fee decimal(16,2),
    status nvarchar(10)
);

select ripl_id, txn_type, entity_type, entity_no, accr_amt, status
from rms_ripl
where status = 'IP'
and dt_writeoff <= current;

-- Update to rms_ripl status to IP
update rms_ripl
set status = 'WO', -- update to impair
    modified_by = 'system',
    dt_modified = current
where ripl_id IN ( select ripl_id from tempripl);

let o_result = dbinfo('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

                        accr_amt_b4, accr_amt_af, status_b4, status_af, dt_created, 
                        dt_modified, created_by, modified_by, status) 
select ripl_id, current, txn_type||'I',entity_type,entity_no,
    unit_fee, 0,status,'WO',current,
    current,'system','system','A'
from tempripl;

drop table tempripl;

commit work;

if o_result > 0 then
    return o_result;
else
    return -1;
end if;

end procedure

create or replace procedure sp_updrolestatus(i_role_nm_en NVARCHAR(255), i_modified_by nvarchar(25))
    RETURNING INT as row_count;

    DEFINE o_row_count INT;

    UPDATE rms_role 
    SET status = CASE
                    WHEN status = 'A' THEN 'D'
                    WHEN status = 'D' THEN 'A'
                    ELSE status  -- Add this line to handle any other cases
                 END,
                 dt_modified = current,
                 modified_by = i_modified_by

    WHERE role_nm_en = i_role_nm_en;

    LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

    RETURN o_row_count;
    
END PROCEDURE;

create or replace procedure sp_updtaxcode(i_tax_cd NVARCHAR(10),i_tax_cd_nm_en NVARCHAR(50),i_tax_cd_nm_bm NVARCHAR(50),i_tax_pct DECIMAL
									,i_modified_by NVARCHAR(25), i_status NVARCHAR(10))
	RETURNING INT as row_count;

	DEFINE o_row_count INT;

	UPDATE rms_tax_code 
	SET tax_cd_nm_en = i_tax_cd_nm_en,
	tax_cd_nm_bm = i_tax_cd_nm_bm,
	tax_pct = i_tax_pct,
	modified_by = i_modified_by,
	dt_modified = current 
	WHERE tax_cd = i_tax_cd AND Status = i_status;

	LET o_row_count = DBINFO('sqlca.sqlerrd2');

	RETURN o_row_count;
	
END PROCEDURE
GO
